 = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = 
 
 using System.Text;
using TQGA.Application.Paths;

namespace TQGA.Application.Services;

public sealed class FullReportService
{
    private static readonly string[] IncludeExtensions = { ".txt", ".csv" };

    private const string Report32TxtPrefix = "REPORT_32_TRADE_BLOTTER_ENTRY_EXIT_REASON_JOURNAL_";
    private const string Report33TxtPrefix = "REPORT_33_TRADE_INTELLIGENCE_MASTER_";
    private const string Report34TxtPrefix = "REPORT_34_TRADE_BLOTTER_";
    private const string Report35TxtPrefix = "REPORT_35_TRADE_INTELLIGENCE_";

    public string BuildCombinedReport()
    {
        var sb = new StringBuilder();

        var files = Directory
            .EnumerateFiles(DataPaths.Reports, "*.*", SearchOption.TopDirectoryOnly)
            .Where(ShouldIncludeInCombinedReport)
            .OrderBy(f => Path.GetFileName(f), StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase)
            .ToList();

        sb.AppendLine("TQGA FULL REPORT");
        sb.AppendLine("===============");
        sb.AppendLine($"Folder: {DataPaths.Reports}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Files:  {files.Count}");
        sb.AppendLine($"UTC:    {DateTime.UtcNow:yyyy-MM-dd HH:mm:ss}");
        sb.AppendLine();
        sb.AppendLine("SIZE CONTROL POLICY");
        sb.AppendLine("-------------------");
        sb.AppendLine("REPORT 32 TXT omitted from combined report for GitHub size control.");
        sb.AppendLine("REPORT 33 TXT omitted from combined report for GitHub size control.");
        sb.AppendLine("REPORT 34 TRADE_BLOTTER included as compact replacement.");
        sb.AppendLine("REPORT 35 TRADE_INTELLIGENCE included as compact replacement.");
        sb.AppendLine();

        AppendCompactReplacementNotice(sb);
        sb.AppendLine();

        foreach (var file in files)
        {
            string name = Path.GetFileName(file);

            sb.AppendLine($"FILE: {name}");
            sb.AppendLine(new string('-', 70));
            sb.AppendLine(File.ReadAllText(file));
            sb.AppendLine();
            sb.AppendLine(new string('=', 70));
            sb.AppendLine();
        }

        return sb.ToString();
    }

    public string BuildChatGptSizedReport(int maxChars = 120_000)
    {
        string full = BuildCombinedReport();
        return full.Length <= maxChars ? full : full[..maxChars];
    }

    public string SaveCombinedToFile()
    {
        string text = BuildCombinedReport();
        string path = Path.Combine(
            DataPaths.Reports,
            $"FULL_REPORT_{DateTime.Now:yyyyMMdd_HHmmss}.txt");

        File.WriteAllText(path, text);
        return path;
    }

    private static bool ShouldIncludeInCombinedReport(string filePath)
    {
        string extension = Path.GetExtension(filePath);
        if (!IncludeExtensions.Contains(extension, StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase))
            return false;

        string fileName = Path.GetFileName(filePath);

        if (extension.Equals(".txt", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase))
        {
            if (fileName.StartsWith(Report32TxtPrefix, StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase))
                return false;

            if (fileName.StartsWith(Report33TxtPrefix, StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase))
                return false;
        }

        return true;
    }

    private static void AppendCompactReplacementNotice(StringBuilder sb)
    {
        string? report32Txt = Directory
            .EnumerateFiles(DataPaths.Reports, $"{Report32TxtPrefix}*.txt", SearchOption.TopDirectoryOnly)
            .OrderByDescending(File.GetLastWriteTimeUtc)
            .FirstOrDefault();

        string? report33Txt = Directory
            .EnumerateFiles(DataPaths.Reports, $"{Report33TxtPrefix}*.txt", SearchOption.TopDirectoryOnly)
            .OrderByDescending(File.GetLastWriteTimeUtc)
            .FirstOrDefault();

        string? report34Txt = Directory
            .EnumerateFiles(DataPaths.Reports, $"{Report34TxtPrefix}*.txt", SearchOption.TopDirectoryOnly)
            .OrderByDescending(File.GetLastWriteTimeUtc)
            .FirstOrDefault();

        string? report35Txt = Directory
            .EnumerateFiles(DataPaths.Reports, $"{Report35TxtPrefix}*.txt", SearchOption.TopDirectoryOnly)
            .OrderByDescending(File.GetLastWriteTimeUtc)
            .FirstOrDefault();

        if (report32Txt != null)
            sb.AppendLine($"OMITTED: {Path.GetFileName(report32Txt)} -- replaced by compact REPORT 34 in REPORT_ALL");

        if (report33Txt != null)
            sb.AppendLine($"OMITTED: {Path.GetFileName(report33Txt)} -- replaced by compact REPORT 35 in REPORT_ALL");

        if (report34Txt != null)
            sb.AppendLine($"INCLUDED: {Path.GetFileName(report34Txt)}");

        if (report35Txt != null)
            sb.AppendLine($"INCLUDED: {Path.GetFileName(report35Txt)}");
    }
}

 = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = 
 
 using System;
using System.ComponentModel;
using System.Diagnostics;
using System.IO;
using System.Linq;
using System.Text;
using TQGA.Application.Paths;

namespace TQGA.Application.Services;

public sealed class GitHubCodeAuditPublishService
{
    private const string TargetPublishedFileName = "fourtyfied561234598.html";
    private const string PublicUrl = "https://arifpisonium.github.io/fourtyfied561234598.html";
    private const string RemoteName = "origin";
    private const string BranchName = "main";

    public GitHubCodeAuditPublishResult PublishLatestAuditHtml(string repoRootPath)
    {
        ArgumentException.ThrowIfNullOrWhiteSpace(repoRootPath);

        if (!Directory.Exists(repoRootPath))
            throw new DirectoryNotFoundException($"GitHub Pages repo folder not found: {repoRootPath}");

        EnsureGitRepository(repoRootPath);

        Directory.CreateDirectory(DataPaths.Reports);

        string latestAuditHtml = Directory
            .EnumerateFiles(DataPaths.Reports, "TQGA_AUDIT_MASTER__*.html", SearchOption.TopDirectoryOnly)
            .OrderByDescending(File.GetLastWriteTimeUtc)
            .FirstOrDefault()
            ?? throw new FileNotFoundException(
                "No generated audit HTML file was found in Reports. Please click CODES FILE first.");

        string sourceHtmlText = File.ReadAllText(latestAuditHtml, Encoding.UTF8);
        if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(sourceHtmlText))
            throw new InvalidOperationException($"Audit HTML file is empty: {latestAuditHtml}");

        // PATCH:
        // This repo is a publish mirror and may be edited manually on GitHub web.
        // We do NOT want rebase/merge conflict workflows here.
        // Always recover to a clean state first, then hard-sync to origin/main.

        // 1) Abort any unfinished rebase if present.
        RunGit(repoRootPath, "rebase --abort", allowFailure: true);

        // 2) Fetch latest remote state.
        RunGit(repoRootPath, $"fetch {RemoteName}");

        // 3) Force local repo to match remote main exactly.
        // This intentionally discards local uncommitted / unpublished repo changes.
        RunGit(repoRootPath, $"reset --hard {RemoteName}/{BranchName}");

        string destinationPath = Path.Combine(repoRootPath, TargetPublishedFileName);
        string timestamp = DateTime.UtcNow.ToString("yyyyMMdd_HHmmss");

        File.WriteAllText(destinationPath, sourceHtmlText, new UTF8Encoding(encoderShouldEmitUTF8Identifier: false));

        RunGit(repoRootPath, $"add \"{TargetPublishedFileName}\"");
        RunGit(repoRootPath, $"commit -m \"TQGA code audit publish {timestamp}\"", allowNoChanges: true);
        RunGit(repoRootPath, $"push {RemoteName} {BranchName}");

        return new GitHubCodeAuditPublishResult
        {
            RepoRootPath = repoRootPath,
            SourceAuditHtmlPath = latestAuditHtml,
            PublishedHtmlPath = destinationPath,
            PublicUrl = PublicUrl
        };
    }

    private static void EnsureGitRepository(string repoRootPath)
    {
        string gitFolder = Path.Combine(repoRootPath, ".git");
        if (!Directory.Exists(gitFolder))
        {
            throw new InvalidOperationException(
                $"Selected folder is not a Git repository. Missing .git folder at: {repoRootPath}");
        }
    }

    private static void RunGit(
        string workingDirectory,
        string arguments,
        bool allowNoChanges = false,
        bool allowFailure = false)
    {
        string gitExePath = ResolveGitExecutablePath();

        using var process = new Process();
        process.StartInfo = new ProcessStartInfo
        {
            FileName = gitExePath,
            Arguments = arguments,
            WorkingDirectory = workingDirectory,
            RedirectStandardOutput = true,
            RedirectStandardError = true,
            UseShellExecute = false,
            CreateNoWindow = true
        };

        try
        {
            process.Start();
        }
        catch (Win32Exception ex)
        {
            throw new InvalidOperationException(
                "Git executable could not be started. Install Git for Windows or add git.exe to PATH. " +
                $"Resolved git path attempt: {gitExePath}",
                ex);
        }

        string stdOut = process.StandardOutput.ReadToEnd();
        string stdErr = process.StandardError.ReadToEnd();

        process.WaitForExit();

        if (process.ExitCode == 0)
            return;

        string combined = $"{stdOut}\n{stdErr}".Trim();

        if (allowFailure)
            return;

        if (allowNoChanges &&
            (combined.Contains("nothing to commit", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase) ||
             combined.Contains("no changes added to commit", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase)))
        {
            return;
        }

        throw new InvalidOperationException(
            $"Git command failed.\n\nCommand: git {arguments}\n\nOutput:\n{combined}");
    }

    private static string ResolveGitExecutablePath()
    {
        string[] candidates =
        [
            "git",
            @"C:\Program Files\Git\cmd\git.exe",
            @"C:\Program Files\Git\bin\git.exe",
            @"C:\Program Files (x86)\Git\cmd\git.exe",
            @"C:\Program Files (x86)\Git\bin\git.exe"
        ];

        foreach (string candidate in candidates)
        {
            if (candidate.Equals("git", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase))
                return candidate;

            if (File.Exists(candidate))
                return candidate;
        }

        return "git";
    }
}

public sealed class GitHubCodeAuditPublishResult
{
    public string RepoRootPath { get; init; } = string.Empty;
    public string SourceAuditHtmlPath { get; init; } = string.Empty;
    public string PublishedHtmlPath { get; init; } = string.Empty;
    public string PublicUrl { get; init; } = string.Empty;
}

 F I L E :   D : \ D   D A T A   B A C K U P \ A R I F 5 \ T Q G A \ T Q G A . A p p l i c a t i o n \ S e r v i c e s \ G i t H u b P a g e s P u b l i s h S e r v i c e . c s 
 
 T Y P E :   . c s 
 
 S I Z E :   2 2 . 4 8   K B 
 
 L I N E S :   4 5 8 
 
 = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = 
 
 using System.ComponentModel;
using System.Diagnostics;
using System.Text;
using TQGA.Application.Paths;

namespace TQGA.Application.Services;

public sealed class GitHubPagesPublishService
{
    private const string RepoPathConfigFileName = "github_pages_repo_path.txt";
    private const int WebSafeMaxChars = 500_000;
    private const string RemoteName = "origin";
    private const string BranchName = "main";

    public GitHubPagesPublishResult PublishReportAll31(
        string sourceReportPath,
        string sourceReportText,
        string repoRootPath)
    {
        ArgumentException.ThrowIfNullOrWhiteSpace(sourceReportPath);
        ArgumentException.ThrowIfNullOrWhiteSpace(sourceReportText);
        ArgumentException.ThrowIfNullOrWhiteSpace(repoRootPath);

        if (!File.Exists(sourceReportPath))
            throw new FileNotFoundException("Source report file not found.", sourceReportPath);

        if (!Directory.Exists(repoRootPath))
            throw new DirectoryNotFoundException($"GitHub Pages repo folder not found: {repoRootPath}");

        EnsureGitRepository(repoRootPath);

        string timestamp = DateTime.UtcNow.ToString("yyyyMMdd_HHmmss");
        string sourceFileName = Path.GetFileName(sourceReportPath);

        string localArchiveRoot = GetLocalArchiveRoot(repoRootPath);
        Directory.CreateDirectory(localArchiveRoot);

        string archivedReportPath = Path.Combine(
            localArchiveRoot,
            $"REPORT_ALL_31_{timestamp}.txt");

        string latestReportPath = Path.Combine(repoRootPath, "FULL_REPORT_LATEST.txt");
        string latestHtmlPath = Path.Combine(repoRootPath, "index.html");
        string reportsIndexHtmlPath = Path.Combine(repoRootPath, "reports.html");
        string gitIgnorePath = Path.Combine(repoRootPath, ".gitignore");

        File.Copy(sourceReportPath, archivedReportPath, overwrite: true);

        string webSafeText = TrimReportForWeb(sourceReportText, WebSafeMaxChars);
        File.WriteAllText(latestReportPath, webSafeText, Encoding.UTF8);

        string html = BuildHtmlAuditPage(webSafeText, sourceFileName, timestamp);
        File.WriteAllText(latestHtmlPath, html, Encoding.UTF8);

        string reportsIndexHtml = BuildReportsIndexPage(localArchiveRoot);
        File.WriteAllText(reportsIndexHtmlPath, reportsIndexHtml, Encoding.UTF8);

        EnsureGitIgnoreRules(gitIgnorePath);

        CleanupGitTrackedLargeFiles(repoRootPath);
        CleanupPhysicalLargeFilesFromRepoRoot(repoRootPath);

        RunGit(repoRootPath, "add .");
        RunGit(repoRootPath, $"commit -m \"TQGA auto publish {timestamp}\"", allowNoChanges: true);
        RunGit(repoRootPath, "push");

        SaveRepoPath(repoRootPath);

        return new GitHubPagesPublishResult
        {
            RepoRootPath = repoRootPath,
            SourceReportPath = sourceReportPath,
            PublishedLatestTextPath = latestReportPath,
            PublishedIndexHtmlPath = latestHtmlPath,
            PublishedArchiveReportPath = archivedReportPath,
            PublishedReportsIndexPath = reportsIndexHtmlPath,
            PublicUrl = "https://arifpisonium.github.io/",
            PublicLatestTextUrl = "https://arifpisonium.github.io/FULL_REPORT_LATEST.txt",
            PublicReportsIndexUrl = "https://arifpisonium.github.io/reports.html"
        };
    }

    public GitHubLatestReportHtmlPublishResult PublishLatestReportAll31Html(string repoRootPath)
    {
        ArgumentException.ThrowIfNullOrWhiteSpace(repoRootPath);

        if (!Directory.Exists(repoRootPath))
            throw new DirectoryNotFoundException($"GitHub Pages repo folder not found: {repoRootPath}");

        EnsureGitRepository(repoRootPath);
        Directory.CreateDirectory(DataPaths.Reports);

        string latestReportHtmlPath = Directory
            .EnumerateFiles(DataPaths.Reports, "REPORT_ALL_31_*.html", SearchOption.TopDirectoryOnly)
            .OrderByDescending(File.GetLastWriteTimeUtc)
            .FirstOrDefault()
            ?? throw new FileNotFoundException(
                "No generated REPORT_ALL_31 HTML file was found in Reports. Please click REPORT ALL 31 first.");

        string sourceHtmlText = File.ReadAllText(latestReportHtmlPath, Encoding.UTF8);
        if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(sourceHtmlText))
            throw new InvalidOperationException($"REPORT_ALL_31 HTML file is empty: {latestReportHtmlPath}");

        // Same operational discipline as code-audit publishing:
        // manual GitHub web edits may exist, so always hard-sync local clone to remote first.
        RunGit(repoRootPath, "rebase --abort", allowFailure: true);
        RunGit(repoRootPath, $"fetch {RemoteName}");
        RunGit(repoRootPath, $"reset --hard {RemoteName}/{BranchName}");

        string timestamp = DateTime.UtcNow.ToString("yyyyMMdd_HHmmss");
        string localArchiveRoot = GetLocalArchiveRoot(repoRootPath);
        Directory.CreateDirectory(localArchiveRoot);

        string archivedHtmlPath = Path.Combine(
            localArchiveRoot,
            $"REPORT_ALL_31_PUBLISHED_HTML_{timestamp}.html");

        string publishedIndexHtmlPath = Path.Combine(repoRootPath, "index.html");

        File.Copy(latestReportHtmlPath, archivedHtmlPath, overwrite: true);
        File.WriteAllText(
            publishedIndexHtmlPath,
            sourceHtmlText,
            new UTF8Encoding(encoderShouldEmitUTF8Identifier: false));

        RunGit(repoRootPath, "add index.html");
        RunGit(repoRootPath, $"commit -m \"TQGA report html publish {timestamp}\"", allowNoChanges: true);
        RunGit(repoRootPath, $"push {RemoteName} {BranchName}");

        SaveRepoPath(repoRootPath);

        return new GitHubLatestReportHtmlPublishResult
        {
            RepoRootPath = repoRootPath,
            SourceReportHtmlPath = latestReportHtmlPath,
            PublishedIndexHtmlPath = publishedIndexHtmlPath,
            ArchivedHtmlPath = archivedHtmlPath,
            PublicUrl = "https://arifpisonium.github.io/"
        };
    }

    public string? TryLoadSavedRepoPath()
    {
        string path = GetRepoPathConfigPath();
        if (!File.Exists(path))
            return null;

        string value = File.ReadAllText(path).Trim();
        if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(value))
            return null;

        return Directory.Exists(value) ? value : null;
    }

    public void SaveRepoPath(string repoRootPath)
    {
        ArgumentException.ThrowIfNullOrWhiteSpace(repoRootPath);

        string path = GetRepoPathConfigPath();
        File.WriteAllText(path, repoRootPath.Trim(), Encoding.UTF8);
    }

    private static void EnsureGitRepository(string repoRootPath)
    {
        string gitFolder = Path.Combine(repoRootPath, ".git");
        if (!Directory.Exists(gitFolder))
            throw new InvalidOperationException(
                $"Selected folder is not a Git repository. Missing .git folder at: {repoRootPath}");
    }

    private static string GetRepoPathConfigPath()
    {
        string configDir = Path.Combine(AppContext.BaseDirectory, "Config");
        Directory.CreateDirectory(configDir);
        return Path.Combine(configDir, RepoPathConfigFileName);
    }

    private static string GetLocalArchiveRoot(string repoRootPath)
    {
        string parent = Directory.GetParent(repoRootPath)?.FullName ?? repoRootPath;
        return Path.Combine(parent, "TQGA_LocalArchives");
    }

    private static void CleanupGitTrackedLargeFiles(string repoRootPath)
    {
        RunGit(repoRootPath, "reset HEAD .", allowNoChanges: true);

        RunGit(repoRootPath, "rm --cached --ignore-unmatch FULL_REPORT_*.txt", allowNoChanges: true);
        RunGit(repoRootPath, "rm --cached --ignore-unmatch REPORT_ALL_31_*.txt", allowNoChanges: true);
        RunGit(repoRootPath, "rm -r --cached --ignore-unmatch reports", allowNoChanges: true);

        RunGit(repoRootPath, "rm --cached --ignore-unmatch FULL_REPORT_LATEST.txt", allowNoChanges: true);
        RunGit(repoRootPath, "rm --cached --ignore-unmatch index.html", allowNoChanges: true);
        RunGit(repoRootPath, "rm --cached --ignore-unmatch reports.html", allowNoChanges: true);
    }

    private static void CleanupPhysicalLargeFilesFromRepoRoot(string repoRootPath)
    {
        foreach (string file in Directory.GetFiles(repoRootPath, "FULL_REPORT_*.txt", SearchOption.TopDirectoryOnly))
        {
            TryDeleteFile(file);
        }

        foreach (string file in Directory.GetFiles(repoRootPath, "REPORT_ALL_31_*.txt", SearchOption.TopDirectoryOnly))
        {
            TryDeleteFile(file);
        }

        string reportsFolder = Path.Combine(repoRootPath, "reports");
        if (Directory.Exists(reportsFolder))
        {
            try
            {
                Directory.Delete(reportsFolder, recursive: true);
            }
            catch
            {
                // Keep non-fatal. Git index cleanup above is the critical part.
            }
        }
    }

    private static void TryDeleteFile(string filePath)
    {
        try
        {
            if (File.Exists(filePath))
                File.Delete(filePath);
        }
        catch
        {
            // Non-fatal cleanup attempt.
        }
    }

    private static void RunGit(
        string workingDirectory,
        string arguments,
        bool allowNoChanges = false,
        bool allowFailure = false)
    {
        string gitExePath = ResolveGitExecutablePath();

        using var process = new Process();

        process.StartInfo = new ProcessStartInfo
        {
            FileName = gitExePath,
            Arguments = arguments,
            WorkingDirectory = workingDirectory,
            RedirectStandardOutput = true,
            RedirectStandardError = true,
            UseShellExecute = false,
            CreateNoWindow = true
        };

        try
        {
            process.Start();
        }
        catch (Win32Exception ex)
        {
            throw new InvalidOperationException(
                "Git executable could not be started. " +
                "Install Git for Windows or add git.exe to PATH. " +
                $"Resolved git path attempt: {gitExePath}",
                ex);
        }

        string stdOut = process.StandardOutput.ReadToEnd();
        string stdErr = process.StandardError.ReadToEnd();

        process.WaitForExit();

        if (process.ExitCode == 0)
            return;

        string combined = $"{stdOut}\n{stdErr}".Trim();

        if (allowFailure)
            return;

        if (allowNoChanges &&
            (combined.Contains("nothing to commit", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase) ||
             combined.Contains("did not match any files", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase) ||
             combined.Contains("fatal: pathspec", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase) ||
             combined.Contains("no changes added to commit", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase)))
        {
            return;
        }

        throw new InvalidOperationException(
            $"Git command failed.\nExecutable: {gitExePath}\nCommand: git {arguments}\n\n{combined}");
    }

    private static string ResolveGitExecutablePath()
    {
        var candidates = new List();

        string pathEnv = Environment.GetEnvironmentVariable("PATH") ?? string.Empty;
        foreach (string rawPart in pathEnv.Split(';', StringSplitOptions.RemoveEmptyEntries | StringSplitOptions.TrimEntries))
        {
            try
            {
                string candidate = Path.Combine(rawPart, "git.exe");
                candidates.Add(candidate);
            }
            catch
            {
            }
        }

        candidates.Add(@"C:\Program Files\Git\cmd\git.exe");
        candidates.Add(@"C:\Program Files\Git\bin\git.exe");
        candidates.Add(@"C:\Program Files (x86)\Git\cmd\git.exe");
        candidates.Add(@"C:\Program Files (x86)\Git\bin\git.exe");

        string localAppData = Environment.GetFolderPath(Environment.SpecialFolder.LocalApplicationData);
        if (!string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(localAppData))
        {
            candidates.Add(Path.Combine(localAppData, @"Programs\Git\cmd\git.exe"));
            candidates.Add(Path.Combine(localAppData, @"Programs\Git\bin\git.exe"));
        }

        string userProfile = Environment.GetFolderPath(Environment.SpecialFolder.UserProfile);
        if (!string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(userProfile))
        {
            candidates.Add(Path.Combine(userProfile, @"AppData\Local\Programs\Git\cmd\git.exe"));
            candidates.Add(Path.Combine(userProfile, @"AppData\Local\Programs\Git\bin\git.exe"));
        }

        foreach (string candidate in candidates.Distinct(StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase))
        {
            if (File.Exists(candidate))
                return candidate;
        }

        throw new FileNotFoundException(
            "git.exe was not found. Install Git for Windows and ensure git is available in PATH, " +
            "or installed in a standard location such as C:\\Program Files\\Git\\cmd\\git.exe.");
    }

    private static string TrimReportForWeb(string fullText, int maxChars)
    {
        if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(fullText))
            return string.Empty;

        if (fullText.Length <= maxChars)
            return fullText;

        return
            fullText[..maxChars] +
            Environment.NewLine + Environment.NewLine +
            "==============================" + Environment.NewLine +
            "TRUNCATED FOR WEB VIEW" + Environment.NewLine +
            "Full report available locally" + Environment.NewLine +
            "==============================" + Environment.NewLine;
    }

    private static void EnsureGitIgnoreRules(string gitIgnorePath)
    {
        var requiredRules = new[]
        {
            "FULL_REPORT_*.txt",
            "REPORT_ALL_31_*.txt",
            "reports/",
            "TQGA_LocalArchives/"
        };

        List existingLines = File.Exists(gitIgnorePath)
            ? File.ReadAllLines(gitIgnorePath).ToList()
            : new List();

        bool changed = false;

        foreach (string rule in requiredRules)
        {
            if (!existingLines.Any(x => x.Trim().Equals(rule, StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase)))
            {
                existingLines.Add(rule);
                changed = true;
            }
        }

        if (changed)
            File.WriteAllLines(gitIgnorePath, existingLines, Encoding.UTF8);
    }

    private static string BuildHtmlAuditPage(string reportText, string fileName, string timestamp)
    {
        string escaped = System.Net.WebUtility.HtmlEncode(reportText ?? string.Empty);

        var sb = new StringBuilder();

        sb.AppendLine("");
        sb.AppendLine("");
        sb.AppendLine("");
        sb.AppendLine("    ");
        sb.AppendLine("    ");
        sb.AppendLine("    TQGA REPORT ALL 31");
        sb.AppendLine("    ");
        sb.AppendLine("");
        sb.AppendLine("");
        sb.AppendLine("    
");
        sb.AppendLine("        
");
        sb.AppendLine("            
");
        sb.AppendLine("                
TQGA REPORT ALL 31
");
        sb.AppendLine("                
");
        sb.AppendLine($"                    
Published (UTC): {DateTime.UtcNow:yyyy-MM-dd HH:mm:ss}
");
        sb.AppendLine($"                    
Build Stamp: {System.Net.WebUtility.HtmlEncode(timestamp)}
");
        sb.AppendLine($"                    
Source File: {System.Net.WebUtility.HtmlEncode(fileName)}
");
        sb.AppendLine("                    
Mode: Web-safe trimmed publish
");
        sb.AppendLine("                    
Open raw text | Open reports index
");
        sb.AppendLine("                
");
        sb.AppendLine("            
");
        sb.AppendLine($"            
{escaped}
");
        sb.AppendLine("        
");
        sb.AppendLine("    
");
        sb.AppendLine("");
        sb.AppendLine("");

        return sb.ToString();
    }

    private static string BuildReportsIndexPage(string localArchiveRoot)
    {
        Directory.CreateDirectory(localArchiveRoot);

        var files = Directory.GetFiles(localArchiveRoot, "*.txt", SearchOption.TopDirectoryOnly)
            .Select(Path.GetFileName)
            .Where(x => !string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(x))
            .OrderByDescending(x => x, StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase)
            .ToList();

        var sb = new StringBuilder();

        sb.AppendLine("");
        sb.AppendLine("");
        sb.AppendLine("");
        sb.AppendLine("    ");
        sb.AppendLine("    ");
        sb.AppendLine("    TQGA Reports Index");
        sb.AppendLine("    ");
        sb.AppendLine("");
        sb.AppendLine("");
        sb.AppendLine("    
");
        sb.AppendLine("        
");
        sb.AppendLine("            
TQGA Reports Index
");
        sb.AppendLine("            
Open latest audit page | Open latest raw text
");
        sb.AppendLine("            
Full archive files are kept locally outside the GitHub Pages repo and are not pushed to GitHub.
");
        sb.AppendLine("            
    ");

        foreach (string? file in files)
        {
            if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(file))
                continue;

            string safe = System.Net.WebUtility.HtmlEncode(file);
            sb.AppendLine($"                
  • {safe}
    • ");
        }

        sb.AppendLine("            
");
        sb.AppendLine("        
");
        sb.AppendLine("    
");
        sb.AppendLine("");
        sb.AppendLine("");

        return sb.ToString();
    }
}

public sealed class GitHubPagesPublishResult
{
    public string RepoRootPath { get; init; } = string.Empty;
    public string SourceReportPath { get; init; } = string.Empty;
    public string PublishedLatestTextPath { get; init; } = string.Empty;
    public string PublishedIndexHtmlPath { get; init; } = string.Empty;
    public string PublishedArchiveReportPath { get; init; } = string.Empty;
    public string PublishedReportsIndexPath { get; init; } = string.Empty;
    public string PublicUrl { get; init; } = string.Empty;
    public string PublicLatestTextUrl { get; init; } = string.Empty;
    public string PublicReportsIndexUrl { get; init; } = string.Empty;
}

public sealed class GitHubLatestReportHtmlPublishResult
{
    public string RepoRootPath { get; init; } = string.Empty;
    public string SourceReportHtmlPath { get; init; } = string.Empty;
    public string PublishedIndexHtmlPath { get; init; } = string.Empty;
    public string ArchivedHtmlPath { get; init; } = string.Empty;
    public string PublicUrl { get; init; } = string.Empty;
}

 using System.Diagnostics;
using System.Text;
using Google.Apis.Auth.OAuth2;
using Google.Apis.Drive.v3;
using Google.Apis.Services;
using Google.Apis.Util.Store;
using TQGA.Application.Paths;

namespace TQGA.Application.Services;

public sealed class GoogleDriveCombinedPublishService
{
    private const string GoogleRootFolderName = "TQGA_GOOGLE";
    private const string OAuthClientFileName = "oauth_client_secret.json";
    private const string TokenStoreFolderName = "token_store";

    // User-requested dedicated folder for the combined report only.
    private const string CombinedFolderIdOrLink =
        "https://drive.google.com/drive/folders/1fnfG5-xfsk-rwaLL351r3ePScOh7p3S0";

    private static readonly string[] Scopes =
    [
        DriveService.Scope.Drive
    ];

    public async Task PublishCombinedAsync(CancellationToken ct = default)
    {
        string reportDir = DataPaths.Reports;
        Directory.CreateDirectory(reportDir);

        string combinedFilePath = BuildCombinedReportFile(reportDir);

        string backupRoot = ResolveBackupRoot(reportDir);
        string googleRoot = Path.Combine(backupRoot, GoogleRootFolderName);
        Directory.CreateDirectory(googleRoot);

        string oauthClientPath = Path.Combine(googleRoot, OAuthClientFileName);
        string tokenStorePath = Path.Combine(googleRoot, TokenStoreFolderName);

        EnsureRequiredFileExists(
            oauthClientPath,
            "Google OAuth client file not found. Please create:\n" + oauthClientPath);

        string folderId = ParseFolderId(CombinedFolderIdOrLink);

        if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(folderId))
        {
            throw new InvalidOperationException(
                "Combined Google Drive folder id is empty or invalid.");
        }

        DriveService service = await CreateDriveServiceAsync(
            oauthClientPath,
            tokenStorePath,
            "TQGA Google Combined Publish",
            ct);

        // Keep only the latest combined report in this dedicated folder.
        await DeleteExistingFilesInFolderAsync(service, folderId, ct);

        string uploadFileName = Path.GetFileName(combinedFilePath);

        var metadata = new Google.Apis.Drive.v3.Data.File
        {
            Name = uploadFileName,
            Parents = [folderId]
        };

        await using FileStream stream = new(combinedFilePath, FileMode.Open, FileAccess.Read, FileShare.Read);

        var createRequest = service.Files.Create(metadata, stream, "text/plain");
        createRequest.Fields = "id,name";

        var uploaded = await createRequest.UploadAsync(ct);
        if (uploaded.Status != Google.Apis.Upload.UploadStatus.Completed)
        {
            throw new InvalidOperationException(
                $"Google Drive combined upload failed. Status: {uploaded.Status}");
        }

        Google.Apis.Drive.v3.Data.File? created = createRequest.ResponseBody;
        if (created == null || string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(created.Id))
        {
            throw new InvalidOperationException(
                "Google Drive did not return a file id for the combined report.");
        }

        var permission = new Google.Apis.Drive.v3.Data.Permission
        {
            Type = "anyone",
            Role = "reader"
        };

        var permissionRequest = service.Permissions.Create(permission, created.Id);
        permissionRequest.Fields = "id";
        await permissionRequest.ExecuteAsync(ct);

        string folderLink = $"https://drive.google.com/drive/folders/{folderId}";
        string viewLink = $"https://drive.google.com/file/d/{created.Id}/view";
        string directLink = $"https://drive.google.com/uc?export=download&id={created.Id}";

        TryOpenInBrowser(viewLink);

        return new GoogleDriveCombinedPublishResult
        {
            Success = true,
            ReportDirectory = reportDir,
            CombinedFilePath = combinedFilePath,
            CombinedFileName = uploadFileName,
            GoogleDriveFolderId = folderId,
            GoogleDriveFolderLink = folderLink,
            PublishedFileId = created.Id,
            PublicViewLink = viewLink,
            PublicDirectLink = directLink
        };
    }

    private static string BuildCombinedReportFile(string reportDir)
    {
        var eligibleFiles = Directory
            .GetFiles(reportDir, "*.*", SearchOption.AllDirectories)
            .Where(IsEligibleReportFile)
            .OrderBy(x => x, StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase)
            .ToList();

        if (eligibleFiles.Count == 0)
            throw new InvalidOperationException("No eligible report files found to combine.");

        string combinedPath = Path.Combine(
            reportDir,
            $"REPORT_ALL_30_{DateTime.UtcNow:yyyyMMdd_HHmmss}.txt");

        var sb = new StringBuilder();

        sb.AppendLine("TQGA REPORT ALL 30");
        sb.AppendLine("============================================================");
        sb.AppendLine($"Generated UTC: {DateTime.UtcNow:yyyy-MM-dd HH:mm:ss}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Total Files Combined: {eligibleFiles.Count}");
        sb.AppendLine();

        foreach (string filePath in eligibleFiles)
        {
            string fileName = Path.GetFileName(filePath);
            string content = ReadAllTextSafe(filePath);

            sb.AppendLine("############################################################");
            sb.AppendLine($"BEGIN FILE: {fileName}");
            sb.AppendLine("############################################################");
            sb.AppendLine(content.TrimEnd());
            sb.AppendLine();
            sb.AppendLine("############################################################");
            sb.AppendLine($"END FILE: {fileName}");
            sb.AppendLine("############################################################");
            sb.AppendLine();
        }

        File.WriteAllText(combinedPath, sb.ToString(), Encoding.UTF8);
        return combinedPath;
    }

    private static bool IsEligibleReportFile(string path)
    {
        string fileName = Path.GetFileName(path);
        string ext = Path.GetExtension(path);

        if (!ext.Equals(".txt", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase) &&
            !ext.Equals(".csv", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase))
        {
            return false;
        }

        if (fileName.StartsWith("REPORT_ALL_", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase))
            return false;

        if (fileName.Equals("latest_public_links.txt", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase))
            return false;

        return true;
    }

    private static string ReadAllTextSafe(string path)
    {
        try
        {
            return File.ReadAllText(path, Encoding.UTF8);
        }
        catch
        {
            return File.ReadAllText(path);
        }
    }

    private static async Task CreateDriveServiceAsync(
        string oauthClientPath,
        string tokenStorePath,
        string applicationName,
        CancellationToken ct)
    {
        await using FileStream stream = new(oauthClientPath, FileMode.Open, FileAccess.Read, FileShare.Read);
        ClientSecrets secrets = GoogleClientSecrets.FromStream(stream).Secrets;

        UserCredential credential = await GoogleWebAuthorizationBroker.AuthorizeAsync(
            secrets,
            Scopes,
            "user",
            ct,
            new FileDataStore(tokenStorePath, true));

        return new DriveService(new BaseClientService.Initializer
        {
            HttpClientInitializer = credential,
            ApplicationName = applicationName
        });
    }

    private static async Task DeleteExistingFilesInFolderAsync(
        DriveService service,
        string folderId,
        CancellationToken ct)
    {
        string? pageToken = null;

        do
        {
            var listRequest = service.Files.List();
            listRequest.Q = $"'{folderId}' in parents and trashed = false";
            listRequest.Fields = "nextPageToken, files(id, name)";
            listRequest.PageToken = pageToken;

            var page = await listRequest.ExecuteAsync(ct);

            foreach (Google.Apis.Drive.v3.Data.File file in page.Files ?? Enumerable.Empty())
            {
                if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(file.Id))
                    continue;

                var deleteRequest = service.Files.Delete(file.Id);
                await deleteRequest.ExecuteAsync(ct);
            }

            pageToken = page.NextPageToken;
        }
        while (!string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(pageToken));
    }

    private static string ParseFolderId(string value)
    {
        if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(value))
            return string.Empty;

        string trimmed = value.Trim();

        if (!trimmed.Contains("http", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase))
            return trimmed;

        const string marker = "/folders/";
        int idx = trimmed.IndexOf(marker, StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase);
        if (idx >= 0)
        {
            string tail = trimmed[(idx + marker.Length)..];
            int end = tail.IndexOfAny(['?', '&', '/']);
            return end >= 0 ? tail[..end] : tail;
        }

        return trimmed;
    }

    private static string ResolveBackupRoot(string reportDir)
    {
        DirectoryInfo? current = new(reportDir);

        while (current != null)
        {
            if (current.Name.Equals("D DATA BACKUP", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase))
                return current.FullName;

            current = current.Parent;
        }

        return Directory.GetParent(reportDir)?.FullName ?? reportDir;
    }

    private static void EnsureRequiredFileExists(string path, string message)
    {
        if (!File.Exists(path))
            throw new FileNotFoundException(message, path);
    }

    private static void TryOpenInBrowser(string url)
    {
        Process.Start(new ProcessStartInfo
        {
            FileName = url,
            UseShellExecute = true
        });
    }
}

    public bool Success { get; init; }
    public string ReportDirectory { get; init; } = string.Empty;
    public string CombinedFilePath { get; init; } = string.Empty;
    public string CombinedFileName { get; init; } = string.Empty;
    public string GoogleDriveFolderId { get; init; } = string.Empty;
    public string GoogleDriveFolderLink { get; init; } = string.Empty;
    public string PublishedFileId { get; init; } = string.Empty;
    public string PublicViewLink { get; init; } = string.Empty;
    public string PublicDirectLink { get; init; } = string.Empty;

 = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = 
 
 using System.Diagnostics;
using System.Text;
using Google.Apis.Auth.OAuth2;
using Google.Apis.Drive.v3;
using Google.Apis.Services;
using Google.Apis.Util.Store;
using TQGA.Application.Paths;

namespace TQGA.Application.Services;

public sealed class GoogleDriveCombinedStablePublishService
{
    private const string GoogleRootFolderName = "TQGA_GOOGLE";
    private const string OAuthClientFileName = "oauth_client_secret.json";
    private const string TokenStoreFolderName = "token_store";

    // Stable file ID provided by user.
    private const string StableGoogleDriveFileId = "1AD0USboa-n0TiHlx0ki-cwgEFmfd-Bws";

    private static readonly string[] Scopes =
    [
        DriveService.Scope.Drive
    ];

    public async Task PublishStableAsync(CancellationToken ct = default)
    {
        string reportDir = DataPaths.Reports;
        Directory.CreateDirectory(reportDir);

        string combinedFilePath = BuildCombinedReportFile(reportDir);

        string backupRoot = ResolveBackupRoot(reportDir);
        string googleRoot = Path.Combine(backupRoot, GoogleRootFolderName);
        Directory.CreateDirectory(googleRoot);

        string oauthClientPath = Path.Combine(googleRoot, OAuthClientFileName);
        string tokenStorePath = Path.Combine(googleRoot, TokenStoreFolderName);

        EnsureRequiredFileExists(
            oauthClientPath,
            "Google OAuth client file not found. Please create:\n" + oauthClientPath);

        DriveService service = await CreateDriveServiceAsync(
            oauthClientPath,
            tokenStorePath,
            "TQGA Google Stable Combined Publish",
            ct);

        var existing = await service.Files.Get(StableGoogleDriveFileId).ExecuteAsync(ct);
        if (existing == null || string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(existing.Id))
        {
            throw new InvalidOperationException(
                $"Google Drive stable file not found for id: {StableGoogleDriveFileId}");
        }

        string uploadFileName = Path.GetFileName(combinedFilePath);

        var metadata = new Google.Apis.Drive.v3.Data.File
        {
            Name = uploadFileName,
            MimeType = "text/plain"
        };

        await using FileStream stream = new(combinedFilePath, FileMode.Open, FileAccess.Read, FileShare.Read);

        var updateRequest = service.Files.Update(metadata, StableGoogleDriveFileId, stream, "text/plain");
        updateRequest.Fields = "id,name,webViewLink,webContentLink";

        var uploaded = await updateRequest.UploadAsync(ct);
        if (uploaded.Status != Google.Apis.Upload.UploadStatus.Completed)
        {
            throw new InvalidOperationException(
                $"Google Drive stable combined update failed. Status: {uploaded.Status}");
        }

        Google.Apis.Drive.v3.Data.File? updated = updateRequest.ResponseBody;
        if (updated == null || string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(updated.Id))
        {
            throw new InvalidOperationException(
                "Google Drive did not return a valid file after stable combined update.");
        }

        var permission = new Google.Apis.Drive.v3.Data.Permission
        {
            Type = "anyone",
            Role = "reader"
        };

        try
        {
            var permissionRequest = service.Permissions.Create(permission, updated.Id);
            permissionRequest.Fields = "id";
            await permissionRequest.ExecuteAsync(ct);
        }
        catch
        {
            // Ignore duplicate/public permission creation issues.
        }

        string publicViewLink = $"https://drive.google.com/file/d/{updated.Id}/view";
        string publicDirectLink = $"https://drive.google.com/uc?export=download&id={updated.Id}";

        TryOpenInBrowser(publicViewLink);

        return new GoogleDriveCombinedStablePublishResult
        {
            Success = true,
            ReportDirectory = reportDir,
            CombinedFilePath = combinedFilePath,
            CombinedFileName = uploadFileName,
            StableFileId = updated.Id,
            PublicViewLink = publicViewLink,
            PublicDirectLink = publicDirectLink
        };
    }

    private static string BuildCombinedReportFile(string reportDir)
    {
        List eligibleFiles = Directory
            .GetFiles(reportDir, "*.*", SearchOption.AllDirectories)
            .Where(IsEligibleReportFile)
            .OrderBy(x => x, StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase)
            .ToList();

        if (eligibleFiles.Count == 0)
            throw new InvalidOperationException("No eligible report files found to combine.");

        string combinedPath = Path.Combine(
            reportDir,
            $"REPORT_ALL_30_{DateTime.UtcNow:yyyyMMdd_HHmmss}.txt");

        var sb = new StringBuilder();

        sb.AppendLine("TQGA REPORT ALL 30");
        sb.AppendLine("============================================================");
        sb.AppendLine($"Generated UTC: {DateTime.UtcNow:yyyy-MM-dd HH:mm:ss}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Total Files Combined: {eligibleFiles.Count}");
        sb.AppendLine();

        foreach (string filePath in eligibleFiles)
        {
            string fileName = Path.GetFileName(filePath);
            string content = ReadAllTextSafe(filePath);

            sb.AppendLine("############################################################");
            sb.AppendLine($"BEGIN FILE: {fileName}");
            sb.AppendLine("############################################################");
            sb.AppendLine(content.TrimEnd());
            sb.AppendLine();
            sb.AppendLine("############################################################");
            sb.AppendLine($"END FILE: {fileName}");
            sb.AppendLine("############################################################");
            sb.AppendLine();
        }

        File.WriteAllText(combinedPath, sb.ToString(), Encoding.UTF8);
        return combinedPath;
    }

    private static bool IsEligibleReportFile(string path)
    {
        string fileName = Path.GetFileName(path);
        string ext = Path.GetExtension(path);

        if (!ext.Equals(".txt", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase) &&
            !ext.Equals(".csv", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase))
        {
            return false;
        }

        if (fileName.StartsWith("REPORT_ALL_", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase))
            return false;

        if (fileName.Equals("latest_public_links.txt", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase))
            return false;

        return true;
    }

    private static string ReadAllTextSafe(string path)
    {
        try
        {
            return File.ReadAllText(path, Encoding.UTF8);
        }
        catch
        {
            return File.ReadAllText(path);
        }
    }

    private static async Task CreateDriveServiceAsync(
        string oauthClientPath,
        string tokenStorePath,
        string applicationName,
        CancellationToken ct)
    {
        await using FileStream stream = new(oauthClientPath, FileMode.Open, FileAccess.Read, FileShare.Read);
        ClientSecrets secrets = GoogleClientSecrets.FromStream(stream).Secrets;

        UserCredential credential = await GoogleWebAuthorizationBroker.AuthorizeAsync(
            secrets,
            Scopes,
            "user",
            ct,
            new FileDataStore(tokenStorePath, true));

        return new DriveService(new BaseClientService.Initializer
        {
            HttpClientInitializer = credential,
            ApplicationName = applicationName
        });
    }

    private static string ResolveBackupRoot(string reportDir)
    {
        DirectoryInfo? current = new(reportDir);

        while (current != null)
        {
            if (current.Name.Equals("D DATA BACKUP", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase))
                return current.FullName;

            current = current.Parent;
        }

        return Directory.GetParent(reportDir)?.FullName ?? reportDir;
    }

    private static void EnsureRequiredFileExists(string path, string message)
    {
        if (!File.Exists(path))
            throw new FileNotFoundException(message, path);
    }

    private static void TryOpenInBrowser(string url)
    {
        Process.Start(new ProcessStartInfo
        {
            FileName = url,
            UseShellExecute = true
        });
    }
}

    public string CombinedFilePath { get; init; } = string.Empty;
    public string CombinedFileName { get; init; } = string.Empty;
    public string StableFileId { get; init; } = string.Empty;
    public string PublicViewLink { get; init; } = string.Empty;
    public string PublicDirectLink { get; init; } = string.Empty;
}

 F I L E :   D : \ D   D A T A   B A C K U P \ A R I F 5 \ T Q G A \ T Q G A . A p p l i c a t i o n \ S e r v i c e s \ G o o g l e D r i v e R e p o r t P u b l i s h S e r v i c e . c s

 = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = 
 
 using System.Diagnostics;
using System.Text;
using System.Text.Json;
using Google.Apis.Auth.OAuth2;
using Google.Apis.Drive.v3;
using Google.Apis.Services;
using Google.Apis.Util.Store;
using TQGA.Application.Paths;

namespace TQGA.Application.Services;

public sealed class GoogleDriveReportPublishService
{
    private const string GoogleRootFolderName = "TQGA_GOOGLE";
    private const string OAuthClientFileName = "oauth_client_secret.json";
    private const string PublishSettingsFileName = "publish_settings.json";
    private const string TokenStoreFolderName = "token_store";
    private const string LinksOutputFileName = "latest_public_links.txt";

    private static readonly string[] Scopes =
    [
        DriveService.Scope.Drive
    ];

    private static readonly JsonSerializerOptions SettingsJsonOptions = new()
    {
        PropertyNameCaseInsensitive = true
    };

    public async Task PublishAsync(CancellationToken ct = default)
    {
        string reportDir = DataPaths.Reports;
        Directory.CreateDirectory(reportDir);

        string backupRoot = ResolveBackupRoot(reportDir);
        string googleRoot = Path.Combine(backupRoot, GoogleRootFolderName);
        Directory.CreateDirectory(googleRoot);

        string oauthClientPath = Path.Combine(googleRoot, OAuthClientFileName);
        string settingsPath = Path.Combine(googleRoot, PublishSettingsFileName);
        string tokenStorePath = Path.Combine(googleRoot, TokenStoreFolderName);
        string linksOutputPath = Path.Combine(googleRoot, LinksOutputFileName);

        EnsureRequiredFileExists(
            oauthClientPath,
            "Google OAuth client file not found. Please create:\n" + oauthClientPath);

        EnsureRequiredFileExists(
            settingsPath,
            "Google publish settings file not found. Please create:\n" + settingsPath);

        GoogleDrivePublishSettings settings = LoadSettings(settingsPath);
        string folderId = ParseFolderId(settings.GoogleDriveFolderIdOrLink);

        if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(folderId))
        {
            throw new InvalidOperationException(
                "GoogleDriveFolderIdOrLink is empty or invalid in publish_settings.json.");
        }

        DriveService service = await CreateDriveServiceAsync(
            oauthClientPath,
            tokenStorePath,
            settings.ApplicationName,
            ct);

        if (settings.DeleteExistingFilesInFolderBeforeUpload)
            await DeleteExistingFilesInFolderAsync(service, folderId, ct);

        List localFiles = Directory
            .GetFiles(reportDir, "*.*", SearchOption.AllDirectories)
            .OrderBy(x => x, StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase)
            .ToList();

        List publishedFiles = [];

        foreach (string localPath in localFiles)
        {
            ct.ThrowIfCancellationRequested();

            string relativePath = Path.GetRelativePath(reportDir, localPath);
            string driveName = BuildDriveSafeName(relativePath);
            string mimeType = GetMimeType(localPath);

            var metadata = new Google.Apis.Drive.v3.Data.File
            {
                Name = driveName,
                Parents = [folderId]
            };

            await using FileStream stream = new(localPath, FileMode.Open, FileAccess.Read, FileShare.Read);

            var createRequest = service.Files.Create(metadata, stream, mimeType);
            createRequest.Fields = "id,name,webViewLink,webContentLink";

            var uploaded = await createRequest.UploadAsync(ct);
            if (uploaded.Status != Google.Apis.Upload.UploadStatus.Completed)
            {
                throw new InvalidOperationException(
                    $"Google Drive upload failed for file: {relativePath}. Status: {uploaded.Status}");
            }

            Google.Apis.Drive.v3.Data.File? created = createRequest.ResponseBody;
            if (created == null || string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(created.Id))
            {
                throw new InvalidOperationException(
                    $"Google Drive did not return a file id for: {relativePath}");
            }

            if (settings.MakeAnyoneWithLinkViewer)
            {
                var permission = new Google.Apis.Drive.v3.Data.Permission
                {
                    Type = "anyone",
                    Role = "reader"
                };

                var permissionRequest = service.Permissions.Create(permission, created.Id);
                permissionRequest.Fields = "id";
                await permissionRequest.ExecuteAsync(ct);
            }

            string publicLink = $"https://drive.google.com/uc?export=download&id={created.Id}";

            publishedFiles.Add(new GoogleDrivePublishedFile
            {
                LocalPath = localPath,
                RelativePath = relativePath,
                DriveFileId = created.Id,
                DriveFileName = created.Name ?? driveName,
                PublicLink = publicLink
            });
        }

        string folderPublicLink = $"https://drive.google.com/drive/folders/{folderId}";
        string linksText = BuildLinksText(folderPublicLink, publishedFiles);

        File.WriteAllText(linksOutputPath, linksText, Encoding.UTF8);
        TryOpenInBrowser(folderPublicLink);

        return new GoogleDrivePublishResult
        {
            Success = true,
            ReportDirectory = reportDir,
            GoogleConfigRoot = googleRoot,
            GoogleDriveFolderId = folderId,
            GoogleDriveFolderLink = folderPublicLink,
            PublishedCount = publishedFiles.Count,
            LinksOutputPath = linksOutputPath,
            FullLinksText = linksText,
            PublishedFiles = publishedFiles
        };
    }

    private static async Task CreateDriveServiceAsync(
        string oauthClientPath,
        string tokenStorePath,
        string? applicationName,
        CancellationToken ct)
    {
        await using FileStream stream = new(oauthClientPath, FileMode.Open, FileAccess.Read, FileShare.Read);
        ClientSecrets secrets = GoogleClientSecrets.FromStream(stream).Secrets;

        UserCredential credential = await GoogleWebAuthorizationBroker.AuthorizeAsync(
            secrets,
            Scopes,
            "user",
            ct,
            new FileDataStore(tokenStorePath, true));

        return new DriveService(new BaseClientService.Initializer
        {
            HttpClientInitializer = credential,
            ApplicationName = string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(applicationName)
                ? "TQGA Google Publish"
                : applicationName
        });
    }

    private static async Task DeleteExistingFilesInFolderAsync(
        DriveService service,
        string folderId,
        CancellationToken ct)
    {
        string? pageToken = null;

        do
        {
            var listRequest = service.Files.List();
            listRequest.Q = $"'{folderId}' in parents and trashed = false";
            listRequest.Fields = "nextPageToken, files(id, name)";
            listRequest.PageToken = pageToken;

            var page = await listRequest.ExecuteAsync(ct);

            foreach (Google.Apis.Drive.v3.Data.File file in page.Files ?? Enumerable.Empty())
            {
                if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(file.Id))
                    continue;

                var deleteRequest = service.Files.Delete(file.Id);
                await deleteRequest.ExecuteAsync(ct);
            }

            pageToken = page.NextPageToken;
        }
        while (!string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(pageToken));
    }

    private static GoogleDrivePublishSettings LoadSettings(string settingsPath)
    {
        string json = File.ReadAllText(settingsPath, Encoding.UTF8);

        GoogleDrivePublishSettings? settings = JsonSerializer.Deserialize(
            json,
            SettingsJsonOptions);

        if (settings == null)
            throw new InvalidOperationException("Could not parse publish_settings.json.");

        return settings;
    }

    private static string ParseFolderId(string value)
    {
        if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(value))
            return string.Empty;

        string trimmed = value.Trim();

        if (!trimmed.Contains("http", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase))
            return trimmed;

        const string marker = "/folders/";
        int idx = trimmed.IndexOf(marker, StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase);
        if (idx >= 0)
        {
            string tail = trimmed[(idx + marker.Length)..];
            int end = tail.IndexOfAny(['?', '&', '/']);
            return end >= 0 ? tail[..end] : tail;
        }

        return trimmed;
    }

    private static string ResolveBackupRoot(string reportDir)
    {
        DirectoryInfo? current = new(reportDir);

        while (current != null)
        {
            if (current.Name.Equals("D DATA BACKUP", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase))
                return current.FullName;

            current = current.Parent;
        }

        return Directory.GetParent(reportDir)?.FullName ?? reportDir;
    }

    private static void EnsureRequiredFileExists(string path, string message)
    {
        if (!File.Exists(path))
            throw new FileNotFoundException(message, path);
    }

    private static string BuildDriveSafeName(string relativePath)
    {
        return relativePath
            .Replace('\\', '_')
            .Replace('/', '_')
            .Replace(':', '_');
    }

    private static string GetMimeType(string path)
    {
        string ext = Path.GetExtension(path).ToLowerInvariant();

        return ext switch
        {
            ".txt" => "text/plain",
            ".csv" => "text/csv",
            ".json" => "application/json",
            ".html" => "text/html",
            ".pdf" => "application/pdf",
            ".zip" => "application/zip",
            ".png" => "image/png",
            ".jpg" or ".jpeg" => "image/jpeg",
            ".svg" => "image/svg+xml",
            _ => "application/octet-stream"
        };
    }

    private static string BuildLinksText(
        string folderPublicLink,
        IReadOnlyList files)
    {
        var sb = new StringBuilder();

        sb.AppendLine("TQGA GOOGLE DRIVE PUBLIC LINKS");
        sb.AppendLine("================================");
        sb.AppendLine($"Published Files: {files.Count}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Folder Link: {folderPublicLink}");
        sb.AppendLine();

        foreach (GoogleDrivePublishedFile file in files.OrderBy(x => x.RelativePath, StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase))
        {
            sb.AppendLine(file.RelativePath);
            sb.AppendLine(file.PublicLink);
            sb.AppendLine();
        }

        return sb.ToString().TrimEnd();
    }

    private static void TryOpenInBrowser(string url)
    {
        Process.Start(new ProcessStartInfo
        {
            FileName = url,
            UseShellExecute = true
        });
    }
}

public sealed class GoogleDrivePublishResult
{
    public bool Success { get; init; }
    public string ReportDirectory { get; init; } = string.Empty;
    public string GoogleConfigRoot { get; init; } = string.Empty;
    public string GoogleDriveFolderId { get; init; } = string.Empty;
    public string GoogleDriveFolderLink { get; init; } = string.Empty;
    public int PublishedCount { get; init; }
    public string LinksOutputPath { get; init; } = string.Empty;
    public string FullLinksText { get; init; } = string.Empty;
    public IReadOnlyList PublishedFiles { get; init; } = Array.Empty();
}

public sealed class GoogleDrivePublishedFile
{
    public string LocalPath { get; init; } = string.Empty;
    public string RelativePath { get; init; } = string.Empty;
    public string DriveFileId { get; init; } = string.Empty;
    public string DriveFileName { get; init; } = string.Empty;
    public string PublicLink { get; init; } = string.Empty;
}

public sealed class GoogleDrivePublishSettings
{
    public string GoogleDriveFolderIdOrLink { get; init; } = string.Empty;
    public string ApplicationName { get; init; } = "TQGA Google Publish";
    public bool MakeAnyoneWithLinkViewer { get; init; } = true;
    public bool DeleteExistingFilesInFolderBeforeUpload { get; init; } = false;
}

 F I L E :   D : \ D   D A T A   B A C K U P \ A R I F 5 \ T Q G A \ T Q G A . A p p l i c a t i o n \ S e r v i c e s \ L o c a l S t a t i c S i t e H o s t . c s

 = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = 
 
 using System.Net;
using System.Text;

namespace TQGA.Application.Services;

public sealed class LocalStaticSiteHost : IDisposable
{
    private readonly object _sync = new();
    private HttpListener? _listener;
    private CancellationTokenSource? _cts;
    private Task? _listenLoopTask;
    private string _siteRoot = string.Empty;
    private int _port;

    public int Port => _port;
    public bool IsRunning => _listener != null && _listener.IsListening;

    public string Start(string siteRoot, int preferredPort = 8787)
    {
        if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(siteRoot))
            throw new ArgumentException("Site root is required.", nameof(siteRoot));

        if (!Directory.Exists(siteRoot))
            throw new DirectoryNotFoundException($"Site root not found: {siteRoot}");

        lock (_sync)
        {
            if (IsRunning && string.Equals(_siteRoot, siteRoot, StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase))
                return BuildBaseUrl(_port);

            StopInternal();

            _siteRoot = siteRoot;
            _port = FindAvailablePort(preferredPort);

            _listener = new HttpListener();
            _listener.Prefixes.Add($"http://localhost:{_port}/");
            _listener.Start();

            _cts = new CancellationTokenSource();
            _listenLoopTask = Task.Run(() => ListenLoopAsync(_cts.Token));

            return BuildBaseUrl(_port);
        }
    }

    public void Stop()
    {
        lock (_sync)
        {
            StopInternal();
        }
    }

    private void StopInternal()
    {
        try
        {
            _cts?.Cancel();
        }
        catch
        {
        }

        try
        {
            if (_listener != null && _listener.IsListening)
                _listener.Stop();
        }
        catch
        {
        }

        try
        {
            _listener?.Close();
        }
        catch
        {
        }

        _listener = null;
        _cts?.Dispose();
        _cts = null;
        _listenLoopTask = null;
        _siteRoot = string.Empty;
        _port = 0;
    }

    private async Task ListenLoopAsync(CancellationToken ct)
    {
        while (!ct.IsCancellationRequested && _listener != null)
        {
            HttpListenerContext? context = null;

            try
            {
                context = await _listener.GetContextAsync();
            }
            catch
            {
                if (ct.IsCancellationRequested)
                    break;

                if (_listener == null || !_listener.IsListening)
                    break;
            }

            if (context == null)
                continue;

            _ = Task.Run(() => HandleRequestAsync(context, ct), ct);
        }
    }

    private async Task HandleRequestAsync(HttpListenerContext context, CancellationToken ct)
    {
        try
        {
            string relativePath = context.Request.Url?.AbsolutePath ?? "/";
            if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(relativePath) || relativePath == "/")
                relativePath = "/index.html";

            relativePath = Uri.UnescapeDataString(relativePath.TrimStart('/'));
            relativePath = relativePath.Replace('/', Path.DirectorySeparatorChar);

            string fullPath = Path.GetFullPath(Path.Combine(_siteRoot, relativePath));
            string siteRootFull = Path.GetFullPath(_siteRoot);

            if (!fullPath.StartsWith(siteRootFull, StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase))
            {
                context.Response.StatusCode = 403;
                await WriteTextAsync(context.Response, "Forbidden", "text/plain", ct);
                return;
            }

            if (Directory.Exists(fullPath))
            {
                string indexPath = Path.Combine(fullPath, "index.html");
                if (File.Exists(indexPath))
                    fullPath = indexPath;
            }

            if (!File.Exists(fullPath))
            {
                context.Response.StatusCode = 404;
                await WriteTextAsync(context.Response, "Not Found", "text/plain", ct);
                return;
            }

            byte[] bytes = await File.ReadAllBytesAsync(fullPath, ct);
            context.Response.StatusCode = 200;
            context.Response.ContentType = GetContentType(fullPath);
            context.Response.ContentLength64 = bytes.LongLength;
            context.Response.AddHeader("Cache-Control", "no-cache, no-store, must-revalidate");
            await context.Response.OutputStream.WriteAsync(bytes, 0, bytes.Length, ct);
            context.Response.OutputStream.Close();
        }
        catch
        {
            try
            {
                context.Response.StatusCode = 500;
                await WriteTextAsync(context.Response, "Internal Server Error", "text/plain", ct);
            }
            catch
            {
            }
        }
    }

    private static async Task WriteTextAsync(
        HttpListenerResponse response,
        string text,
        string contentType,
        CancellationToken ct)
    {
        byte[] bytes = Encoding.UTF8.GetBytes(text);
        response.ContentType = contentType;
        response.ContentLength64 = bytes.LongLength;
        await response.OutputStream.WriteAsync(bytes, 0, bytes.Length, ct);
        response.OutputStream.Close();
    }

    private static int FindAvailablePort(int preferredPort)
    {
        for (int port = preferredPort; port < preferredPort + 50; port++)
        {
            try
            {
                using var listener = new HttpListener();
                listener.Prefixes.Add($"http://localhost:{port}/");
                listener.Start();
                listener.Stop();
                return port;
            }
            catch
            {
                // try next port
            }
        }

        throw new InvalidOperationException("Could not find an available localhost port.");
    }

    private static string BuildBaseUrl(int port)
    {
        return $"http://localhost:{port}/";
    }

    private static string GetContentType(string path)
    {
        string ext = Path.GetExtension(path).ToLowerInvariant();

        return ext switch
        {
            ".html" => "text/html; charset=utf-8",
            ".txt" => "text/plain; charset=utf-8",
            ".csv" => "text/csv; charset=utf-8",
            ".json" => "application/json; charset=utf-8",
            ".css" => "text/css; charset=utf-8",
            ".js" => "application/javascript; charset=utf-8",
            ".png" => "image/png",
            ".jpg" or ".jpeg" => "image/jpeg",
            ".webp" => "image/webp",
            ".svg" => "image/svg+xml",
            ".pdf" => "application/pdf",
            ".zip" => "application/zip",
            _ => "application/octet-stream"
        };
    }

    public void Dispose()
    {
        Stop();
    }
}

 = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = 
 
 using System.Globalization;

namespace TQGA.Application.Services;

public sealed class MiniReportSamplingService
{
    public IEnumerable<(DateTime time, decimal value)> DownSample(
        IReadOnlyDictionary source,
        TimeSpan interval)
    {
        if (source == null || source.Count == 0)
            yield break;

        var ordered = source.OrderBy(x => x.Key).ToList();

        var nextCut = ordered[0].Key;

        foreach (var point in ordered)
        {
            if (point.Key < nextCut)
                continue;

            yield return (point.Key, point.Value);

            nextCut = point.Key + interval;
        }
    }
}

 = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = 
 
 using System.Globalization;
using System.Text;
using TQGA.Application.Paths;

namespace TQGA.Application.Services;

public sealed class PortfolioDrawdownReportService
{
    private readonly MiniReportSamplingService _mini;

    public PortfolioDrawdownReportService(MiniReportSamplingService mini)
    {
        _mini = mini;
    }

    public void Generate(IReadOnlyDictionary timeline)
    {
        Directory.CreateDirectory(DataPaths.Reports);

        var ts = DateTime.UtcNow.ToString("yyyyMMdd_HHmmss");

        var fullPath = Path.Combine(
            DataPaths.Reports,
            $"REPORT_10_DRAWDOWN_{ts}.csv");

        var miniPath = Path.Combine(
            DataPaths.Reports,
            $"REPORT_10_MINI_DRAWDOWN_{ts}.csv");

        var ordered = timeline?
            .OrderBy(x => x.Key)
            .ToList() ?? new List>();

        if (ordered.Count == 0)
        {
            File.WriteAllText(
                fullPath,
                "REPORT 10 — PORTFOLIO DRAWDOWN ENGINE" + Environment.NewLine +
                "=====================================" + Environment.NewLine +
                "NO DATA: PortfolioEquityTimeline is empty." + Environment.NewLine);

            File.WriteAllText(
                miniPath,
                "REPORT 10 — MINI DRAWDOWN" + Environment.NewLine +
                "===================================" + Environment.NewLine +
                "NO DATA: PortfolioEquityTimeline is empty." + Environment.NewLine);

            return;
        }

        decimal peak = decimal.MinValue;
        decimal maxDd = 0m;

        DateTime? ddStart = null;
        TimeSpan longestDd = TimeSpan.Zero;

        var rows = new List<(DateTime time, decimal equity, decimal dd)>();

        foreach (var p in ordered)
        {
            var equity = p.Value;

            if (equity > peak)
            {
                peak = equity;

                if (ddStart != null)
                {
                    var duration = p.Key - ddStart.Value;

                    if (duration > longestDd)
                        longestDd = duration;

                    ddStart = null;
                }
            }

            var dd = peak == 0m ? 0m : (equity - peak) / peak * 100m;

            if (dd < 0m && ddStart == null)
                ddStart = p.Key;

            if (dd < maxDd)
                maxDd = dd;

            rows.Add((p.Key, equity, dd));
        }

        var currentEquity = ordered[^1].Value;

        var currentDd = peak == 0m
            ? 0m
            : (currentEquity - peak) / peak * 100m;

        var full = new StringBuilder();

        full.AppendLine("REPORT 10 — PORTFOLIO DRAWDOWN ENGINE");
        full.AppendLine("=====================================");
        full.AppendLine();
        full.AppendLine($"Peak Equity        : {peak:F2}");
        full.AppendLine($"Current Equity     : {currentEquity:F2}");
        full.AppendLine($"Current Drawdown   : {currentDd:F2} %");
        full.AppendLine($"Max Drawdown       : {maxDd:F2} %");
        full.AppendLine($"Longest Drawdown   : {longestDd.TotalDays:F1} days");
        full.AppendLine();
        full.AppendLine("Time,Equity,Drawdown%");

        foreach (var r in rows)
            full.AppendLine($"{r.time:yyyy-MM-dd HH:mm},{r.equity:F2},{r.dd:F2}");

        File.WriteAllText(fullPath, full.ToString());

        var miniTimeline = rows.ToDictionary(x => x.time, x => x.dd);
        var mini = _mini.DownSample(miniTimeline, TimeSpan.FromDays(7));

        var miniSb = new StringBuilder();

        miniSb.AppendLine("REPORT 10 — MINI DRAWDOWN");
        miniSb.AppendLine("===================================");
        miniSb.AppendLine("Time,Drawdown%");

        foreach (var p in mini)
            miniSb.AppendLine($"{p.time:yyyy-MM-dd HH:mm},{p.value.ToString("F2", CultureInfo.InvariantCulture)}");

        File.WriteAllText(miniPath, miniSb.ToString());
    }
}

 = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = 
 
 using System.Text;
using TQGA.Application.Accounting;

namespace TQGA.Application.Services;

public sealed class QuickAuditReportService
{
    public string Build(
        TradeLedger ledger,
        EquityCurve equity)
    {
        var points = equity.Points;

        if (points.Count == 0)
            return "NO DATA";

        var start = points.First().Value;
        var end = points.Last().Value;

        var pnl = end - start;
        var ret = start == 0 ? 0 : pnl / start * 100m;

        var maxDd = CalculateMaxDrawdown(points);

        var trades = ledger.Trades.Where(t => t.IsClosed).ToList();

        var wins = trades.Count(t => t.RealizedPnL > 0);
        var losses = trades.Count(t => t.RealizedPnL <= 0);

        var winRate = trades.Count == 0
            ? 0
            : (decimal)wins / trades.Count * 100m;

        var avgWin = trades.Where(t => t.RealizedPnL > 0)
                           .Select(t => t.RealizedPnL)
                           .DefaultIfEmpty(0)
                           .Average();

        var avgLoss = trades.Where(t => t.RealizedPnL <= 0)
                            .Select(t => t.RealizedPnL)
                            .DefaultIfEmpty(0)
                            .Average();

        var pf = avgLoss == 0 ? 0 : Math.Abs(avgWin / avgLoss);

        var sb = new StringBuilder();

        sb.AppendLine("QUICK AUDIT");
        sb.AppendLine("===========");
        sb.AppendLine($"Start Equity : {start:F2}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Final Equity : {end:F2}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Net PnL      : {pnl:F2}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Return %     : {ret:F2}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Max DD %     : {maxDd:F2}");
        sb.AppendLine();
        sb.AppendLine($"Trades       : {trades.Count}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Winrate %    : {winRate:F2}");
        sb.AppendLine($"ProfitFactor : {pf:F2}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Avg Win      : {avgWin:F2}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Avg Loss     : {avgLoss:F2}");
        sb.AppendLine();
        sb.AppendLine($"Timeline Pts : {points.Count}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Start Time   : {points.First().Time}");
        sb.AppendLine($"End Time     : {points.Last().Time}");

        return sb.ToString();
    }

    private static decimal CalculateMaxDrawdown(
        IReadOnlyList<(DateTime Time, decimal Value)> pts)
    {
        decimal peak = decimal.MinValue;
        decimal maxDd = 0;

        foreach (var p in pts)
        {
            if (p.Value > peak)
                peak = p.Value;

            if (peak == 0) continue;

            var dd = (peak - p.Value) / peak * 100m;

            if (dd > maxDd)
                maxDd = dd;
        }

        return maxDd;
    }
}
