 = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = 
 
 using System;
using System.IO;
using System.Linq;
using System.Text;
using TQGA.Application.Backtesting;
using TQGA.Application.Paths;

namespace TQGA.Application.Services;

public sealed class ReconciliationReportService
{
    public void Generate(PortfolioBacktestResult result)
    {
        ArgumentNullException.ThrowIfNull(result);

        var sb = new StringBuilder();

        decimal start = 100000m;
        decimal end = result.PortfolioEquityTimeline.Count > 0
            ? result.PortfolioEquityTimeline.Values.Last()
            : start;

        decimal delta = end - start;
        decimal strategySum = result.StrategyPnL.Values.Sum();
        decimal symbolSum = result.SymbolPnL.Values.Sum();
        decimal diffStrategy = delta - strategySum;
        decimal diffSymbol = delta - symbolSum;

        var runnerCandidateMix = result.MarketAllocationWeights
            ?? new System.Collections.Generic.Dictionary(StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase);

        var canonicalDeployable = result.CanonicalCioPostGatingWeights
            ?? new System.Collections.Generic.Dictionary(StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase);

        decimal runnerCandidateMixSum = runnerCandidateMix.Values.Sum();
        decimal canonicalDeployableSum = canonicalDeployable.Values.Sum();
        decimal cashWeight = result.CashAllocationWeight;
        decimal grossDeployablePlusCash = canonicalDeployableSum + cashWeight;

        sb.AppendLine("REPORT 31 â€” RECONCILIATION");
        sb.AppendLine("===========================");
        sb.AppendLine();

        sb.AppendLine("SECTION A â€” ECONOMIC RECONCILIATION");
        sb.AppendLine("-----------------------------------");
        sb.AppendLine($"Start Equity     : {start:F2}");
        sb.AppendLine($"End Equity       : {end:F2}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Portfolio Delta  : {delta:F2}");
        sb.AppendLine();
        sb.AppendLine($"Strategy Sum     : {strategySum:F2}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Symbol Sum       : {symbolSum:F2}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Î” vs Strategy    : {diffStrategy:F2}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Î” vs Symbol      : {diffSymbol:F2}");
        sb.AppendLine();

        bool economicOk = Math.Abs(diffStrategy) < 1m && Math.Abs(diffSymbol) < 1m;
        sb.AppendLine(economicOk
            ? "ECONOMIC STATUS: PASS"
            : "ECONOMIC STATUS: FAIL â€” ECONOMIC INCONSISTENCY");
        sb.AppendLine();

        sb.AppendLine("SECTION B â€” ALLOCATION SEMANTICS SNAPSHOT");
        sb.AppendLine("-----------------------------------------");
        sb.AppendLine("Runner Candidate Mix Count          : " + runnerCandidateMix.Count);
        sb.AppendLine($"Runner Candidate Mix Sum            : {runnerCandidateMixSum:P2}");
        sb.AppendLine("Canonical Deployable Count          : " + canonicalDeployable.Count);
        sb.AppendLine($"Canonical Deployable Sum            : {canonicalDeployableSum:P2}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Preserved Cash (gross)             : {cashWeight:P2}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Gross Deployable + Cash            : {grossDeployablePlusCash:P2}");
        sb.AppendLine();

        sb.AppendLine("SECTION C â€” INTERPRETATION");
        sb.AppendLine("--------------------------");
        sb.AppendLine("Runner candidate mix is a relative sleeve mix only.");
        sb.AppendLine("Canonical deployable allocation plus preserved cash is the gross-capital truth.");
        sb.AppendLine("Do NOT add runner candidate mix sum to preserved cash.");
        sb.AppendLine();

        bool semanticOk = Math.Abs(grossDeployablePlusCash - 1m) < 0.0001m;

        if (runnerCandidateMix.Count > 0 && Math.Abs(runnerCandidateMixSum - 1m) < 0.0001m && cashWeight > 0m)
        {
            sb.AppendLine("NOTE: Candidate mix sums to 100% because it is an internal sleeve distribution, not gross capital deployment.");
        }

        if (!semanticOk)
        {
            sb.AppendLine("WARNING: Canonical deployable allocation plus preserved cash does not reconcile to 100.00% gross capital.");
        }
        else
        {
            sb.AppendLine("ALLOCATION SEMANTICS STATUS: PASS");
        }

        sb.AppendLine();
        sb.AppendLine("SECTION D â€” DEPLOYABLE CIO SNAPSHOT");
        sb.AppendLine("-----------------------------------");

        if (canonicalDeployable.Count == 0)
        {
            sb.AppendLine("NO CANONICAL DEPLOYABLE MARKETS.");
        }
        else
        {
            foreach (var kv in canonicalDeployable.OrderByDescending(x => x.Value))
                sb.AppendLine($"{kv.Key}   {kv.Value:P2}");
        }

        sb.AppendLine();

        Directory.CreateDirectory(DataPaths.Reports);

        File.WriteAllText(
            Path.Combine(
                DataPaths.Reports,
                $"REPORT_31_RECON_{DateTime.UtcNow:yyyyMMdd_HHmmss}.txt"),
            sb.ToString());
    }
}

 = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = 
 
 using System.Text;
using TQGA.Application.Backtesting;
using TQGA.Application.Paths;

namespace TQGA.Application.Services;

public sealed class Report19EdgeDeathMapReportService
{
    public void GenerateAndWrite(
        PortfolioBacktestResult result,
        DateTime runUtc,
        IReadOnlyDictionary fitnessSnapshots,
        IReadOnlyCollection allowedStrategyIds)
    {
        ArgumentNullException.ThrowIfNull(result);
        ArgumentNullException.ThrowIfNull(fitnessSnapshots);
        ArgumentNullException.ThrowIfNull(allowedStrategyIds);

        Directory.CreateDirectory(DataPaths.Reports);

        string stamp = runUtc.ToString("yyyyMMdd_HHmmss");
        string path = Path.Combine(
            DataPaths.Reports,
            $"REPORT_19_EDGE_DEATH_MAP_{stamp}.txt");

        var sb = new StringBuilder();

        var selectedMarkets = result.SelectedMarkets?
            .Where(x => !string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(x))
            .Distinct(StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase)
            .OrderBy(x => x, StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase)
            .ToList()
            ?? new List();

        var rejectionMap = result.MarketSelectionRejections?
            .Where(kv => !string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(kv.Key))
            .GroupBy(kv => kv.Key, StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase)
            .ToDictionary(
                g => g.Key,
                g => g.Last().Value ?? string.Empty,
                StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase)
            ?? new Dictionary(StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase);

        var candidateUniverse = selectedMarkets
            .Concat(rejectionMap.Keys)
            .Where(x => !string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(x))
            .Distinct(StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase)
            .OrderBy(x => x, StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase)
            .ToList();

        var canonicalDeployable = result.CanonicalCioPostGatingWeights?
            .Where(kv => !string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(kv.Key) && kv.Value > 0m)
            .ToDictionary(kv => kv.Key, kv => kv.Value, StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase)
            ?? new Dictionary(StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase);

        var runnerCandidateMix = result.MarketAllocationWeights?
            .Where(kv => !string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(kv.Key) && kv.Value > 0m)
            .ToDictionary(kv => kv.Key, kv => kv.Value, StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase)
            ?? new Dictionary(StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase);

        int rawCandidateCount = candidateUniverse.Count;
        int rejectedCount = rejectionMap.Count;
        int selectedAfterWaveBCount = selectedMarkets.Count;
        int deployableCount = canonicalDeployable.Count;
        decimal preservedCash = result.CashAllocationWeight;

        int totalStrategies = fitnessSnapshots.Count;
        int allowedStrategies = allowedStrategyIds.Count;
        int rejectedStrategies = Math.Max(0, totalStrategies - allowedStrategies);
        int scarcityOverrideCount = fitnessSnapshots.Values.Count(x =>
            !string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(x.GateReason) &&
            x.GateReason.Contains("SCARCITY_OVERRIDE", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase));

        int lostInCanonicalNormalization = selectedMarkets.Count(x =>
            !canonicalDeployable.ContainsKey(x));

        var rejectionReasonCounts = BuildRejectionReasonCounts(rejectionMap);
        var strategyGateReasonCounts = BuildStrategyGateReasonCounts(fitnessSnapshots);
        string dominantKillZone = DetermineDominantKillZone(
            rejectionReasonCounts,
            strategyGateReasonCounts,
            selectedAfterWaveBCount,
            deployableCount,
            preservedCash);

        sb.AppendLine("REPORT 19 — EDGE DEATH MAP");
        sb.AppendLine("==========================");
        sb.AppendLine();
        sb.AppendLine("PURPOSE");
        sb.AppendLine("-------");
        sb.AppendLine("Institutional funnel audit of where candidate breadth is dying.");
        sb.AppendLine("This report is designed to explain why final deployable alpha breadth is narrow.");
        sb.AppendLine();
        sb.AppendLine("RUN CONTEXT");
        sb.AppendLine("-----------");
        sb.AppendLine($"Run Timestamp (UTC)              : {runUtc:yyyy-MM-dd HH:mm:ss}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Raw Candidate Universe           : {rawCandidateCount}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Rejected Before Final Deploy     : {rejectedCount}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Selected After Wave B            : {selectedAfterWaveBCount}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Runner Candidate Mix Count       : {runnerCandidateMix.Count}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Canonical Deployable Count       : {deployableCount}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Preserved Cash Weight            : {preservedCash:P2}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Total Strategies Evaluated       : {totalStrategies}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Strategies Allowed               : {allowedStrategies}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Strategies Rejected              : {rejectedStrategies}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Scarcity Override Count          : {scarcityOverrideCount}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Lost In Canonical Normalization  : {lostInCanonicalNormalization}");
        sb.AppendLine();

        sb.AppendLine("SECTION A — CANDIDATE FUNNEL");
        sb.AppendLine("----------------------------");
        sb.AppendLine($"1. Raw Candidate Universe             : {rawCandidateCount}");
        sb.AppendLine($"2. Markets Rejected (reason present)  : {rejectedCount}");
        sb.AppendLine($"3. Markets Selected After Wave B      : {selectedAfterWaveBCount}");
        sb.AppendLine($"4. Runner Candidate Mix Count         : {runnerCandidateMix.Count}");
        sb.AppendLine($"5. Canonical Deployable Markets       : {deployableCount}");
        sb.AppendLine($"6. Preserved Cash                     : {preservedCash:P2}");
        sb.AppendLine();

        sb.AppendLine("SECTION B — MARKET REJECTION REASON COUNTS");
        sb.AppendLine("------------------------------------------");
        if (rejectionReasonCounts.Count == 0)
        {
            sb.AppendLine("NO MARKET REJECTION DATA");
        }
        else
        {
            foreach (var kv in rejectionReasonCounts.OrderByDescending(x => x.Value).ThenBy(x => x.Key, StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase))
                sb.AppendLine($"{kv.Key,-36} {kv.Value,6}");
        }
        sb.AppendLine();

        sb.AppendLine("SECTION C — STRATEGY GATE REASON COUNTS");
        sb.AppendLine("---------------------------------------");
        if (strategyGateReasonCounts.Count == 0)
        {
            sb.AppendLine("NO STRATEGY GATE DATA");
        }
        else
        {
            foreach (var kv in strategyGateReasonCounts.OrderByDescending(x => x.Value).ThenBy(x => x.Key, StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase))
                sb.AppendLine($"{kv.Key,-36} {kv.Value,6}");
        }
        sb.AppendLine();

        sb.AppendLine("SECTION D — NEAR MISS MARKETS");
        sb.AppendLine("-----------------------------");
        WriteNearMissMarkets(sb, result, rejectionMap);
        sb.AppendLine();

        sb.AppendLine("SECTION E — STRATEGY FITNESS SNAPSHOT");
        sb.AppendLine("-------------------------------------");
        if (fitnessSnapshots.Count == 0)
        {
            sb.AppendLine("NO FITNESS SNAPSHOT DATA");
        }
        else
        {
            sb.AppendLine("StrId | StrategyCode | Allowed | Trades | Exits | FitnessScore | PnL | GateReason");
            sb.AppendLine("------+--------------+---------+--------+-------+--------------+-----+-----------");
            foreach (var row in fitnessSnapshots.Values.OrderBy(x => x.StrategyId))
            {
                sb.AppendLine(
                    $"{row.StrategyId,5} | " +
                    $"{TrimTo(row.StrategyCode, 12),-12} | " +
                    $"{(row.Allowed ? "YES" : "NO "),-7} | " +
                    $"{row.Trades,6} | " +
                    $"{row.Exits,5} | " +
                    $"{row.FitnessScore,12:F4} | " +
                    $"{row.PnL,7:F2} | " +
                    $"{row.GateReason}");
            }
        }
        sb.AppendLine();

        sb.AppendLine("SECTION F — FINAL DEPLOYABLE ALLOCATION");
        sb.AppendLine("---------------------------------------");
        if (canonicalDeployable.Count == 0)
        {
            sb.AppendLine("NO CANONICAL DEPLOYABLE MARKETS");
        }
        else
        {
            foreach (var kv in canonicalDeployable.OrderByDescending(x => x.Value))
                sb.AppendLine($"{kv.Key,-24} {kv.Value,10:P2}");
        }
        sb.AppendLine($"CASH{' ',20} {preservedCash,10:P2}");
        sb.AppendLine();

        sb.AppendLine("SECTION G — BREADTH KILL VERDICT");
        sb.AppendLine("--------------------------------");
        sb.AppendLine($"Dominant Kill Zone : {dominantKillZone}");
        sb.AppendLine(BuildVerdictNarrative(
            dominantKillZone,
            rawCandidateCount,
            selectedAfterWaveBCount,
            deployableCount,
            preservedCash,
            scarcityOverrideCount,
            lostInCanonicalNormalization));
        sb.AppendLine();

        sb.AppendLine("SECTION H — OPERATOR INTERPRETATION");
        sb.AppendLine("-----------------------------------");
        sb.AppendLine("This report should be used before changing thresholds.");
        sb.AppendLine("Do not loosen gates blindly.");
        sb.AppendLine("First identify where breadth dies:");
        sb.AppendLine("1) market selection / Wave B");
        sb.AppendLine("2) strategy fitness gating");
        sb.AppendLine("3) canonical CIO deployment");
        sb.AppendLine("4) preserved-cash regime defense");
        sb.AppendLine();

        File.WriteAllText(path, sb.ToString());
    }

    private static Dictionary BuildRejectionReasonCounts(
        IReadOnlyDictionary rejectionMap)
    {
        var counts = new Dictionary(StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase);

        foreach (var kv in rejectionMap)
        {
            string bucket = NormalizeMarketRejectionReason(kv.Value);
            if (counts.TryGetValue(bucket, out int current))
                counts[bucket] = current + 1;
            else
                counts[bucket] = 1;
        }

        return counts;
    }

    private static Dictionary BuildStrategyGateReasonCounts(
        IReadOnlyDictionary fitnessSnapshots)
    {
        var counts = new Dictionary(StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase);

        foreach (var row in fitnessSnapshots.Values)
        {
            string reason = string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(row.GateReason)
                ? (row.Allowed ? "ALLOWED" : "UNKNOWN")
                : row.GateReason.Trim();

            if (counts.TryGetValue(reason, out int current))
                counts[reason] = current + 1;
            else
                counts[reason] = 1;
        }

        return counts;
    }

    private static string NormalizeMarketRejectionReason(string? reason)
    {
        string value = reason?.Trim() ?? string.Empty;
        if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(value))
            return "UNKNOWN";

        if (value.Contains("dispersion", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase))
            return "DispersionGuard";

        if (value.Contains("per-symbol", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase) ||
            value.Contains("per symbol", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase) ||
            value.Contains("symbol cap", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase))
            return "PerSymbolCap";

        if (value.Contains("top-n", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase) ||
            value.Contains("top n", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase) ||
            value.Contains("overflow", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase))
            return "TopNOverflow";

        if (value.Contains("threshold", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase) ||
            value.Contains("below", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase) ||
            value.Contains("score", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase))
            return "BelowMinScore";

        if (value.Contains("pre-trade", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase) ||
            value.Contains("pretrade", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase))
            return "PreTradeSelection";

        if (value.Contains("duplicate", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase))
            return "DuplicateFiltered";

        return value;
    }

    private static string DetermineDominantKillZone(
        IReadOnlyDictionary marketRejectionReasons,
        IReadOnlyDictionary strategyGateReasons,
        int selectedAfterWaveBCount,
        int deployableCount,
        decimal preservedCash)
    {
        int marketRejectTotal = marketRejectionReasons.Values.Sum();
        int strategyRejectTotal = strategyGateReasons
            .Where(kv => !kv.Key.Equals("ALLOWED", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase) &&
                         !kv.Key.Contains("SCARCITY_OVERRIDE", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase))
            .Sum(kv => kv.Value);

        if (selectedAfterWaveBCount <= 1 && marketRejectTotal >= strategyRejectTotal)
            return "WAVE_B_SELECTION";

        if (strategyRejectTotal > marketRejectTotal && strategyRejectTotal > 0)
            return "STRATEGY_FITNESS_GATING";

        if (deployableCount < selectedAfterWaveBCount)
            return "CANONICAL_CIO_DEPLOYMENT";

        if (preservedCash >= 0.50m)
            return "REGIME_CASH_PRESERVATION";

        return "MIXED_OR_UNCLEAR";
    }

    private static void WriteNearMissMarkets(
        StringBuilder sb,
        PortfolioBacktestResult result,
        IReadOnlyDictionary rejectionMap)
    {
        var symbolTfPnl = result.SymbolTimeframePnL
            ?? new Dictionary(StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase);

        var rows = rejectionMap
            .Select(kv => new
            {
                Market = kv.Key,
                Reason = kv.Value,
                PnL = symbolTfPnl.TryGetValue(kv.Key, out decimal pnl) ? pnl : 0m
            })
            .OrderByDescending(x => x.PnL)
            .ThenBy(x => x.Market, StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase)
            .Take(10)
            .ToList();

        if (rows.Count == 0)
        {
            sb.AppendLine("NO NEAR MISS MARKET DATA");
            return;
        }

        sb.AppendLine("Market                    PnL         Reason");
        sb.AppendLine("------------------------  ----------  --------------------------------");
        foreach (var row in rows)
        {
            sb.AppendLine($"{TrimTo(row.Market, 24),-24}  {row.PnL,10:F2}  {row.Reason}");
        }
    }

    private static string BuildVerdictNarrative(
        string dominantKillZone,
        int rawCandidateCount,
        int selectedAfterWaveBCount,
        int deployableCount,
        decimal preservedCash,
        int scarcityOverrideCount,
        int lostInCanonicalNormalization)
    {
        return dominantKillZone switch
        {
            "WAVE_B_SELECTION" =>
                $"Breadth is dying primarily before or during Wave B. " +
                $"Raw candidates = {rawCandidateCount}, selected after Wave B = {selectedAfterWaveBCount}. " +
                $"This suggests market-level selection pressure is the main bottleneck.",

            "STRATEGY_FITNESS_GATING" =>
                $"Breadth is dying primarily at strategy fitness gating. " +
                $"Markets are surviving far enough to be candidates, but too many strategy sleeves are rejected before robust deployment.",

            "CANONICAL_CIO_DEPLOYMENT" =>
                $"Breadth is dying between runner selection and final deployable CIO normalization. " +
                $"Selected after Wave B = {selectedAfterWaveBCount}, final deployable = {deployableCount}, " +
                $"lost in canonical normalization = {lostInCanonicalNormalization}.",

            "REGIME_CASH_PRESERVATION" =>
                $"The main visible constraint is defensive capital preservation. " +
                $"Preserved cash = {preservedCash:P2}. " +
                $"Scarcity override count = {scarcityOverrideCount}. " +
                $"The platform is choosing honesty over forced deployment.",

            _ =>
                $"No single bottleneck dominates cleanly. " +
                $"This run likely reflects mixed pressure across Wave B, strategy gating, and final deployable normalization."
        };
    }

    private static string TrimTo(string? text, int maxLen)
    {
        string value = text ?? string.Empty;
        if (value.Length <= maxLen)
            return value;

        if (maxLen <= 3)
            return value[..maxLen];

        return value[..(maxLen - 3)] + "...";
    }
}

 using System.Text;
using TQGA.Application.Backtesting;
using TQGA.Application.Paths;

namespace TQGA.Application.Services;

public sealed class Report20AlphaDecayS05DependencyAuditService
{
    public void GenerateAndWrite(
        PortfolioBacktestResult result,
        DateTime runUtc,
        IReadOnlyDictionary fitnessSnapshots)
    {
        ArgumentNullException.ThrowIfNull(result);
        ArgumentNullException.ThrowIfNull(fitnessSnapshots);

        Directory.CreateDirectory(DataPaths.Reports);

        string stamp = runUtc.ToString("yyyyMMdd_HHmmss");
        string path = Path.Combine(
            DataPaths.Reports,
            $"REPORT_20_ALPHA_DECAY_S05_DEPENDENCY_AUDIT_{stamp}.txt");

        var sb = new StringBuilder();

        var timeline = (result.PortfolioEquityTimeline ?? new Dictionary())
            .OrderBy(x => x.Key)
            .ToList();

        var strategyPnl = result.StrategyPnL ?? new Dictionary();
        var symbolTfPnl = result.SymbolTimeframePnL ?? new Dictionary(StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase);
        var strategySymbolTfPnl = result.StrategySymbolTimeframePnL ?? new Dictionary(StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase);
        var selectedMarkets = result.SelectedMarkets ?? new List();
        var runnerMix = result.MarketAllocationWeights ?? new Dictionary(StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase);
        var canonical = result.CanonicalCioPostGatingWeights ?? new Dictionary(StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase);

        decimal totalStrategyPnl = strategyPnl.Values.Sum();
        decimal totalSymbolTfPnl = symbolTfPnl.Values.Sum();

        var dominantStrategy = strategyPnl
            .OrderByDescending(x => x.Value)
            .FirstOrDefault();

        int dominantStrategyId = dominantStrategy.Key;
        decimal dominantStrategyPnl = dominantStrategy.Value;

        decimal dominantStrategyDependencyRatio =
            totalStrategyPnl == 0m ? 0m : dominantStrategyPnl / totalStrategyPnl;

        decimal top1SymbolTfPnl = symbolTfPnl.Count == 0 ? 0m : symbolTfPnl.Values.Max();
        decimal top2SymbolTfPnl = symbolTfPnl
            .OrderByDescending(x => x.Value)
            .Take(2)
            .Sum(x => x.Value);

        decimal top1SymbolTfDependencyRatio =
            totalSymbolTfPnl == 0m ? 0m : top1SymbolTfPnl / totalSymbolTfPnl;

        decimal top2SymbolTfDependencyRatio =
            totalSymbolTfPnl == 0m ? 0m : top2SymbolTfPnl / totalSymbolTfPnl;

        decimal earlyHalfReturn = 0m;
        decimal lateHalfReturn = 0m;
        decimal decayDelta = 0m;

        if (timeline.Count >= 4)
        {
            int half = timeline.Count / 2;
            var early = timeline.Take(half).ToList();
            var late = timeline.Skip(half).ToList();

            earlyHalfReturn = SegmentReturn(early);
            lateHalfReturn = SegmentReturn(late);
            decayDelta = lateHalfReturn - earlyHalfReturn;
        }

        var strategyEarlyLate = BuildStrategyEarlyLate(
            strategyPnl,
            strategySymbolTfPnl);

        var symbolTfEarlyLate = BuildSymbolTimeframeEarlyLate(
            symbolTfPnl,
            strategySymbolTfPnl);

        sb.AppendLine("REPORT 20 — ALPHA DECAY / S05 DEPENDENCY AUDIT");
        sb.AppendLine("==============================================");
        sb.AppendLine();
        sb.AppendLine("PURPOSE");
        sb.AppendLine("-------");
        sb.AppendLine("Audit edge fatigue, concentration risk, and dependence on the dominant strategy sleeve.");
        sb.AppendLine();

        sb.AppendLine("RUN CONTEXT");
        sb.AppendLine("-----------");
        sb.AppendLine($"Run Timestamp (UTC)                : {runUtc:yyyy-MM-dd HH:mm:ss}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Portfolio Timeline Points          : {timeline.Count}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Selected Markets Count             : {selectedMarkets.Count}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Runner Candidate Mix Count         : {runnerMix.Count}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Canonical Deployable Count         : {canonical.Count}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Cash Allocation Weight             : {result.CashAllocationWeight:P2}");
        sb.AppendLine();

        sb.AppendLine("PORTFOLIO ALPHA DECAY");
        sb.AppendLine("---------------------");
        sb.AppendLine($"Early Half Return                  : {earlyHalfReturn:P2}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Late Half Return                   : {lateHalfReturn:P2}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Decay Delta                        : {decayDelta:P2}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Alpha Decay Flag                   : {(lateHalfReturn < earlyHalfReturn ? "YES" : "NO")}");
        sb.AppendLine();

        sb.AppendLine("DOMINANT STRATEGY DEPENDENCY");
        sb.AppendLine("----------------------------");
        if (strategyPnl.Count == 0)
        {
            sb.AppendLine("NO STRATEGY PNL DATA");
        }
        else
        {
            string dominantStrategyCode = ResolveStrategyCode(dominantStrategyId, fitnessSnapshots);
            sb.AppendLine($"Dominant Strategy Id               : S{dominantStrategyId:00}");
            sb.AppendLine($"Dominant Strategy Code             : {dominantStrategyCode}");
            sb.AppendLine($"Dominant Strategy PnL              : {dominantStrategyPnl:F2}");
            sb.AppendLine($"Total Strategy PnL                 : {totalStrategyPnl:F2}");
            sb.AppendLine($"Dominant Strategy Dependency Ratio : {dominantStrategyDependencyRatio:P2}");
            sb.AppendLine($"S05 Dependency Flag                : {(dominantStrategyCode.Contains("EmaTrendQuantStrategy", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase) ? "YES" : "NO")}");
        }
        sb.AppendLine();

        sb.AppendLine("SYMBOL::TF CONCENTRATION");
        sb.AppendLine("------------------------");
        sb.AppendLine($"Total Symbol::TF PnL               : {totalSymbolTfPnl:F2}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Top 1 Symbol::TF Dependency Ratio  : {top1SymbolTfDependencyRatio:P2}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Top 2 Symbol::TF Dependency Ratio  : {top2SymbolTfDependencyRatio:P2}");
        sb.AppendLine();

        sb.AppendLine("STRATEGY PNL TABLE");
        sb.AppendLine("------------------");
        if (strategyPnl.Count == 0)
        {
            sb.AppendLine("NO STRATEGY PNL DATA");
        }
        else
        {
            sb.AppendLine("StrId | StrategyCode                 | PnL        | Share");
            sb.AppendLine("------+------------------------------+------------+------------");
            foreach (var kv in strategyPnl.OrderByDescending(x => x.Value))
            {
                string code = ResolveStrategyCode(kv.Key, fitnessSnapshots);
                decimal share = totalStrategyPnl == 0m ? 0m : kv.Value / totalStrategyPnl;
                sb.AppendLine($"{kv.Key,5} | {TrimTo(code, 28),-28} | {kv.Value,10:F2} | {share,10:P2}");
            }
        }
        sb.AppendLine();

        sb.AppendLine("STRATEGY EARLY/LATE SPLIT");
        sb.AppendLine("-------------------------");
        if (strategyEarlyLate.Count == 0)
        {
            sb.AppendLine("NO STRATEGY EARLY/LATE DATA");
        }
        else
        {
            sb.AppendLine("StrId | StrategyCode                 | EarlyPnL   | LatePnL    | DecayDelta | DecayFlag");
            sb.AppendLine("------+------------------------------+------------+------------+------------+----------");
            foreach (var row in strategyEarlyLate.OrderByDescending(x => x.TotalPnl))
            {
                string code = ResolveStrategyCode(row.StrategyId, fitnessSnapshots);
                sb.AppendLine(
                    $"{row.StrategyId,5} | {TrimTo(code, 28),-28} | " +
                    $"{row.EarlyPnl,10:F2} | {row.LatePnl,10:F2} | {(row.LatePnl - row.EarlyPnl),10:F2} | " +
                    $"{(row.LatePnl < row.EarlyPnl ? "YES" : "NO")}");
            }
        }
        sb.AppendLine();

        sb.AppendLine("TOP SYMBOL::TF DEPENDENCY");
        sb.AppendLine("-------------------------");
        if (symbolTfPnl.Count == 0)
        {
            sb.AppendLine("NO SYMBOL::TF PNL DATA");
        }
        else
        {
            sb.AppendLine("Rank | Symbol::TF                | PnL        | Share");
            sb.AppendLine("-----+---------------------------+------------+------------");
            int rank = 1;
            foreach (var kv in symbolTfPnl.OrderByDescending(x => x.Value).Take(20))
            {
                decimal share = totalSymbolTfPnl == 0m ? 0m : kv.Value / totalSymbolTfPnl;
                sb.AppendLine($"{rank,4} | {TrimTo(kv.Key, 25),-25} | {kv.Value,10:F2} | {share,10:P2}");
                rank++;
            }
        }
        sb.AppendLine();

        sb.AppendLine("SYMBOL::TF EARLY/LATE SPLIT");
        sb.AppendLine("---------------------------");
        if (symbolTfEarlyLate.Count == 0)
        {
            sb.AppendLine("NO SYMBOL::TF EARLY/LATE DATA");
        }
        else
        {
            sb.AppendLine("Symbol::TF                | EarlyPnL   | LatePnL    | DecayDelta | DecayFlag");
            sb.AppendLine("-------------------------+------------+------------+------------+----------");
            foreach (var row in symbolTfEarlyLate.OrderByDescending(x => x.TotalPnl).Take(20))
            {
                sb.AppendLine(
                    $"{TrimTo(row.Key, 25),-25} | {row.EarlyPnl,10:F2} | {row.LatePnl,10:F2} | {(row.LatePnl - row.EarlyPnl),10:F2} | " +
                    $"{(row.LatePnl < row.EarlyPnl ? "YES" : "NO")}");
            }
        }
        sb.AppendLine();

        sb.AppendLine("DEPENDENCY VERDICT");
        sb.AppendLine("------------------");
        sb.AppendLine(BuildVerdict(
            dominantStrategyDependencyRatio,
            top2SymbolTfDependencyRatio,
            earlyHalfReturn,
            lateHalfReturn));
        sb.AppendLine();

        sb.AppendLine("OPERATOR INTERPRETATION");
        sb.AppendLine("-----------------------");
        sb.AppendLine("Use this report before adding new strategy families.");
        sb.AppendLine("If S05 concentration is extreme and late-half weakening is visible,");
        sb.AppendLine("the next fix should target edge durability, not cosmetic breadth.");
        sb.AppendLine();

        File.WriteAllText(path, sb.ToString());
    }

    private static List BuildStrategyEarlyLate(
        IReadOnlyDictionary strategyPnl,
        IReadOnlyDictionary strategySymbolTfPnl)
    {
        var output = new List();

        if (strategyPnl.Count == 0 || strategySymbolTfPnl.Count == 0)
            return output;

        foreach (var kv in strategyPnl)
        {
            int strategyId = kv.Key;
            string prefix = $"S{strategyId:00}::";

            var rows = strategySymbolTfPnl
                .Where(x => x.Key.StartsWith(prefix, StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase))
                .OrderByDescending(x => x.Value)
                .ToList();

            if (rows.Count == 0)
            {
                output.Add(new StrategyEarlyLateRow(strategyId, 0m, 0m, kv.Value));
                continue;
            }

            int half = Math.Max(1, rows.Count / 2);
            decimal early = rows.Take(half).Sum(x => x.Value);
            decimal late = rows.Skip(half).Sum(x => x.Value);

            output.Add(new StrategyEarlyLateRow(strategyId, early, late, kv.Value));
        }

        return output;
    }

    private static List BuildSymbolTimeframeEarlyLate(
        IReadOnlyDictionary symbolTfPnl,
        IReadOnlyDictionary strategySymbolTfPnl)
    {
        var output = new List();

        if (symbolTfPnl.Count == 0)
            return output;

        foreach (var kv in symbolTfPnl)
        {
            string key = kv.Key;

            var contributingRows = strategySymbolTfPnl
                .Where(x => x.Key.EndsWith("::" + key, StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase))
                .OrderByDescending(x => x.Value)
                .ToList();

            if (contributingRows.Count == 0)
            {
                output.Add(new SymbolTfEarlyLateRow(key, 0m, 0m, kv.Value));
                continue;
            }

            int half = Math.Max(1, contributingRows.Count / 2);
            decimal early = contributingRows.Take(half).Sum(x => x.Value);
            decimal late = contributingRows.Skip(half).Sum(x => x.Value);

            output.Add(new SymbolTfEarlyLateRow(key, early, late, kv.Value));
        }

        return output;
    }

    private static decimal SegmentReturn(IReadOnlyList> points)
    {
        if (points == null || points.Count < 2)
            return 0m;

        decimal start = points.First().Value;
        decimal end = points.Last().Value;

        if (start == 0m)
            return 0m;

        return (end - start) / start;
    }

    private static string ResolveStrategyCode(
        int strategyId,
        IReadOnlyDictionary fitnessSnapshots)
    {
        if (fitnessSnapshots.TryGetValue(strategyId, out var snap) &&
            !string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(snap.StrategyCode))
        {
            return snap.StrategyCode;
        }

        return $"S{strategyId:00}";
    }

    private static string BuildVerdict(
        decimal dominantStrategyDependencyRatio,
        decimal top2SymbolTfDependencyRatio,
        decimal earlyHalfReturn,
        decimal lateHalfReturn)
    {
        bool strategyConcentrated = dominantStrategyDependencyRatio >= 0.60m;
        bool symbolConcentrated = top2SymbolTfDependencyRatio >= 0.80m;
        bool decay = lateHalfReturn < earlyHalfReturn;

        if (strategyConcentrated && symbolConcentrated && decay)
        {
            return "High concentration + visible decay. The platform is depending too heavily on one dominant sleeve and a tiny symbol::TF cluster.";
        }

        if (strategyConcentrated && decay)
        {
            return "Dominant strategy dependency is high and late-half performance is weaker. This is edge-fatigue risk even if current equity is still positive.";
        }

        if (symbolConcentrated && decay)
        {
            return "The platform is overly dependent on a tiny symbol::TF set and that cluster is weakening late in the run.";
        }

        if (decay)
        {
            return "Alpha decay is visible, but concentration is not yet extreme. Watch durability before expanding capital confidence.";
        }

        return "No severe combined dependency-decay condition detected in this run.";
    }

    private static string TrimTo(string? text, int maxLen)
    {
        string value = text ?? string.Empty;
        if (value.Length <= maxLen)
            return value;

        if (maxLen <= 3)
            return value[..maxLen];

        return value[..(maxLen - 3)] + "...";
    }

    private sealed record StrategyEarlyLateRow(
        int StrategyId,
        decimal EarlyPnl,
        decimal LatePnl,
        decimal TotalPnl);

    private sealed record SymbolTfEarlyLateRow(
        string Key,
        decimal EarlyPnl,
        decimal LatePnl,
        decimal TotalPnl);
}

 T Y P E :   . c s 
 
 S I Z E :   1 1 . 9 8   K B 
 
 L I N E S :   2 5 0 
 
 = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = 
 
 using System.Text;
using TQGA.Application.Backtesting;
using TQGA.Application.Paths;

namespace TQGA.Application.Services;

public sealed class Report21S05LateHalfFailureAuditService
{
    private const int TargetStrategyId = 5;
    private const string TargetStrategyCode = "EmaTrendQuantStrategy";

    public void GenerateAndWrite(
        PortfolioBacktestResult result,
        DateTime runUtc,
        IReadOnlyDictionary fitnessSnapshots)
    {
        ArgumentNullException.ThrowIfNull(result);
        ArgumentNullException.ThrowIfNull(fitnessSnapshots);

        Directory.CreateDirectory(DataPaths.Reports);

        string stamp = runUtc.ToString("yyyyMMdd_HHmmss");
        string path = Path.Combine(
            DataPaths.Reports,
            $"REPORT_21_S05_LATE_HALF_FAILURE_AUDIT_{stamp}.txt");

        var sb = new StringBuilder();

        var timeline = (result.PortfolioEquityTimeline ?? new Dictionary())
            .OrderBy(x => x.Key)
            .ToList();

        var strategyPnl = result.StrategyPnL ?? new Dictionary();
        var symbolTfPnl = result.SymbolTimeframePnL ?? new Dictionary(StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase);
        var strategySymbolTfPnl = result.StrategySymbolTimeframePnL ?? new Dictionary(StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase);
        var runnerMix = result.MarketAllocationWeights ?? new Dictionary(StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase);
        var canonical = result.CanonicalCioPostGatingWeights ?? new Dictionary(StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase);
        var selectedMarkets = result.SelectedMarkets ?? new List();

        decimal totalStrategyPnl = strategyPnl.Values.Sum();
        decimal totalSymbolTfPnl = symbolTfPnl.Values.Sum();

        decimal s05Pnl = strategyPnl.TryGetValue(TargetStrategyId, out var foundS05Pnl)
            ? foundS05Pnl
            : 0m;

        string s05Code = ResolveStrategyCode(TargetStrategyId, fitnessSnapshots);

        decimal s05DependencyRatio =
            totalStrategyPnl == 0m ? 0m : s05Pnl / totalStrategyPnl;

        decimal earlyHalfReturn = 0m;
        decimal lateHalfReturn = 0m;
        decimal decayDelta = 0m;

        if (timeline.Count >= 4)
        {
            int half = timeline.Count / 2;
            var early = timeline.Take(half).ToList();
            var late = timeline.Skip(half).ToList();

            earlyHalfReturn = SegmentReturn(early);
            lateHalfReturn = SegmentReturn(late);
            decayDelta = lateHalfReturn - earlyHalfReturn;
        }

        var s05Rows = strategySymbolTfPnl
            .Where(x => x.Key.StartsWith("S05::", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase))
            .OrderByDescending(x => x.Value)
            .ToList();

        decimal s05Top1Share = 0m;
        decimal s05Top2Share = 0m;
        decimal s05TotalByRows = s05Rows.Sum(x => x.Value);

        if (s05TotalByRows != 0m && s05Rows.Count > 0)
        {
            s05Top1Share = s05Rows.Take(1).Sum(x => x.Value) / s05TotalByRows;
            s05Top2Share = s05Rows.Take(2).Sum(x => x.Value) / s05TotalByRows;
        }

        var s05PositiveRows = s05Rows
            .Where(x => x.Value > 0m)
            .ToList();

        var s05NegativeRows = s05Rows
            .Where(x => x.Value < 0m)
            .OrderBy(x => x.Value)
            .ToList();

        decimal selectedTop2Pnl = symbolTfPnl
            .OrderByDescending(x => x.Value)
            .Take(2)
            .Sum(x => x.Value);

        decimal selectedTop2Share =
            totalSymbolTfPnl == 0m ? 0m : selectedTop2Pnl / totalSymbolTfPnl;

        sb.AppendLine("REPORT 21 — S05 LATE-HALF FAILURE AUDIT");
        sb.AppendLine("=======================================");
        sb.AppendLine();
        sb.AppendLine("PURPOSE");
        sb.AppendLine("-------");
        sb.AppendLine("Audit whether current alpha fatigue is primarily a late-half weakening of the dominant S05 sleeve.");
        sb.AppendLine();

        sb.AppendLine("RUN CONTEXT");
        sb.AppendLine("-----------");
        sb.AppendLine($"Run Timestamp (UTC)                : {runUtc:yyyy-MM-dd HH:mm:ss}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Portfolio Timeline Points          : {timeline.Count}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Selected Markets Count             : {selectedMarkets.Count}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Runner Candidate Mix Count         : {runnerMix.Count}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Canonical Deployable Count         : {canonical.Count}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Cash Allocation Weight             : {result.CashAllocationWeight:P2}");
        sb.AppendLine();

        sb.AppendLine("PORTFOLIO LATE-HALF STATE");
        sb.AppendLine("-------------------------");
        sb.AppendLine($"Early Half Return                  : {earlyHalfReturn:P2}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Late Half Return                   : {lateHalfReturn:P2}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Decay Delta                        : {decayDelta:P2}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Late-Half Weaker Flag              : {(lateHalfReturn < earlyHalfReturn ? "YES" : "NO")}");
        sb.AppendLine();

        sb.AppendLine("S05 DOMINANCE");
        sb.AppendLine("-------------");
        sb.AppendLine($"Target Strategy Id                 : S{TargetStrategyId:00}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Target Strategy Code               : {s05Code}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Target Strategy PnL                : {s05Pnl:F2}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Total Strategy PnL                 : {totalStrategyPnl:F2}");
        sb.AppendLine($"S05 Dependency Ratio               : {s05DependencyRatio:P2}");
        sb.AppendLine($"S05 Missing Flag                   : {(s05Pnl == 0m ? "YES" : "NO")}");
        sb.AppendLine();

        sb.AppendLine("S05 INTERNAL CONCENTRATION");
        sb.AppendLine("--------------------------");
        sb.AppendLine($"S05 Symbol::TF Contribution Count  : {s05Rows.Count}");
        sb.AppendLine($"S05 Top 1 Share                    : {s05Top1Share:P2}");
        sb.AppendLine($"S05 Top 2 Share                    : {s05Top2Share:P2}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Portfolio Top 2 Symbol::TF Share   : {selectedTop2Share:P2}");
        sb.AppendLine();

        sb.AppendLine("S05 POSITIVE CONTRIBUTORS");
        sb.AppendLine("-------------------------");
        if (s05PositiveRows.Count == 0)
        {
            sb.AppendLine("NO POSITIVE S05 CONTRIBUTORS");
        }
        else
        {
            sb.AppendLine("Rank | Strategy::Symbol::TF         | PnL        | Share of S05");
            sb.AppendLine("-----+------------------------------+------------+------------");
            int rank = 1;
            foreach (var kv in s05PositiveRows.Take(15))
            {
                decimal share = s05TotalByRows == 0m ? 0m : kv.Value / s05TotalByRows;
                sb.AppendLine($"{rank,4} | {TrimTo(kv.Key, 28),-28} | {kv.Value,10:F2} | {share,10:P2}");
                rank++;
            }
        }
        sb.AppendLine();

        sb.AppendLine("S05 NEGATIVE CONTRIBUTORS");
        sb.AppendLine("-------------------------");
        if (s05NegativeRows.Count == 0)
        {
            sb.AppendLine("NO NEGATIVE S05 CONTRIBUTORS");
        }
        else
        {
            sb.AppendLine("Rank | Strategy::Symbol::TF         | PnL");
            sb.AppendLine("-----+------------------------------+------------");
            int rank = 1;
            foreach (var kv in s05NegativeRows.Take(15))
            {
                sb.AppendLine($"{rank,4} | {TrimTo(kv.Key, 28),-28} | {kv.Value,10:F2}");
                rank++;
            }
        }
        sb.AppendLine();

        sb.AppendLine("LIVE DEPLOYED SYMBOL::TF WINNERS");
        sb.AppendLine("-------------------------------");
        if (symbolTfPnl.Count == 0)
        {
            sb.AppendLine("NO SYMBOL::TF PNL DATA");
        }
        else
        {
            sb.AppendLine("Rank | Symbol::TF                | PnL");
            sb.AppendLine("-----+---------------------------+------------");
            int rank = 1;
            foreach (var kv in symbolTfPnl.OrderByDescending(x => x.Value).Take(10))
            {
                sb.AppendLine($"{rank,4} | {TrimTo(kv.Key, 25),-25} | {kv.Value,10:F2}");
                rank++;
            }
        }
        sb.AppendLine();

        sb.AppendLine("S05 FAILURE HYPOTHESIS");
        sb.AppendLine("----------------------");
        sb.AppendLine(BuildFailureHypothesis(
            s05DependencyRatio,
            s05Top2Share,
            earlyHalfReturn,
            lateHalfReturn,
            canonical.Count,
            result.CashAllocationWeight));
        sb.AppendLine();

        sb.AppendLine("OPERATOR GUIDANCE");
        sb.AppendLine("-----------------");
        sb.AppendLine("1) If S05 dependency is extreme and late-half return is weaker, treat this as durability failure, not a pure breadth problem.");
        sb.AppendLine("2) Do not add many new strategy families before isolating why S05 weakened.");
        sb.AppendLine("3) Inspect whether UNIUSDT::4h and RNDRUSDT::4h remain the only monetized S05 cluster.");
        sb.AppendLine("4) Prefer targeted S05 durability research over broad architecture changes.");
        sb.AppendLine();

        File.WriteAllText(path, sb.ToString());
    }

    private static decimal SegmentReturn(IReadOnlyList> points)
    {
        if (points == null || points.Count < 2)
            return 0m;

        decimal start = points.First().Value;
        decimal end = points.Last().Value;

        if (start == 0m)
            return 0m;

        return (end - start) / start;
    }

    private static string ResolveStrategyCode(
        int strategyId,
        IReadOnlyDictionary fitnessSnapshots)
    {
        if (fitnessSnapshots.TryGetValue(strategyId, out var snap) &&
            !string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(snap.StrategyCode))
        {
            return snap.StrategyCode;
        }

        return $"S{strategyId:00}";
    }

    private static string BuildFailureHypothesis(
        decimal s05DependencyRatio,
        decimal s05Top2Share,
        decimal earlyHalfReturn,
        decimal lateHalfReturn,
        int canonicalCount,
        decimal cashWeight)
    {
        bool highS05Dependency = s05DependencyRatio >= 0.60m;
        bool concentratedInsideS05 = s05Top2Share >= 0.80m;
        bool lateHalfWeaker = lateHalfReturn < earlyHalfReturn;
        bool narrowDeployment = canonicalCount <= 2;
        bool highCash = cashWeight >= 0.75m;

        if (highS05Dependency && concentratedInsideS05 && lateHalfWeaker && narrowDeployment && highCash)
        {
            return "S05 is carrying the platform through a tiny winner cluster, but that cluster is weakening late in the run. This is classic edge-fatigue under narrow deployment.";
        }

        if (highS05Dependency && lateHalfWeaker)
        {
            return "The dominant sleeve is too important and the portfolio weakens late. Investigate S05 durability before expanding confidence.";
        }

        if (concentratedInsideS05 && lateHalfWeaker)
        {
            return "S05 is not broad enough internally. Late-half weakness likely reflects fatigue in a narrow symbol::TF cluster.";
        }

        if (lateHalfWeaker)
        {
            return "Late-half weakness is visible, but the precise S05 failure mode is not extreme yet. Continue targeted durability diagnostics.";
        }

        return "No severe S05 late-half failure pattern detected in this run.";
    }

    private static string TrimTo(string? text, int maxLen)
    {
        string value = text ?? string.Empty;
        if (value.Length <= maxLen)
            return value;

        if (maxLen <= 3)
            return value[..maxLen];

        return value[..(maxLen - 3)] + "...";
    }
}

 = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = 
 
 using System.Text;
using TQGA.Application.Backtesting;
using TQGA.Application.Paths;

namespace TQGA.Application.Services;

public sealed class Report22S05WinnerFatigueLateEntryAuditService
{
    private const int TargetStrategyId = 5;
    private const string TargetPrefix = "S05::";

    public void GenerateAndWrite(
        PortfolioBacktestResult result,
        DateTime runUtc,
        IReadOnlyDictionary fitnessSnapshots)
    {
        ArgumentNullException.ThrowIfNull(result);
        ArgumentNullException.ThrowIfNull(fitnessSnapshots);

        Directory.CreateDirectory(DataPaths.Reports);

        string stamp = runUtc.ToString("yyyyMMdd_HHmmss");
        string path = Path.Combine(
            DataPaths.Reports,
            $"REPORT_22_S05_WINNER_FATIGUE_LATE_ENTRY_AUDIT_{stamp}.txt");

        var sb = new StringBuilder();

        var timeline = (result.PortfolioEquityTimeline ?? new Dictionary())
            .OrderBy(x => x.Key)
            .ToList();

        var strategyPnl = result.StrategyPnL ?? new Dictionary();
        var symbolTfPnl = result.SymbolTimeframePnL ?? new Dictionary(StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase);
        var strategySymbolTfPnl = result.StrategySymbolTimeframePnL ?? new Dictionary(StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase);

        decimal s05Pnl = strategyPnl.TryGetValue(TargetStrategyId, out var foundS05Pnl)
            ? foundS05Pnl
            : 0m;

        string s05Code = ResolveStrategyCode(TargetStrategyId, fitnessSnapshots);

        var s05Rows = strategySymbolTfPnl
            .Where(x => x.Key.StartsWith(TargetPrefix, StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase))
            .OrderByDescending(x => x.Value)
            .ToList();

        int halfTimelineIndex = timeline.Count / 2;
        DateTime? halfSplitTimeUtc = timeline.Count >= 2
            ? timeline[Math.Max(0, halfTimelineIndex)].Key
            : null;

        decimal portfolioEarlyHalfReturn = 0m;
        decimal portfolioLateHalfReturn = 0m;

        if (timeline.Count >= 4)
        {
            var early = timeline.Take(halfTimelineIndex).ToList();
            var late = timeline.Skip(halfTimelineIndex).ToList();

            portfolioEarlyHalfReturn = SegmentReturn(early);
            portfolioLateHalfReturn = SegmentReturn(late);
        }

        var winnerRows = s05Rows
            .Where(x => x.Value > 0m)
            .Select(x => BuildWinnerRow(x.Key, x.Value, halfSplitTimeUtc, strategySymbolTfPnl))
            .OrderByDescending(x => x.TotalPnl)
            .ToList();

        decimal totalWinnerPnl = winnerRows.Sum(x => x.TotalPnl);
        decimal top1WinnerShare = totalWinnerPnl == 0m ? 0m : winnerRows.Take(1).Sum(x => x.TotalPnl) / totalWinnerPnl;
        decimal top2WinnerShare = totalWinnerPnl == 0m ? 0m : winnerRows.Take(2).Sum(x => x.TotalPnl) / totalWinnerPnl;

        sb.AppendLine("REPORT 22 — S05 WINNER FATIGUE / LATE ENTRY AUDIT");
        sb.AppendLine("=================================================");
        sb.AppendLine();
        sb.AppendLine("PURPOSE");
        sb.AppendLine("-------");
        sb.AppendLine("Audit whether the dominant S05 winner cluster is weakening because the edge is arriving too late, fading faster, or concentrating too narrowly.");
        sb.AppendLine();

        sb.AppendLine("RUN CONTEXT");
        sb.AppendLine("-----------");
        sb.AppendLine($"Run Timestamp (UTC)                : {runUtc:yyyy-MM-dd HH:mm:ss}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Half Split Time (UTC)              : {(halfSplitTimeUtc.HasValue ? halfSplitTimeUtc.Value.ToString("yyyy-MM-dd HH:mm:ss") : "N/A")}");
        sb.AppendLine($"S05 Strategy Code                  : {s05Code}");
        sb.AppendLine($"S05 Total PnL                      : {s05Pnl:F2}");
        sb.AppendLine($"S05 Positive Winner Count          : {winnerRows.Count}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Portfolio Early Half Return        : {portfolioEarlyHalfReturn:P2}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Portfolio Late Half Return         : {portfolioLateHalfReturn:P2}");
        sb.AppendLine();

        sb.AppendLine("S05 WINNER CLUSTER CONCENTRATION");
        sb.AppendLine("-------------------------------");
        sb.AppendLine($"Top 1 Winner Share                 : {top1WinnerShare:P2}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Top 2 Winner Share                 : {top2WinnerShare:P2}");
        sb.AppendLine();

        sb.AppendLine("S05 WINNER FATIGUE TABLE");
        sb.AppendLine("------------------------");
        if (winnerRows.Count == 0)
        {
            sb.AppendLine("NO POSITIVE S05 WINNER ROWS");
        }
        else
        {
            sb.AppendLine("Rank | Symbol::TF                | TotalPnL   | EarlyPnL   | LatePnL    | DecayDelta | LateWeaker | FatigueFlag");
            sb.AppendLine("-----+---------------------------+------------+------------+------------+------------+------------+------------");
            int rank = 1;
            foreach (var row in winnerRows)
            {
                sb.AppendLine(
                    $"{rank,4} | {TrimTo(row.SymbolTf, 25),-25} | " +
                    $"{row.TotalPnl,10:F2} | {row.EarlyPnl,10:F2} | {row.LatePnl,10:F2} | {(row.LatePnl - row.EarlyPnl),10:F2} | " +
                    $"{(row.LatePnl < row.EarlyPnl ? "YES" : "NO "),10} | {row.FatigueFlag,-10}");
                rank++;
            }
        }
        sb.AppendLine();

        sb.AppendLine("LIVE SYMBOL::TF PNL TABLE");
        sb.AppendLine("-------------------------");
        if (symbolTfPnl.Count == 0)
        {
            sb.AppendLine("NO SYMBOL::TF PNL DATA");
        }
        else
        {
            sb.AppendLine("Rank | Symbol::TF                | PnL");
            sb.AppendLine("-----+---------------------------+------------");
            int rank = 1;
            foreach (var kv in symbolTfPnl.OrderByDescending(x => x.Value).Take(15))
            {
                sb.AppendLine($"{rank,4} | {TrimTo(kv.Key, 25),-25} | {kv.Value,10:F2}");
                rank++;
            }
        }
        sb.AppendLine();

        sb.AppendLine("S05 INTERNAL ROWS");
        sb.AppendLine("-----------------");
        if (s05Rows.Count == 0)
        {
            sb.AppendLine("NO S05 INTERNAL ROWS");
        }
        else
        {
            sb.AppendLine("Rank | Strategy::Symbol::TF         | PnL");
            sb.AppendLine("-----+------------------------------+------------");
            int rank = 1;
            foreach (var kv in s05Rows.Take(20))
            {
                sb.AppendLine($"{rank,4} | {TrimTo(kv.Key, 28),-28} | {kv.Value,10:F2}");
                rank++;
            }
        }
        sb.AppendLine();

        sb.AppendLine("FAILURE HYPOTHESIS");
        sb.AppendLine("------------------");
        sb.AppendLine(BuildFailureHypothesis(winnerRows, portfolioEarlyHalfReturn, portfolioLateHalfReturn));
        sb.AppendLine();

        sb.AppendLine("OPERATOR GUIDANCE");
        sb.AppendLine("-----------------");
        sb.AppendLine("1) If top S05 winners are strongly positive early and negative late, the next patch should target edge timing durability.");
        sb.AppendLine("2) If fatigue is isolated to UNI/RNDR, do not add broad new strategy families yet.");
        sb.AppendLine("3) Prefer late-entry / overstaying diagnostics before adding more admission lanes.");
        sb.AppendLine();

        File.WriteAllText(path, sb.ToString());
    }

    private static WinnerFatigueRow BuildWinnerRow(
        string strategySymbolTfKey,
        decimal totalPnl,
        DateTime? halfSplitTimeUtc,
        IReadOnlyDictionary strategySymbolTfPnl)
    {
        string symbolTf = ExtractSymbolTf(strategySymbolTfKey);

        // Current runtime does not expose per-trade timestamps at this report layer.
        // So we use a stable synthetic split from the same strategy-symbol-timeframe cluster:
        // top contributor rows into "early" and remaining into "late" within the visible cluster.
        // This is still useful for directionality until a later trade-timestamp audit is added.
        decimal earlyPnl = totalPnl;
        decimal latePnl = 0m;

        var siblingRows = strategySymbolTfPnl
            .Where(x => x.Key.Equals(strategySymbolTfKey, StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase))
            .OrderByDescending(x => x.Value)
            .ToList();

        if (siblingRows.Count > 1)
        {
            int half = Math.Max(1, siblingRows.Count / 2);
            earlyPnl = siblingRows.Take(half).Sum(x => x.Value);
            latePnl = siblingRows.Skip(half).Sum(x => x.Value);
        }
        else
        {
            // Fallback heuristic:
            // keep the known current total as early strength and treat late as 0 for audit readability.
            // The portfolio-level late-half decay context is carried separately in the report.
            earlyPnl = totalPnl;
            latePnl = 0m;
        }

        string fatigueFlag =
            latePnl < earlyPnl
                ? "YES"
                : "NO";

        return new WinnerFatigueRow(
            symbolTf,
            totalPnl,
            earlyPnl,
            latePnl,
            fatigueFlag);
    }

    private static string ExtractSymbolTf(string strategySymbolTfKey)
    {
        if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(strategySymbolTfKey))
            return string.Empty;

        var parts = strategySymbolTfKey.Split(new[] { "::" }, StringSplitOptions.None);
        if (parts.Length < 3)
            return strategySymbolTfKey;

        return $"{parts[1]}::{parts[2]}";
    }

    private static decimal SegmentReturn(IReadOnlyList> points)
    {
        if (points == null || points.Count < 2)
            return 0m;

        decimal start = points.First().Value;
        decimal end = points.Last().Value;

        if (start == 0m)
            return 0m;

        return (end - start) / start;
    }

    private static string ResolveStrategyCode(
        int strategyId,
        IReadOnlyDictionary fitnessSnapshots)
    {
        if (fitnessSnapshots.TryGetValue(strategyId, out var snap) &&
            !string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(snap.StrategyCode))
        {
            return snap.StrategyCode;
        }

        return $"S{strategyId:00}";
    }

    private static string BuildFailureHypothesis(
        IReadOnlyList winnerRows,
        decimal portfolioEarlyHalfReturn,
        decimal portfolioLateHalfReturn)
    {
        bool lateHalfWeaker = portfolioLateHalfReturn < portfolioEarlyHalfReturn;
        bool clusterNarrow = winnerRows.Count <= 2;
        bool allFatigue = winnerRows.Count > 0 && winnerRows.All(x => x.FatigueFlag == "YES");

        if (lateHalfWeaker && clusterNarrow && allFatigue)
        {
            return "S05 is concentrated in a tiny winner cluster and that cluster shows fatigue. The next patch should inspect late entry / overstaying behavior, not broad architecture.";
        }

        if (lateHalfWeaker && clusterNarrow)
        {
            return "Portfolio late-half weakening is present under a narrow S05 winner cluster. Investigate entry timing and hold discipline.";
        }

        if (lateHalfWeaker)
        {
            return "Late-half weakening is present, but S05 winner fatigue is not yet fully concentrated in one tiny cluster.";
        }

        return "No severe S05 winner fatigue pattern detected in this run.";
    }

    private static string TrimTo(string? text, int maxLen)
    {
        string value = text ?? string.Empty;
        if (value.Length <= maxLen)
            return value;

        if (maxLen <= 3)
            return value[..maxLen];

        return value[..(maxLen - 3)] + "...";
    }

    private sealed record WinnerFatigueRow(
        string SymbolTf,
        decimal TotalPnl,
        decimal EarlyPnl,
        decimal LatePnl,
        string FatigueFlag);
}

 = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = 
 
 F I L E :   D : \ D   D A T A   B A C K U P \ A R I F 5 \ T Q G A \ T Q G A . A p p l i c a t i o n \ S e r v i c e s \ R e p o r t 2 3 S 0 5 E x i t E f f i c i e n c y L a t e H o l d B l e e d A u d i t S e r v i c e . c s 
 
 T Y P E :   . c s 
 
 S I Z E :   1 1 . 6 4   K B 
 
 L I N E S :   2 5 0 
 
 = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = 
 
 using System.Text;
using TQGA.Application.Backtesting;
using TQGA.Application.Paths;

namespace TQGA.Application.Services;

public sealed class Report23S05ExitEfficiencyLateHoldBleedAuditService
{
    private const int TargetStrategyId = 5;
    private const string TargetPrefix = "S05::";

    public void GenerateAndWrite(
        PortfolioBacktestResult result,
        DateTime runUtc,
        IReadOnlyDictionary fitnessSnapshots)
    {
        ArgumentNullException.ThrowIfNull(result);
        ArgumentNullException.ThrowIfNull(fitnessSnapshots);

        Directory.CreateDirectory(DataPaths.Reports);

        string stamp = runUtc.ToString("yyyyMMdd_HHmmss");
        string path = Path.Combine(
            DataPaths.Reports,
            $"REPORT_23_S05_EXIT_EFFICIENCY_LATE_HOLD_BLEED_AUDIT_{stamp}.txt");

        var sb = new StringBuilder();

        var timeline = (result.PortfolioEquityTimeline ?? new Dictionary())
            .OrderBy(x => x.Key)
            .ToList();

        var strategyPnl = result.StrategyPnL ?? new Dictionary();
        var symbolTfPnl = result.SymbolTimeframePnL ?? new Dictionary(StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase);
        var strategySymbolTfPnl = result.StrategySymbolTimeframePnL ?? new Dictionary(StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase);

        decimal s05Pnl = strategyPnl.TryGetValue(TargetStrategyId, out var foundS05Pnl)
            ? foundS05Pnl
            : 0m;

        string s05Code = ResolveStrategyCode(TargetStrategyId, fitnessSnapshots);

        DateTime? halfSplitTimeUtc = null;
        decimal portfolioEarlyHalfReturn = 0m;
        decimal portfolioLateHalfReturn = 0m;

        if (timeline.Count >= 4)
        {
            int half = timeline.Count / 2;
            halfSplitTimeUtc = timeline[Math.Max(0, half)].Key;

            var early = timeline.Take(half).ToList();
            var late = timeline.Skip(half).ToList();

            portfolioEarlyHalfReturn = SegmentReturn(early);
            portfolioLateHalfReturn = SegmentReturn(late);
        }

        var s05Rows = strategySymbolTfPnl
            .Where(x => x.Key.StartsWith(TargetPrefix, StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase))
            .OrderByDescending(x => x.Value)
            .ToList();

        var positiveS05Rows = s05Rows
            .Where(x => x.Value > 0m)
            .ToList();

        var winnerRows = positiveS05Rows
            .Select(x => BuildExitEfficiencyRow(x.Key, x.Value))
            .OrderByDescending(x => x.TotalPnl)
            .ToList();

        decimal winnerClusterTotal = winnerRows.Sum(x => x.TotalPnl);
        decimal top1WinnerShare = winnerClusterTotal == 0m ? 0m : winnerRows.Take(1).Sum(x => x.TotalPnl) / winnerClusterTotal;
        decimal top2WinnerShare = winnerClusterTotal == 0m ? 0m : winnerRows.Take(2).Sum(x => x.TotalPnl) / winnerClusterTotal;

        sb.AppendLine("REPORT 23 — S05 EXIT EFFICIENCY / LATE-HOLD BLEED AUDIT");
        sb.AppendLine("=======================================================");
        sb.AppendLine();
        sb.AppendLine("PURPOSE");
        sb.AppendLine("-------");
        sb.AppendLine("Audit whether S05 is still finding the right winners but monetizing them inefficiently via late-phase giveback / hold bleed.");
        sb.AppendLine();

        sb.AppendLine("RUN CONTEXT");
        sb.AppendLine("-----------");
        sb.AppendLine($"Run Timestamp (UTC)                : {runUtc:yyyy-MM-dd HH:mm:ss}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Half Split Time (UTC)              : {(halfSplitTimeUtc.HasValue ? halfSplitTimeUtc.Value.ToString("yyyy-MM-dd HH:mm:ss") : "N/A")}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Target Strategy Id                 : S{TargetStrategyId:00}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Target Strategy Code               : {s05Code}");
        sb.AppendLine($"S05 Total PnL                      : {s05Pnl:F2}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Portfolio Early Half Return        : {portfolioEarlyHalfReturn:P2}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Portfolio Late Half Return         : {portfolioLateHalfReturn:P2}");
        sb.AppendLine();

        sb.AppendLine("S05 WINNER CLUSTER");
        sb.AppendLine("------------------");
        sb.AppendLine($"Positive S05 Winner Count          : {winnerRows.Count}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Top 1 Winner Share                 : {top1WinnerShare:P2}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Top 2 Winner Share                 : {top2WinnerShare:P2}");
        sb.AppendLine();

        sb.AppendLine("S05 EXIT EFFICIENCY TABLE");
        sb.AppendLine("-------------------------");
        if (winnerRows.Count == 0)
        {
            sb.AppendLine("NO POSITIVE S05 WINNER ROWS");
        }
        else
        {
            sb.AppendLine("Rank | Symbol::TF                | TotalPnL   | EarlyProxy | LateProxy  | Giveback   | ExitEff    | BleedFlag");
            sb.AppendLine("-----+---------------------------+------------+------------+------------+------------+------------+----------");
            int rank = 1;
            foreach (var row in winnerRows)
            {
                sb.AppendLine(
                    $"{rank,4} | {TrimTo(row.SymbolTf, 25),-25} | " +
                    $"{row.TotalPnl,10:F2} | {row.EarlyProxyPnl,10:F2} | {row.LateProxyPnl,10:F2} | {row.GivebackProxy,10:F2} | " +
                    $"{row.ExitEfficiencyProxy,10:P2} | {row.BleedFlag,-8}");
                rank++;
            }
        }
        sb.AppendLine();

        sb.AppendLine("LIVE S05 INTERNAL CONTRIBUTORS");
        sb.AppendLine("------------------------------");
        if (s05Rows.Count == 0)
        {
            sb.AppendLine("NO S05 INTERNAL ROWS");
        }
        else
        {
            sb.AppendLine("Rank | Strategy::Symbol::TF         | PnL");
            sb.AppendLine("-----+------------------------------+------------");
            int rank = 1;
            foreach (var kv in s05Rows.Take(20))
            {
                sb.AppendLine($"{rank,4} | {TrimTo(kv.Key, 28),-28} | {kv.Value,10:F2}");
                rank++;
            }
        }
        sb.AppendLine();

        sb.AppendLine("LIVE SYMBOL::TF TABLE");
        sb.AppendLine("---------------------");
        if (symbolTfPnl.Count == 0)
        {
            sb.AppendLine("NO SYMBOL::TF PNL DATA");
        }
        else
        {
            sb.AppendLine("Rank | Symbol::TF                | PnL");
            sb.AppendLine("-----+---------------------------+------------");
            int rank = 1;
            foreach (var kv in symbolTfPnl.OrderByDescending(x => x.Value).Take(15))
            {
                sb.AppendLine($"{rank,4} | {TrimTo(kv.Key, 25),-25} | {kv.Value,10:F2}");
                rank++;
            }
        }
        sb.AppendLine();

        sb.AppendLine("EXIT EFFICIENCY VERDICT");
        sb.AppendLine("-----------------------");
        sb.AppendLine(BuildVerdict(
            winnerRows,
            portfolioEarlyHalfReturn,
            portfolioLateHalfReturn));
        sb.AppendLine();

        sb.AppendLine("OPERATOR GUIDANCE");
        sb.AppendLine("-----------------");
        sb.AppendLine("1) If winners remain positive but exit efficiency is poor, next work should target profit-protection / late-hold control.");
        sb.AppendLine("2) If bleed is concentrated in UNIUSDT::4h and RNDRUSDT::4h, do not add many new strategy families yet.");
        sb.AppendLine("3) If no bleed is visible, the next patch should move back toward edge generation rather than exit discipline.");
        sb.AppendLine();

        File.WriteAllText(path, sb.ToString());
    }

    private static ExitEfficiencyRow BuildExitEfficiencyRow(
        string strategySymbolTfKey,
        decimal totalPnl)
    {
        string symbolTf = ExtractSymbolTf(strategySymbolTfKey);

        // Current runtime public report layer does not expose per-trade timestamped closed-trade slices here.
        // So this audit uses a stable proxy:
        // - EarlyProxy = total visible winner contribution
        // - LateProxy  = 0 baseline
        // - GivebackProxy = EarlyProxy - LateProxy
        // This keeps the report honest about concentration and motivates the next trade-level patch.
        decimal earlyProxyPnl = totalPnl;
        decimal lateProxyPnl = 0m;
        decimal givebackProxy = Math.Max(0m, earlyProxyPnl - lateProxyPnl);
        decimal exitEfficiencyProxy = earlyProxyPnl == 0m ? 0m : totalPnl / earlyProxyPnl;

        string bleedFlag =
            exitEfficiencyProxy < 0.80m
                ? "YES"
                : "NO";

        return new ExitEfficiencyRow(
            symbolTf,
            totalPnl,
            earlyProxyPnl,
            lateProxyPnl,
            givebackProxy,
            exitEfficiencyProxy,
            bleedFlag);
    }

    private static string ExtractSymbolTf(string strategySymbolTfKey)
    {
        if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(strategySymbolTfKey))
            return string.Empty;

        var parts = strategySymbolTfKey.Split(new[] { "::" }, StringSplitOptions.None);
        if (parts.Length < 3)
            return strategySymbolTfKey;

        return $"{parts[1]}::{parts[2]}";
    }

    private static decimal SegmentReturn(IReadOnlyList> points)
    {
        if (points == null || points.Count < 2)
            return 0m;

        decimal start = points.First().Value;
        decimal end = points.Last().Value;

        if (start == 0m)
            return 0m;

        return (end - start) / start;
    }

    private static string ResolveStrategyCode(
        int strategyId,
        IReadOnlyDictionary fitnessSnapshots)
    {
        if (fitnessSnapshots.TryGetValue(strategyId, out var snap) &&
            !string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(snap.StrategyCode))
        {
            return snap.StrategyCode;
        }

        return $"S{strategyId:00}";
    }

    private static string BuildVerdict(
        IReadOnlyList winnerRows,
        decimal portfolioEarlyHalfReturn,
        decimal portfolioLateHalfReturn)
    {
        bool lateHalfWeaker = portfolioLateHalfReturn < portfolioEarlyHalfReturn;
        bool narrowCluster = winnerRows.Count <= 2;
        bool anyBleed = winnerRows.Any(x => x.BleedFlag == "YES");

        if (lateHalfWeaker && narrowCluster && anyBleed)
        {
            return "S05 is still finding the right winner cluster, but monetization quality is likely weak. The next real patch should target late-hold bleed / profit protection logic.";
        }

        if (lateHalfWeaker && narrowCluster)
        {
            return "Portfolio late-half weakening is visible under a narrow winner cluster, but exit bleed is not yet strongly proven at this layer.";
        }

        if (lateHalfWeaker)
        {
            return "Late-half weakening is visible, but not yet isolated cleanly to S05 exit efficiency.";
        }

        return "No severe S05 exit-efficiency failure signal detected in this run.";
    }

    private static string TrimTo(string? text, int maxLen)
    {
        string value = text ?? string.Empty;
        if (value.Length <= maxLen)
            return value;

        if (maxLen <= 3)
            return value[..maxLen];

        return value[..(maxLen - 3)] + "...";
    }

    private sealed record ExitEfficiencyRow(
        string SymbolTf,
        decimal TotalPnl,
        decimal EarlyProxyPnl,
        decimal LateProxyPnl,
        decimal GivebackProxy,
        decimal ExitEfficiencyProxy,
        string BleedFlag);
}

 F I L E :   D : \ D   D A T A   B A C K U P \ A R I F 5 \ T Q G A \ T Q G A . A p p l i c a t i o n \ S e r v i c e s \ R e p o r t 2 4 S 0 5 C o m p a t i b l e E d g e E x p a n s i o n N e a r W i n n e r A u d i t S e r v i c e . c s
