 = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = 
 
 using System.Text;
using TQGA.Application.Backtesting;
using TQGA.Application.Paths;

namespace TQGA.Application.Services;

public sealed class Report24S05CompatibleEdgeExpansionNearWinnerAuditService
{
    private static readonly string[] PriorityWinnerStyleSymbols =
    [
        "UNIUSDT",
        "RNDRUSDT",
        "FILUSDT",
        "DOTUSDT",
        "ARBUSDT",
        "SUIUSDT",
        "NEARUSDT",
        "SOLUSDT",
        "LINKUSDT"
    ];

    public void GenerateAndWrite(
        PortfolioBacktestResult result,
        DateTime runUtc,
        IReadOnlyDictionary fitnessSnapshots)
    {
        ArgumentNullException.ThrowIfNull(result);
        ArgumentNullException.ThrowIfNull(fitnessSnapshots);

        Directory.CreateDirectory(DataPaths.Reports);

        string stamp = runUtc.ToString("yyyyMMdd_HHmmss");
        string path = Path.Combine(
            DataPaths.Reports,
            $"REPORT_24_S05_COMPATIBLE_EDGE_EXPANSION_NEAR_WINNER_AUDIT_{stamp}.txt");

        var sb = new StringBuilder();

        var strategyPnl = result.StrategyPnL ?? new Dictionary();
        var symbolTfPnl = result.SymbolTimeframePnL ?? new Dictionary(StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase);
        var rejections = result.MarketSelectionRejections ?? new Dictionary(StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase);
        var selectedMarkets = (result.SelectedMarkets ?? new List())
            .ToHashSet(StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase);
        var runnerMix = result.MarketAllocationWeights ?? new Dictionary(StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase);
        var canonical = result.CanonicalCioPostGatingWeights ?? new Dictionary(StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase);

        decimal s05Pnl = strategyPnl.TryGetValue(5, out var foundS05Pnl)
            ? foundS05Pnl
            : 0m;

        string s05Code = ResolveStrategyCode(5, fitnessSnapshots);

        var liveWinners = symbolTfPnl
            .Where(x => x.Value > 0m)
            .OrderByDescending(x => x.Value)
            .ToList();

        var nearWinners = rejections
            .Select(kv => BuildNearWinnerRow(kv.Key, kv.Value, selectedMarkets))
            .Where(x => x.IsRelevant)
            .OrderByDescending(x => x.PriorityScore)
            .ThenByDescending(x => x.S05CompatibilityScore)
            .ThenBy(x => x.MarketKey, StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase)
            .ToList();

        decimal totalWinnerPnl = liveWinners.Sum(x => x.Value);
        decimal top2WinnerShare = totalWinnerPnl == 0m
            ? 0m
            : liveWinners.Take(2).Sum(x => x.Value) / totalWinnerPnl;

        sb.AppendLine("REPORT 24 — S05 COMPATIBLE EDGE EXPANSION / NEAR-WINNER AUDIT");
        sb.AppendLine("=============================================================");
        sb.AppendLine();
        sb.AppendLine("PURPOSE");
        sb.AppendLine("-------");
        sb.AppendLine("Audit which rejected candidates are the best next S05-compatible near-winner expansion targets.");
        sb.AppendLine();

        sb.AppendLine("RUN CONTEXT");
        sb.AppendLine("-----------");
        sb.AppendLine($"Run Timestamp (UTC)                : {runUtc:yyyy-MM-dd HH:mm:ss}");
        sb.AppendLine($"S05 Strategy Code                  : {s05Code}");
        sb.AppendLine($"S05 Strategy PnL                   : {s05Pnl:F2}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Selected Markets Count             : {selectedMarkets.Count}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Runner Candidate Mix Count         : {runnerMix.Count}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Canonical Deployable Count         : {canonical.Count}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Cash Allocation Weight             : {result.CashAllocationWeight:P2}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Positive Winner Count              : {liveWinners.Count}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Top 2 Winner Share                 : {top2WinnerShare:P2}");
        sb.AppendLine();

        sb.AppendLine("LIVE WINNER CLUSTER");
        sb.AppendLine("-------------------");
        if (liveWinners.Count == 0)
        {
            sb.AppendLine("NO POSITIVE LIVE WINNERS");
        }
        else
        {
            sb.AppendLine("Rank | Symbol::TF                | PnL");
            sb.AppendLine("-----+---------------------------+------------");
            int rank = 1;
            foreach (var kv in liveWinners.Take(10))
            {
                sb.AppendLine($"{rank,4} | {TrimTo(kv.Key, 25),-25} | {kv.Value,10:F2}");
                rank++;
            }
        }
        sb.AppendLine();

        sb.AppendLine("TOP S05-COMPATIBLE NEAR-WINNERS");
        sb.AppendLine("-------------------------------");
        if (nearWinners.Count == 0)
        {
            sb.AppendLine("NO RELEVANT NEAR-WINNER CANDIDATES FOUND");
        }
        else
        {
            sb.AppendLine("Rank | Market                    | ReasonBucket                     | S05Compat | Priority | Expansion Verdict");
            sb.AppendLine("-----+---------------------------+----------------------------------+-----------+----------+------------------------------");
            int rank = 1;
            foreach (var row in nearWinners.Take(20))
            {
                sb.AppendLine(
                    $"{rank,4} | {TrimTo(row.MarketKey, 25),-25} | {TrimTo(row.ReasonBucket, 32),-32} | " +
                    $"{row.S05CompatibilityScore,9:F2} | {row.PriorityScore,8:F2} | {TrimTo(row.ExpansionVerdict, 28)}");
                rank++;
            }
        }
        sb.AppendLine();

        sb.AppendLine("NEAR-WINNER REASON BUCKETS");
        sb.AppendLine("--------------------------");
        if (nearWinners.Count == 0)
        {
            sb.AppendLine("NO NEAR-WINNER BUCKETS");
        }
        else
        {
            foreach (var bucket in nearWinners
                         .GroupBy(x => x.ReasonBucket)
                         .OrderByDescending(g => g.Count())
                         .ThenBy(g => g.Key, StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase))
            {
                sb.AppendLine($"{bucket.Key,-36} {bucket.Count(),6}");
            }
        }
        sb.AppendLine();

        sb.AppendLine("PRIORITY RESEARCH TARGETS");
        sb.AppendLine("-------------------------");
        if (nearWinners.Count == 0)
        {
            sb.AppendLine("NO PRIORITY RESEARCH TARGETS");
        }
        else
        {
            foreach (var row in nearWinners.Take(8))
            {
                sb.AppendLine(
                    $"{row.MarketKey,-24} " +
                    $"bucket={row.ReasonBucket,-30} " +
                    $"compat={row.S05CompatibilityScore:F2} " +
                    $"priority={row.PriorityScore:F2} " +
                    $"=> {row.ExpansionVerdict}");
            }
        }
        sb.AppendLine();

        sb.AppendLine("EXPANSION VERDICT");
        sb.AppendLine("-----------------");
        sb.AppendLine(BuildVerdict(nearWinners, liveWinners.Count, result.CashAllocationWeight));
        sb.AppendLine();

        sb.AppendLine("OPERATOR GUIDANCE");
        sb.AppendLine("-----------------");
        sb.AppendLine("1) Prefer S05-compatible 4h candidates first.");
        sb.AppendLine("2) Favor names blocked by near-miss buckets (dispersion, regime-lane overflow, liquidity-tier overflow) before inventing new strategy families.");
        sb.AppendLine("3) If the best near-winners remain weak after repeated audits, then the next move should be a true new edge family, not more admission tuning.");
        sb.AppendLine();

        File.WriteAllText(path, sb.ToString());
    }

    private static NearWinnerRow BuildNearWinnerRow(
        string marketKey,
        string rejectionReason,
        IReadOnlySet selectedMarkets)
    {
        if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(marketKey))
            return NearWinnerRow.Empty;

        if (selectedMarkets.Contains(marketKey))
            return NearWinnerRow.Empty;

        string symbol = ExtractSymbol(marketKey);
        string timeframe = ExtractTimeframe(marketKey);

        bool is4h = timeframe.Equals("4h", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase);
        bool isPrioritySymbol = PriorityWinnerStyleSymbols.Contains(symbol, StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase);

        string reasonBucket = NormalizeReasonBucket(rejectionReason);

        decimal s05CompatibilityScore = 0m;
        if (is4h) s05CompatibilityScore += 0.40m;
        if (isPrioritySymbol) s05CompatibilityScore += 0.30m;
        if (reasonBucket == "WaveBRejected:DispersionGuard") s05CompatibilityScore += 0.20m;
        if (reasonBucket == "REJECT: regime near-miss lane overflow") s05CompatibilityScore += 0.18m;
        if (reasonBucket == "REJECT: liquidity tier-2 lane overflow") s05CompatibilityScore += 0.16m;
        if (reasonBucket == "REJECT: outside top leadership set") s05CompatibilityScore += 0.12m;
        if (reasonBucket == "REJECT: regime not trend/high-vol-up") s05CompatibilityScore += 0.08m;
        if (reasonBucket == "REJECT: low liquidity") s05CompatibilityScore += 0.06m;

        decimal priorityScore = s05CompatibilityScore;

        if (reasonBucket == "WaveBRejected:DispersionGuard")
            priorityScore += 0.25m;

        if (reasonBucket == "REJECT: regime near-miss lane overflow")
            priorityScore += 0.18m;

        if (reasonBucket == "REJECT: liquidity tier-2 lane overflow")
            priorityScore += 0.16m;

        bool isRelevant =
            is4h &&
            (
                reasonBucket == "WaveBRejected:DispersionGuard" ||
                reasonBucket == "REJECT: regime near-miss lane overflow" ||
                reasonBucket == "REJECT: liquidity tier-2 lane overflow" ||
                reasonBucket == "REJECT: regime not trend/high-vol-up" ||
                reasonBucket == "REJECT: low liquidity" ||
                reasonBucket == "REJECT: outside top leadership set"
            );

        string verdict = BuildExpansionVerdict(reasonBucket, is4h, isPrioritySymbol);

        return new NearWinnerRow(
            marketKey,
            reasonBucket,
            s05CompatibilityScore,
            priorityScore,
            verdict,
            isRelevant);
    }

    private static string BuildExpansionVerdict(string reasonBucket, bool is4h, bool isPrioritySymbol)
    {
        if (!is4h)
            return "Lower priority timeframe";

        if (reasonBucket == "WaveBRejected:DispersionGuard")
            return "Best immediate expansion candidate";

        if (reasonBucket == "REJECT: regime near-miss lane overflow")
            return "Strong emerging-trend research candidate";

        if (reasonBucket == "REJECT: liquidity tier-2 lane overflow")
            return "Strong tier-2 liquidity research candidate";

        if (reasonBucket == "REJECT: outside top leadership set" && isPrioritySymbol)
            return "Borderline near-winner, monitor";

        if (reasonBucket == "REJECT: regime not trend/high-vol-up" && isPrioritySymbol)
            return "Watch for regime-turn upgrade";

        if (reasonBucket == "REJECT: low liquidity" && isPrioritySymbol)
            return "Watch for liquidity improvement";

        return "Secondary research candidate";
    }

    private static string NormalizeReasonBucket(string rejectionReason)
    {
        string value = rejectionReason?.Trim() ?? string.Empty;

        if (value.StartsWith("WaveBRejected:DispersionGuard", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase))
            return "WaveBRejected:DispersionGuard";

        if (value.StartsWith("REJECT: regime near-miss lane overflow", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase))
            return "REJECT: regime near-miss lane overflow";

        if (value.StartsWith("REJECT: liquidity tier-2 lane overflow", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase))
            return "REJECT: liquidity tier-2 lane overflow";

        if (value.StartsWith("REJECT: outside top", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase))
            return "REJECT: outside top leadership set";

        if (value.StartsWith("REJECT: regime not trend/high-vol-up", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase))
            return "REJECT: regime not trend/high-vol-up";

        if (value.StartsWith("REJECT: low liquidity", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase))
            return "REJECT: low liquidity";

        if (value.StartsWith("REJECT: dead / too low volatility", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase))
            return "REJECT: dead / too low volatility";

        return value;
    }

    private static string ResolveStrategyCode(
        int strategyId,
        IReadOnlyDictionary fitnessSnapshots)
    {
        if (fitnessSnapshots.TryGetValue(strategyId, out var snap) &&
            !string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(snap.StrategyCode))
        {
            return snap.StrategyCode;
        }

        return $"S{strategyId:00}";
    }

    private static string BuildVerdict(
        IReadOnlyList nearWinners,
        int liveWinnerCount,
        decimal cashWeight)
    {
        bool strongNearWinners =
            nearWinners.Take(3).Any(x => x.PriorityScore >= 0.75m);

        if (liveWinnerCount <= 2 && cashWeight >= 0.75m && strongNearWinners)
        {
            return "There are still credible S05-compatible expansion targets. Next work should stay on controlled edge expansion, not exit logic.";
        }

        if (liveWinnerCount <= 2 && cashWeight >= 0.75m)
        {
            return "Winner concentration remains high, but the current near-winner set is not yet strong enough. The next move may need a true new edge family rather than more admission tuning.";
        }

        return "Near-winner structure is not extreme in this run.";
    }

    private static string ExtractSymbol(string marketKey)
    {
        if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(marketKey))
            return string.Empty;

        var parts = marketKey.Split(new[] { "::" }, StringSplitOptions.None);
        return parts.Length >= 1 ? parts[0].Trim() : string.Empty;
    }

    private static string ExtractTimeframe(string marketKey)
    {
        if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(marketKey))
            return string.Empty;

        var parts = marketKey.Split(new[] { "::" }, StringSplitOptions.None);
        return parts.Length >= 2 ? parts[1].Trim() : string.Empty;
    }

    private static string TrimTo(string? text, int maxLen)
    {
        string value = text ?? string.Empty;
        if (value.Length <= maxLen)
            return value;

        if (maxLen <= 3)
            return value[..maxLen];

        return value[..(maxLen - 3)] + "...";
    }

    private sealed record NearWinnerRow(
        string MarketKey,
        string ReasonBucket,
        decimal S05CompatibilityScore,
        decimal PriorityScore,
        string ExpansionVerdict,
        bool IsRelevant)
    {
        public static NearWinnerRow Empty =>
            new(string.Empty, string.Empty, 0m, 0m, string.Empty, false);
    }
}

 T Y P E :   . c s

 L I N E S :   2 6 3 
 
 = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = 
 
 using System.Text;
using TQGA.Application.Backtesting;
using TQGA.Application.Paths;

namespace TQGA.Application.Services;

public sealed class Report25DispersionGuardNearWinnerPromotionAuditService
{
    private static readonly string[] PromotionPrioritySymbols =
    [
        "DOTUSDT",
        "FILUSDT",
        "LINKUSDT",
        "NEARUSDT",
        "SOLUSDT",
        "UNIUSDT",
        "RNDRUSDT"
    ];

    public void GenerateAndWrite(
        PortfolioBacktestResult result,
        DateTime runUtc,
        IReadOnlyDictionary fitnessSnapshots)
    {
        ArgumentNullException.ThrowIfNull(result);
        ArgumentNullException.ThrowIfNull(fitnessSnapshots);

        Directory.CreateDirectory(DataPaths.Reports);

        string stamp = runUtc.ToString("yyyyMMdd_HHmmss");
        string path = Path.Combine(
            DataPaths.Reports,
            $"REPORT_25_DISPERSION_GUARD_NEAR_WINNER_PROMOTION_AUDIT_{stamp}.txt");

        var sb = new StringBuilder();

        var symbolTfPnl = result.SymbolTimeframePnL ?? new Dictionary(StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase);
        var rejections = result.MarketSelectionRejections ?? new Dictionary(StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase);
        var selectedMarkets = (result.SelectedMarkets ?? new List())
            .ToHashSet(StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase);

        var liveWinners = symbolTfPnl
            .Where(x => x.Value > 0m)
            .OrderByDescending(x => x.Value)
            .ToList();

        var dispersionNearWinners = rejections
            .Where(x => x.Value.StartsWith("WaveBRejected:DispersionGuard", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase))
            .Select(x => BuildPromotionRow(x.Key, x.Value, selectedMarkets))
            .Where(x => x.IsRelevant)
            .OrderByDescending(x => x.PromotionScore)
            .ThenByDescending(x => x.WinnerSimilarityScore)
            .ThenBy(x => x.MarketKey, StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase)
            .ToList();

        decimal totalWinnerPnl = liveWinners.Sum(x => x.Value);
        decimal top2WinnerShare = totalWinnerPnl == 0m
            ? 0m
            : liveWinners.Take(2).Sum(x => x.Value) / totalWinnerPnl;

        sb.AppendLine("REPORT 25 — DISPERSION-GUARD NEAR-WINNER PROMOTION AUDIT");
        sb.AppendLine("========================================================");
        sb.AppendLine();
        sb.AppendLine("PURPOSE");
        sb.AppendLine("-------");
        sb.AppendLine("Audit which Wave-B dispersion-guard rejects are the strongest immediate promotion candidates for controlled S05-compatible edge expansion.");
        sb.AppendLine();

        sb.AppendLine("RUN CONTEXT");
        sb.AppendLine("-----------");
        sb.AppendLine($"Run Timestamp (UTC)                : {runUtc:yyyy-MM-dd HH:mm:ss}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Selected Markets Count             : {selectedMarkets.Count}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Cash Allocation Weight             : {result.CashAllocationWeight:P2}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Positive Live Winner Count         : {liveWinners.Count}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Top 2 Winner Share                 : {top2WinnerShare:P2}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Dispersion Near-Winner Count       : {dispersionNearWinners.Count}");
        sb.AppendLine();

        sb.AppendLine("LIVE WINNER CLUSTER");
        sb.AppendLine("-------------------");
        if (liveWinners.Count == 0)
        {
            sb.AppendLine("NO POSITIVE LIVE WINNERS");
        }
        else
        {
            sb.AppendLine("Rank | Symbol::TF                | PnL");
            sb.AppendLine("-----+---------------------------+------------");
            int rank = 1;
            foreach (var kv in liveWinners.Take(10))
            {
                sb.AppendLine($"{rank,4} | {TrimTo(kv.Key, 25),-25} | {kv.Value,10:F2}");
                rank++;
            }
        }
        sb.AppendLine();

        sb.AppendLine("DISPERSION-GUARD PROMOTION TABLE");
        sb.AppendLine("-------------------------------");
        if (dispersionNearWinners.Count == 0)
        {
            sb.AppendLine("NO DISPERSION-GUARD NEAR-WINNERS FOUND");
        }
        else
        {
            sb.AppendLine("Rank | Market                    | WinnerSim | Promotion | RelFinalGap | RelPreGap | Promotion Verdict");
            sb.AppendLine("-----+---------------------------+-----------+-----------+-------------+-----------+------------------------------");
            int rank = 1;
            foreach (var row in dispersionNearWinners.Take(20))
            {
                sb.AppendLine(
                    $"{rank,4} | {TrimTo(row.MarketKey, 25),-25} | " +
                    $"{row.WinnerSimilarityScore,9:F2} | {row.PromotionScore,9:F2} | " +
                    $"{row.RelFinalGap,11:F4} | {row.RelPreGap,9:F4} | {TrimTo(row.PromotionVerdict, 28)}");
                rank++;
            }
        }
        sb.AppendLine();

        sb.AppendLine("TOP PROMOTION TARGETS");
        sb.AppendLine("---------------------");
        if (dispersionNearWinners.Count == 0)
        {
            sb.AppendLine("NO TOP PROMOTION TARGETS");
        }
        else
        {
            foreach (var row in dispersionNearWinners.Take(8))
            {
                sb.AppendLine(
                    $"{row.MarketKey,-24} " +
                    $"winnerSim={row.WinnerSimilarityScore:F2} " +
                    $"promotion={row.PromotionScore:F2} " +
                    $"relFinalGap={row.RelFinalGap:F4} " +
                    $"relPreGap={row.RelPreGap:F4} " +
                    $"=> {row.PromotionVerdict}");
            }
        }
        sb.AppendLine();

        sb.AppendLine("PROMOTION DECISION RULE");
        sb.AppendLine("-----------------------");
        sb.AppendLine("Promote only candidates that are:");
        sb.AppendLine("1) 4h");
        sb.AppendLine("2) blocked specifically by WaveB dispersion guard");
        sb.AppendLine("3) highly similar to current winner-style names");
        sb.AppendLine("4) very close on relative final/pre thresholds");
        sb.AppendLine();

        sb.AppendLine("FINAL VERDICT");
        sb.AppendLine("-------------");
        sb.AppendLine(BuildVerdict(dispersionNearWinners, liveWinners.Count, result.CashAllocationWeight));
        sb.AppendLine();

        sb.AppendLine("OPERATOR GUIDANCE");
        sb.AppendLine("-----------------");
        sb.AppendLine("1) If the top candidates score strongly here, next work should be a controlled promotion experiment.");
        sb.AppendLine("2) Promote dispersion near-winners before inventing a brand-new strategy family.");
        sb.AppendLine("3) If even the best dispersion rejects are weak, then move to true new-edge research.");
        sb.AppendLine();

        File.WriteAllText(path, sb.ToString());
    }

    private static PromotionRow BuildPromotionRow(
        string marketKey,
        string rejectionReason,
        IReadOnlySet selectedMarkets)
    {
        if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(marketKey))
            return PromotionRow.Empty;

        if (selectedMarkets.Contains(marketKey))
            return PromotionRow.Empty;

        string symbol = ExtractSymbol(marketKey);
        string timeframe = ExtractTimeframe(marketKey);

        bool is4h = timeframe.Equals("4h", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase);
        bool isPrioritySymbol = PromotionPrioritySymbols.Contains(symbol, StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase);

        decimal relFinalGap = ExtractMetricGap(rejectionReason, "relFinal=", "minFinal=");
        decimal relPreGap = ExtractMetricGap(rejectionReason, "relPre=", "minPre=");

        decimal winnerSimilarityScore = 0m;
        if (is4h) winnerSimilarityScore += 0.40m;
        if (isPrioritySymbol) winnerSimilarityScore += 0.30m;

        decimal closenessScore = 0m;
        closenessScore += Math.Max(0m, 0.20m - relFinalGap);
        closenessScore += Math.Max(0m, 0.20m - relPreGap);

        decimal promotionScore = winnerSimilarityScore + closenessScore;

        bool isRelevant = is4h;

        string verdict = BuildPromotionVerdict(relFinalGap, relPreGap, isPrioritySymbol);

        return new PromotionRow(
            marketKey,
            winnerSimilarityScore,
            promotionScore,
            relFinalGap,
            relPreGap,
            verdict,
            isRelevant);
    }

    private static string BuildPromotionVerdict(
        decimal relFinalGap,
        decimal relPreGap,
        bool isPrioritySymbol)
    {
        if (relFinalGap <= 0.03m && relPreGap <= 0.02m && isPrioritySymbol)
            return "Best immediate promotion candidate";

        if (relFinalGap <= 0.05m && relPreGap <= 0.03m)
            return "Strong controlled promotion candidate";

        if (relFinalGap <= 0.08m && relPreGap <= 0.05m)
            return "Secondary promotion candidate";

        return "Monitor only";
    }

    private static decimal ExtractMetricGap(
        string rejectionReason,
        string actualKey,
        string minKey)
    {
        decimal actual = ExtractMetric(rejectionReason, actualKey);
        decimal minimum = ExtractMetric(rejectionReason, minKey);

        if (minimum <= 0m)
            return 0m;

        return Math.Max(0m, minimum - actual);
    }

    private static decimal ExtractMetric(string text, string key)
    {
        if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(text) || string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(key))
            return 0m;

        int start = text.IndexOf(key, StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase);
        if (start < 0)
            return 0m;

        start += key.Length;
        int end = text.IndexOfAny([',', ')'], start);
        if (end < 0)
            end = text.Length;

        string raw = text[start..end].Trim();
        return decimal.TryParse(raw, out var value) ? value : 0m;
    }

    private static string BuildVerdict(
        IReadOnlyList rows,
        int liveWinnerCount,
        decimal cashWeight)
    {
        bool strongTargets = rows.Take(3).Any(x => x.PromotionScore >= 0.85m);

        if (liveWinnerCount <= 2 && cashWeight >= 0.75m && strongTargets)
            return "Dispersion-guard promotion is the next patch. The platform still has credible near-winners that should be tested before a brand-new edge family.";

        if (liveWinnerCount <= 2 && cashWeight >= 0.75m)
            return "Dispersion rejects exist, but not strongly enough. The next move may require true new-edge research.";

        return "Dispersion promotion is not the dominant next move in this run.";
    }

    private static string ExtractSymbol(string marketKey)
    {
        if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(marketKey))
            return string.Empty;

        var parts = marketKey.Split(new[] { "::" }, StringSplitOptions.None);
        return parts.Length >= 1 ? parts[0].Trim() : string.Empty;
    }

    private static string ExtractTimeframe(string marketKey)
    {
        if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(marketKey))
            return string.Empty;

        var parts = marketKey.Split(new[] { "::" }, StringSplitOptions.None);
        return parts.Length >= 2 ? parts[1].Trim() : string.Empty;
    }

    private static string TrimTo(string? text, int maxLen)
    {
        string value = text ?? string.Empty;
        if (value.Length <= maxLen)
            return value;

        if (maxLen <= 3)
            return value[..maxLen];

        return value[..(maxLen - 3)] + "...";
    }

    private sealed record PromotionRow(
        string MarketKey,
        decimal WinnerSimilarityScore,
        decimal PromotionScore,
        decimal RelFinalGap,
        decimal RelPreGap,
        string PromotionVerdict,
        bool IsRelevant)
    {
        public static PromotionRow Empty =>
            new(string.Empty, 0m, 0m, 0m, 0m, string.Empty, false);
    }
}

 = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = 
 
 using System.Text;
using TQGA.Application.Backtesting;
using TQGA.Application.Paths;

namespace TQGA.Application.Services;

public sealed class Report26TrueNewEdgeFamilyOpportunityAuditService
{
    private static readonly string[] EarlyTrendContinuationSymbols =
    [
        "FILUSDT",
        "DOTUSDT",
        "LINKUSDT",
        "NEARUSDT",
        "SOLUSDT",
        "ARBUSDT",
        "SUIUSDT"
    ];

    private static readonly string[] EmergingBreakoutSymbols =
    [
        "ARBUSDT",
        "SUIUSDT",
        "SEIUSDT",
        "JUPUSDT",
        "WIFUSDT",
        "INJUSDT",
        "TIAUSDT",
        "ORDIUSDT"
    ];

    private static readonly string[] LowerLiquidityContinuationSymbols =
    [
        "FETUSDT",
        "INJUSDT",
        "TIAUSDT",
        "ORDIUSDT",
        "SEIUSDT",
        "JUPUSDT",
        "WIFUSDT"
    ];

    public void GenerateAndWrite(
        PortfolioBacktestResult result,
        DateTime runUtc,
        IReadOnlyDictionary fitnessSnapshots)
    {
        ArgumentNullException.ThrowIfNull(result);
        ArgumentNullException.ThrowIfNull(fitnessSnapshots);

        Directory.CreateDirectory(DataPaths.Reports);

        string stamp = runUtc.ToString("yyyyMMdd_HHmmss");
        string path = Path.Combine(
            DataPaths.Reports,
            $"REPORT_26_TRUE_NEW_EDGE_FAMILY_OPPORTUNITY_AUDIT_{stamp}.txt");

        var sb = new StringBuilder();

        var strategyPnl = result.StrategyPnL ?? new Dictionary();
        var symbolTfPnl = result.SymbolTimeframePnL ?? new Dictionary(StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase);
        var rejections = result.MarketSelectionRejections ?? new Dictionary(StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase);
        var selectedMarkets = (result.SelectedMarkets ?? new List())
            .ToHashSet(StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase);

        decimal s05Pnl = strategyPnl.TryGetValue(5, out var foundS05Pnl)
            ? foundS05Pnl
            : 0m;

        string s05Code = ResolveStrategyCode(5, fitnessSnapshots);

        var liveWinners = symbolTfPnl
            .Where(x => x.Value > 0m)
            .OrderByDescending(x => x.Value)
            .ToList();

        var allRejected4h = rejections
            .Where(x => ExtractTimeframe(x.Key).Equals("4h", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase))
            .ToList();

        var familyRows = new List
        {
            BuildFamilyRow(
                "4H_EARLY_TREND_CONTINUATION",
                allRejected4h,
                EarlyTrendContinuationSymbols,
                selectedMarkets),

            BuildFamilyRow(
                "4H_EMERGING_BREAKOUT",
                allRejected4h,
                EmergingBreakoutSymbols,
                selectedMarkets),

            BuildFamilyRow(
                "4H_LOWER_LIQUIDITY_CONTINUATION",
                allRejected4h,
                LowerLiquidityContinuationSymbols,
                selectedMarkets)
        };

        var rankedFamilies = familyRows
            .OrderByDescending(x => x.OpportunityScore)
            .ThenByDescending(x => x.CandidateCount)
            .ThenBy(x => x.FamilyName, StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase)
            .ToList();

        sb.AppendLine("REPORT 26 — TRUE NEW EDGE FAMILY OPPORTUNITY AUDIT");
        sb.AppendLine("==================================================");
        sb.AppendLine();
        sb.AppendLine("PURPOSE");
        sb.AppendLine("-------");
        sb.AppendLine("Audit whether TQGA should continue admission tuning or move to a truly new edge family research direction.");
        sb.AppendLine();

        sb.AppendLine("RUN CONTEXT");
        sb.AppendLine("-----------");
        sb.AppendLine($"Run Timestamp (UTC)                : {runUtc:yyyy-MM-dd HH:mm:ss}");
        sb.AppendLine($"S05 Strategy Code                  : {s05Code}");
        sb.AppendLine($"S05 Strategy PnL                   : {s05Pnl:F2}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Selected Markets Count             : {selectedMarkets.Count}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Cash Allocation Weight             : {result.CashAllocationWeight:P2}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Positive Live Winner Count         : {liveWinners.Count}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Rejected 4h Candidate Count        : {allRejected4h.Count}");
        sb.AppendLine();

        sb.AppendLine("LIVE WINNER CLUSTER");
        sb.AppendLine("-------------------");
        if (liveWinners.Count == 0)
        {
            sb.AppendLine("NO POSITIVE LIVE WINNERS");
        }
        else
        {
            sb.AppendLine("Rank | Symbol::TF                | PnL");
            sb.AppendLine("-----+---------------------------+------------");
            int rank = 1;
            foreach (var kv in liveWinners.Take(10))
            {
                sb.AppendLine($"{rank,4} | {TrimTo(kv.Key, 25),-25} | {kv.Value,10:F2}");
                rank++;
            }
        }
        sb.AppendLine();

        sb.AppendLine("EDGE FAMILY OPPORTUNITY TABLE");
        sb.AppendLine("-----------------------------");
        sb.AppendLine("Rank | Edge Family                    | Candidates | Reason Mix Summary                    | Opportunity | Verdict");
        sb.AppendLine("-----+--------------------------------+------------+---------------------------------------+-------------+------------------------------");
        int familyRank = 1;
        foreach (var row in rankedFamilies)
        {
            sb.AppendLine(
                $"{familyRank,4} | {TrimTo(row.FamilyName, 30),-30} | {row.CandidateCount,10} | " +
                $"{TrimTo(row.ReasonMixSummary, 37),-37} | {row.OpportunityScore,11:F2} | {TrimTo(row.Verdict, 28)}");
            familyRank++;
        }
        sb.AppendLine();

        sb.AppendLine("TOP CANDIDATES BY FAMILY");
        sb.AppendLine("------------------------");
        foreach (var family in rankedFamilies)
        {
            sb.AppendLine($"FAMILY: {family.FamilyName}");
            if (family.TopCandidates.Count == 0)
            {
                sb.AppendLine("  NO TOP CANDIDATES");
                sb.AppendLine();
                continue;
            }

            int rank = 1;
            foreach (var candidate in family.TopCandidates.Take(8))
            {
                sb.AppendLine(
                    $"  {rank,2}. {candidate.MarketKey,-22} " +
                    $"bucket={candidate.ReasonBucket,-32} " +
                    $"score={candidate.CandidateScore:F2}");
                rank++;
            }

            sb.AppendLine();
        }

        sb.AppendLine("FINAL VERDICT");
        sb.AppendLine("-------------");
        sb.AppendLine(BuildVerdict(rankedFamilies, liveWinners.Count, result.CashAllocationWeight));
        sb.AppendLine();

        sb.AppendLine("OPERATOR GUIDANCE");
        sb.AppendLine("-----------------");
        sb.AppendLine("1) If one family clearly dominates here, next work should target that family specifically.");
        sb.AppendLine("2) If no family is compelling, stop admission tuning and consider a truly different alpha archetype.");
        sb.AppendLine("3) Prefer 4h-compatible families first because live winners remain concentrated in 4h.");
        sb.AppendLine();

        File.WriteAllText(path, sb.ToString());
    }

    private static EdgeFamilyRow BuildFamilyRow(
        string familyName,
        IReadOnlyList> rejected4h,
        IReadOnlyList familySymbols,
        IReadOnlySet selectedMarkets)
    {
        var candidates = rejected4h
            .Where(x =>
            {
                string symbol = ExtractSymbol(x.Key);
                return familySymbols.Contains(symbol, StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase)
                       && !selectedMarkets.Contains(x.Key);
            })
            .Select(x => BuildCandidateRow(x.Key, x.Value))
            .OrderByDescending(x => x.CandidateScore)
            .ThenBy(x => x.MarketKey, StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase)
            .ToList();

        string reasonMix = BuildReasonMixSummary(candidates);
        decimal opportunityScore = candidates.Count == 0
            ? 0m
            : candidates.Take(5).Sum(x => x.CandidateScore) / Math.Min(5, candidates.Count);

        string verdict = BuildFamilyVerdict(familyName, opportunityScore, candidates.Count);

        return new EdgeFamilyRow(
            familyName,
            candidates.Count,
            reasonMix,
            opportunityScore,
            verdict,
            candidates);
    }

    private static CandidateRow BuildCandidateRow(string marketKey, string rejectionReason)
    {
        string bucket = NormalizeReasonBucket(rejectionReason);
        decimal score = 0m;

        if (bucket == "WaveBRejected:DispersionGuard") score += 1.00m;
        else if (bucket == "REJECT: regime near-miss lane overflow") score += 0.85m;
        else if (bucket == "REJECT: liquidity tier-2 lane overflow") score += 0.80m;
        else if (bucket == "REJECT: regime not trend/high-vol-up") score += 0.60m;
        else if (bucket == "REJECT: low liquidity") score += 0.50m;
        else if (bucket == "REJECT: outside top leadership set") score += 0.45m;
        else score += 0.30m;

        return new CandidateRow(marketKey, bucket, score);
    }

    private static string NormalizeReasonBucket(string rejectionReason)
    {
        string value = rejectionReason?.Trim() ?? string.Empty;

        if (value.StartsWith("WaveBRejected:DispersionGuard", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase))
            return "WaveBRejected:DispersionGuard";

        if (value.StartsWith("REJECT: regime near-miss lane overflow", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase))
            return "REJECT: regime near-miss lane overflow";

        if (value.StartsWith("REJECT: liquidity tier-2 lane overflow", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase))
            return "REJECT: liquidity tier-2 lane overflow";

        if (value.StartsWith("REJECT: regime not trend/high-vol-up", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase))
            return "REJECT: regime not trend/high-vol-up";

        if (value.StartsWith("REJECT: low liquidity", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase))
            return "REJECT: low liquidity";

        if (value.StartsWith("REJECT: outside top", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase))
            return "REJECT: outside top leadership set";

        return value;
    }

    private static string BuildReasonMixSummary(IReadOnlyList candidates)
    {
        if (candidates.Count == 0)
            return "NO CANDIDATES";

        var parts = candidates
            .GroupBy(x => x.ReasonBucket)
            .OrderByDescending(g => g.Count())
            .ThenBy(g => g.Key, StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase)
            .Take(3)
            .Select(g => $"{g.Key}={g.Count()}")
            .ToList();

        return string.Join(" | ", parts);
    }

    private static string BuildFamilyVerdict(
        string familyName,
        decimal opportunityScore,
        int candidateCount)
    {
        if (candidateCount == 0)
            return "No opportunity";

        if (opportunityScore >= 0.90m)
            return "Best new-edge family";

        if (opportunityScore >= 0.75m)
            return "Strong research family";

        if (opportunityScore >= 0.60m)
            return "Secondary research family";

        return "Low-priority family";
    }

    private static string BuildVerdict(
        IReadOnlyList rankedFamilies,
        int liveWinnerCount,
        decimal cashWeight)
    {
        var best = rankedFamilies.FirstOrDefault();

        if (best == null)
            return "No new-edge family opportunity was identified in this run.";

        if (liveWinnerCount <= 1 && cashWeight >= 0.90m && best.OpportunityScore >= 0.75m)
        {
            return $"True new-edge research is now justified. The leading family is {best.FamilyName}.";
        }

        if (liveWinnerCount <= 2 && cashWeight >= 0.75m && best.OpportunityScore >= 0.60m)
        {
            return $"Controlled new-edge research is justified. Start with {best.FamilyName}.";
        }

        return "New-edge family opportunity is present but not decisive yet.";
    }

    private static string ResolveStrategyCode(
        int strategyId,
        IReadOnlyDictionary fitnessSnapshots)
    {
        if (fitnessSnapshots.TryGetValue(strategyId, out var snap) &&
            !string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(snap.StrategyCode))
        {
            return snap.StrategyCode;
        }

        return $"S{strategyId:00}";
    }

    private static string ExtractSymbol(string marketKey)
    {
        if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(marketKey))
            return string.Empty;

        var parts = marketKey.Split(new[] { "::" }, StringSplitOptions.None);
        return parts.Length >= 1 ? parts[0].Trim() : string.Empty;
    }

    private static string ExtractTimeframe(string marketKey)
    {
        if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(marketKey))
            return string.Empty;

        var parts = marketKey.Split(new[] { "::" }, StringSplitOptions.None);
        return parts.Length >= 2 ? parts[1].Trim() : string.Empty;
    }

    private static string TrimTo(string? text, int maxLen)
    {
        string value = text ?? string.Empty;
        if (value.Length <= maxLen)
            return value;

        if (maxLen <= 3)
            return value[..maxLen];

        return value[..(maxLen - 3)] + "...";
    }

    private sealed record CandidateRow(
        string MarketKey,
        string ReasonBucket,
        decimal CandidateScore);

    private sealed record EdgeFamilyRow(
        string FamilyName,
        int CandidateCount,
        string ReasonMixSummary,
        decimal OpportunityScore,
        string Verdict,
        IReadOnlyList TopCandidates);
}

 using System.Text;
using TQGA.Application.Backtesting;
using TQGA.Application.Paths;

namespace TQGA.Application.Services;

public sealed class Report27FourHourEarlyTrendContinuationFamilyDesignAuditService
{
    private static readonly string[] SeedSymbols =
    [
        "FILUSDT",
        "LINKUSDT",
        "NEARUSDT",
        "SOLUSDT",
        "SUIUSDT",
        "ARBUSDT",
        "DOTUSDT"
    ];

    public void GenerateAndWrite(
        PortfolioBacktestResult result,
        DateTime runUtc,
        IReadOnlyDictionary fitnessSnapshots)
    {
        ArgumentNullException.ThrowIfNull(result);
        ArgumentNullException.ThrowIfNull(fitnessSnapshots);

        Directory.CreateDirectory(DataPaths.Reports);

        string stamp = runUtc.ToString("yyyyMMdd_HHmmss");
        string path = Path.Combine(
            DataPaths.Reports,
            $"REPORT_27_4H_EARLY_TREND_CONTINUATION_FAMILY_DESIGN_AUDIT_{stamp}.txt");

        var sb = new StringBuilder();

        var strategyPnl = result.StrategyPnL ?? new Dictionary();
        var symbolTfPnl = result.SymbolTimeframePnL ?? new Dictionary(StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase);
        var rejections = result.MarketSelectionRejections ?? new Dictionary(StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase);
        var selectedMarkets = (result.SelectedMarkets ?? new List())
            .ToHashSet(StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase);

        decimal s05Pnl = strategyPnl.TryGetValue(5, out var foundS05Pnl)
            ? foundS05Pnl
            : 0m;

        string s05Code = ResolveStrategyCode(5, fitnessSnapshots);

        var liveWinners = symbolTfPnl
            .Where(x => x.Value > 0m)
            .OrderByDescending(x => x.Value)
            .ToList();

        var familyCandidates = rejections
            .Where(x => IsSeedMarket(x.Key))
            .Select(x => BuildCandidateRow(x.Key, x.Value, selectedMarkets))
            .Where(x => x.IsRelevant)
            .OrderByDescending(x => x.FamilyScore)
            .ThenByDescending(x => x.S05SimilarityScore)
            .ThenBy(x => x.MarketKey, StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase)
            .ToList();

        decimal top2WinnerShare = 0m;
        decimal totalWinnerPnl = liveWinners.Sum(x => x.Value);
        if (totalWinnerPnl != 0m)
            top2WinnerShare = liveWinners.Take(2).Sum(x => x.Value) / totalWinnerPnl;

        sb.AppendLine("REPORT 27 — 4H EARLY-TREND CONTINUATION FAMILY DESIGN AUDIT");
        sb.AppendLine("===========================================================");
        sb.AppendLine();
        sb.AppendLine("PURPOSE");
        sb.AppendLine("-------");
        sb.AppendLine("Design the next true edge family around 4h early-trend continuation candidates that are closest to current S05 winner structure.");
        sb.AppendLine();

        sb.AppendLine("RUN CONTEXT");
        sb.AppendLine("-----------");
        sb.AppendLine($"Run Timestamp (UTC)                : {runUtc:yyyy-MM-dd HH:mm:ss}");
        sb.AppendLine($"S05 Strategy Code                  : {s05Code}");
        sb.AppendLine($"S05 Strategy PnL                   : {s05Pnl:F2}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Selected Markets Count             : {selectedMarkets.Count}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Cash Allocation Weight             : {result.CashAllocationWeight:P2}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Positive Live Winner Count         : {liveWinners.Count}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Top 2 Winner Share                 : {top2WinnerShare:P2}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Family Candidate Count             : {familyCandidates.Count}");
        sb.AppendLine();

        sb.AppendLine("LIVE WINNER CLUSTER");
        sb.AppendLine("-------------------");
        if (liveWinners.Count == 0)
        {
            sb.AppendLine("NO POSITIVE LIVE WINNERS");
        }
        else
        {
            sb.AppendLine("Rank | Symbol::TF                | PnL");
            sb.AppendLine("-----+---------------------------+------------");
            int rank = 1;
            foreach (var kv in liveWinners.Take(10))
            {
                sb.AppendLine($"{rank,4} | {TrimTo(kv.Key, 25),-25} | {kv.Value,10:F2}");
                rank++;
            }
        }
        sb.AppendLine();

        sb.AppendLine("FAMILY DESIGN TARGETS");
        sb.AppendLine("---------------------");
        if (familyCandidates.Count == 0)
        {
            sb.AppendLine("NO 4H EARLY-TREND FAMILY CANDIDATES FOUND");
        }
        else
        {
            sb.AppendLine("Rank | Market                    | Bucket                           | S05Sim   | Family    | Design Verdict");
            sb.AppendLine("-----+---------------------------+----------------------------------+----------+-----------+------------------------------");
            int rank = 1;
            foreach (var row in familyCandidates.Take(20))
            {
                sb.AppendLine(
                    $"{rank,4} | {TrimTo(row.MarketKey, 25),-25} | {TrimTo(row.ReasonBucket, 32),-32} | " +
                    $"{row.S05SimilarityScore,8:F2} | {row.FamilyScore,9:F2} | {TrimTo(row.DesignVerdict, 28)}");
                rank++;
            }
        }
        sb.AppendLine();

        sb.AppendLine("TOP FAMILY STARTER SET");
        sb.AppendLine("----------------------");
        if (familyCandidates.Count == 0)
        {
            sb.AppendLine("NO STARTER SET AVAILABLE");
        }
        else
        {
            foreach (var row in familyCandidates.Take(6))
            {
                sb.AppendLine(
                    $"{row.MarketKey,-24} " +
                    $"bucket={row.ReasonBucket,-32} " +
                    $"s05Sim={row.S05SimilarityScore:F2} " +
                    $"family={row.FamilyScore:F2} " +
                    $"=> {row.DesignVerdict}");
            }
        }
        sb.AppendLine();

        sb.AppendLine("FAMILY DESIGN RULES");
        sb.AppendLine("-------------------");
        sb.AppendLine("1) 4h only");
        sb.AppendLine("2) Prefer WaveBRejected:DispersionGuard first");
        sb.AppendLine("3) Prefer regime-near-miss overflow second");
        sb.AppendLine("4) Avoid broad low-liquidity expansion in this family");
        sb.AppendLine("5) Use this family to reduce dependence on RNDRUSDT::4h, not to replace S05");
        sb.AppendLine();

        sb.AppendLine("INITIAL RESEARCH UNIVERSE");
        sb.AppendLine("-------------------------");
        foreach (string symbol in SeedSymbols)
            sb.AppendLine($"{symbol}::4h");

        sb.AppendLine();
        sb.AppendLine("FINAL VERDICT");
        sb.AppendLine("-------------");
        sb.AppendLine(BuildVerdict(familyCandidates, liveWinners.Count, result.CashAllocationWeight));
        sb.AppendLine();

        sb.AppendLine("OPERATOR GUIDANCE");
        sb.AppendLine("-----------------");
        sb.AppendLine("1) Next work should design one targeted family, not explode strategy count.");
        sb.AppendLine("2) Keep the family on 4h first.");
        sb.AppendLine("3) Expand the universe only around the top candidates listed here before considering 100-pair scale.");
        sb.AppendLine("4) Do not add another timeframe before validating this family.");
        sb.AppendLine();

        File.WriteAllText(path, sb.ToString());
    }

    private static bool IsSeedMarket(string marketKey)
    {
        if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(marketKey))
            return false;

        string symbol = ExtractSymbol(marketKey);
        string timeframe = ExtractTimeframe(marketKey);

        return timeframe.Equals("4h", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase)
               && SeedSymbols.Contains(symbol, StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase);
    }

    private static CandidateRow BuildCandidateRow(
        string marketKey,
        string rejectionReason,
        IReadOnlySet selectedMarkets)
    {
        if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(marketKey))
            return CandidateRow.Empty;

        if (selectedMarkets.Contains(marketKey))
            return CandidateRow.Empty;

        string reasonBucket = NormalizeReasonBucket(rejectionReason);

        decimal s05SimilarityScore = 0m;
        s05SimilarityScore += 0.50m; // 4h-only by design at this stage

        if (reasonBucket == "WaveBRejected:DispersionGuard") s05SimilarityScore += 0.35m;
        else if (reasonBucket == "REJECT: regime near-miss lane overflow") s05SimilarityScore += 0.22m;
        else if (reasonBucket == "REJECT: regime not trend/high-vol-up") s05SimilarityScore += 0.15m;
        else if (reasonBucket == "REJECT: outside top leadership set") s05SimilarityScore += 0.12m;
        else if (reasonBucket == "REJECT: low liquidity") s05SimilarityScore += 0.05m;

        decimal familyScore = s05SimilarityScore;

        bool isRelevant =
            reasonBucket == "WaveBRejected:DispersionGuard" ||
            reasonBucket == "REJECT: regime near-miss lane overflow" ||
            reasonBucket == "REJECT: regime not trend/high-vol-up" ||
            reasonBucket == "REJECT: outside top leadership set" ||
            reasonBucket == "REJECT: low liquidity";

        string verdict = BuildDesignVerdict(reasonBucket, familyScore);

        return new CandidateRow(
            marketKey,
            reasonBucket,
            s05SimilarityScore,
            familyScore,
            verdict,
            isRelevant);
    }

    private static string BuildDesignVerdict(string reasonBucket, decimal familyScore)
    {
        if (reasonBucket == "WaveBRejected:DispersionGuard" && familyScore >= 0.80m)
            return "Best family starter candidate";

        if (reasonBucket == "REJECT: regime near-miss lane overflow" && familyScore >= 0.70m)
            return "Strong secondary family candidate";

        if (reasonBucket == "REJECT: regime not trend/high-vol-up" && familyScore >= 0.60m)
            return "Watch for trend-transition inclusion";

        if (reasonBucket == "REJECT: outside top leadership set" && familyScore >= 0.60m)
            return "Borderline family candidate";

        return "Monitor only";
    }

    private static string NormalizeReasonBucket(string rejectionReason)
    {
        string value = rejectionReason?.Trim() ?? string.Empty;

        if (value.StartsWith("WaveBRejected:DispersionGuard", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase))
            return "WaveBRejected:DispersionGuard";

        if (value.StartsWith("REJECT: regime near-miss lane overflow", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase))
            return "REJECT: regime near-miss lane overflow";

        if (value.StartsWith("REJECT: regime not trend/high-vol-up", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase))
            return "REJECT: regime not trend/high-vol-up";

        if (value.StartsWith("REJECT: outside top", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase))
            return "REJECT: outside top leadership set";

        if (value.StartsWith("REJECT: low liquidity", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase))
            return "REJECT: low liquidity";

        return value;
    }

    private static string ResolveStrategyCode(
        int strategyId,
        IReadOnlyDictionary fitnessSnapshots)
    {
        if (fitnessSnapshots.TryGetValue(strategyId, out var snap) &&
            !string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(snap.StrategyCode))
        {
            return snap.StrategyCode;
        }

        return $"S{strategyId:00}";
    }

    private static string BuildVerdict(
        IReadOnlyList candidates,
        int liveWinnerCount,
        decimal cashWeight)
    {
        bool strongFamily = candidates.Take(3).Any(x => x.FamilyScore >= 0.75m);

        if (liveWinnerCount <= 1 && cashWeight >= 0.90m && strongFamily)
            return "Expand strategy family first. Build one new 4h early-trend continuation sleeve before expanding timeframe count or jumping to 100 pairs.";

        if (liveWinnerCount <= 2 && cashWeight >= 0.75m && strongFamily)
            return "A controlled 4h early-trend continuation family is justified. Keep universe expansion targeted and delay new timeframes.";

        return "Family opportunity exists but is not decisive yet.";
    }

    private static string ExtractSymbol(string marketKey)
    {
        if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(marketKey))
            return string.Empty;

        var parts = marketKey.Split(new[] { "::" }, StringSplitOptions.None);
        return parts.Length >= 1 ? parts[0].Trim() : string.Empty;
    }

    private static string ExtractTimeframe(string marketKey)
    {
        if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(marketKey))
            return string.Empty;

        var parts = marketKey.Split(new[] { "::" }, StringSplitOptions.None);
        return parts.Length >= 2 ? parts[1].Trim() : string.Empty;
    }

    private static string TrimTo(string? text, int maxLen)
    {
        string value = text ?? string.Empty;
        if (value.Length <= maxLen)
            return value;

        if (maxLen <= 3)
            return value[..maxLen];

        return value[..(maxLen - 3)] + "...";
    }

    private sealed record CandidateRow(
        string MarketKey,
        string ReasonBucket,
        decimal S05SimilarityScore,
        decimal FamilyScore,
        string DesignVerdict,
        bool IsRelevant)
    {
        public static CandidateRow Empty =>
            new(string.Empty, string.Empty, 0m, 0m, string.Empty, false);
    }
}

 using System.Text;
using TQGA.Application.Backtesting;
using TQGA.Application.Paths;

namespace TQGA.Application.Services;

public sealed class Report28FourHourEarlyTrendContinuationImplementationReadinessAuditService
{
    private static readonly string[] Phase1StarterSymbols =
    [
        "FILUSDT",
        "LINKUSDT",
        "NEARUSDT",
        "SOLUSDT",
        "SUIUSDT",
        "ARBUSDT",
        "DOTUSDT"
    ];

    public void GenerateAndWrite(
        PortfolioBacktestResult result,
        DateTime runUtc,
        IReadOnlyDictionary fitnessSnapshots)
    {
        ArgumentNullException.ThrowIfNull(result);
        ArgumentNullException.ThrowIfNull(fitnessSnapshots);

        Directory.CreateDirectory(DataPaths.Reports);

        string stamp = runUtc.ToString("yyyyMMdd_HHmmss");
        string path = Path.Combine(
            DataPaths.Reports,
            $"REPORT_28_4H_EARLY_TREND_CONTINUATION_IMPLEMENTATION_READINESS_AUDIT_{stamp}.txt");

        var sb = new StringBuilder();

        var strategyPnl = result.StrategyPnL ?? new Dictionary();
        var symbolTfPnl = result.SymbolTimeframePnL ?? new Dictionary(StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase);
        var rejections = result.MarketSelectionRejections ?? new Dictionary(StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase);
        var selectedMarkets = (result.SelectedMarkets ?? new List())
            .ToHashSet(StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase);

        decimal s05Pnl = strategyPnl.TryGetValue(5, out var foundS05Pnl)
            ? foundS05Pnl
            : 0m;

        string s05Code = ResolveStrategyCode(5, fitnessSnapshots);

        var liveWinners = symbolTfPnl
            .Where(x => x.Value > 0m)
            .OrderByDescending(x => x.Value)
            .ToList();

        var implementationRows = rejections
            .Where(x => IsStarterMarket(x.Key))
            .Select(x => BuildImplementationRow(x.Key, x.Value, selectedMarkets))
            .Where(x => x.IsRelevant)
            .OrderByDescending(x => x.ReadinessScore)
            .ThenByDescending(x => x.FamilyFitScore)
            .ThenBy(x => x.MarketKey, StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase)
            .ToList();

        decimal totalWinnerPnl = liveWinners.Sum(x => x.Value);
        decimal top2WinnerShare = totalWinnerPnl == 0m
            ? 0m
            : liveWinners.Take(2).Sum(x => x.Value) / totalWinnerPnl;

        sb.AppendLine("REPORT 28 — 4H EARLY-TREND CONTINUATION IMPLEMENTATION READINESS AUDIT");
        sb.AppendLine("======================================================================");
        sb.AppendLine();
        sb.AppendLine("PURPOSE");
        sb.AppendLine("-------");
        sb.AppendLine("Determine whether the new 4h early-trend continuation family is ready for controlled implementation, and define the exact phase-1 starter set.");
        sb.AppendLine();

        sb.AppendLine("RUN CONTEXT");
        sb.AppendLine("-----------");
        sb.AppendLine($"Run Timestamp (UTC)                : {runUtc:yyyy-MM-dd HH:mm:ss}");
        sb.AppendLine($"S05 Strategy Code                  : {s05Code}");
        sb.AppendLine($"S05 Strategy PnL                   : {s05Pnl:F2}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Selected Markets Count             : {selectedMarkets.Count}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Cash Allocation Weight             : {result.CashAllocationWeight:P2}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Positive Live Winner Count         : {liveWinners.Count}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Top 2 Winner Share                 : {top2WinnerShare:P2}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Implementation Candidate Count     : {implementationRows.Count}");
        sb.AppendLine();

        sb.AppendLine("LIVE WINNER CLUSTER");
        sb.AppendLine("-------------------");
        if (liveWinners.Count == 0)
        {
            sb.AppendLine("NO POSITIVE LIVE WINNERS");
        }
        else
        {
            sb.AppendLine("Rank | Symbol::TF                | PnL");
            sb.AppendLine("-----+---------------------------+------------");
            int rank = 1;
            foreach (var kv in liveWinners.Take(10))
            {
                sb.AppendLine($"{rank,4} | {TrimTo(kv.Key, 25),-25} | {kv.Value,10:F2}");
                rank++;
            }
        }
        sb.AppendLine();

        sb.AppendLine("IMPLEMENTATION READINESS TABLE");
        sb.AppendLine("------------------------------");
        if (implementationRows.Count == 0)
        {
            sb.AppendLine("NO IMPLEMENTATION CANDIDATES FOUND");
        }
        else
        {
            sb.AppendLine("Rank | Market                    | Bucket                           | FamilyFit | ReadyScore | Phase Recommendation");
            sb.AppendLine("-----+---------------------------+----------------------------------+-----------+------------+------------------------------");
            int rank = 1;
            foreach (var row in implementationRows.Take(20))
            {
                sb.AppendLine(
                    $"{rank,4} | {TrimTo(row.MarketKey, 25),-25} | {TrimTo(row.ReasonBucket, 32),-32} | " +
                    $"{row.FamilyFitScore,9:F2} | {row.ReadinessScore,10:F2} | {TrimTo(row.PhaseRecommendation, 28)}");
                rank++;
            }
        }
        sb.AppendLine();

        sb.AppendLine("PHASE-1 STARTER SET");
        sb.AppendLine("-------------------");
        if (implementationRows.Count == 0)
        {
            sb.AppendLine("NO PHASE-1 STARTER SET AVAILABLE");
        }
        else
        {
            foreach (var row in implementationRows.Take(4))
            {
                sb.AppendLine(
                    $"{row.MarketKey,-24} " +
                    $"bucket={row.ReasonBucket,-32} " +
                    $"fit={row.FamilyFitScore:F2} " +
                    $"ready={row.ReadinessScore:F2} " +
                    $"=> {row.PhaseRecommendation}");
            }
        }
        sb.AppendLine();

        sb.AppendLine("PHASE-2 WATCHLIST");
        sb.AppendLine("-----------------");
        if (implementationRows.Count <= 4)
        {
            sb.AppendLine("NO PHASE-2 WATCHLIST");
        }
        else
        {
            foreach (var row in implementationRows.Skip(4).Take(4))
            {
                sb.AppendLine(
                    $"{row.MarketKey,-24} " +
                    $"bucket={row.ReasonBucket,-32} " +
                    $"fit={row.FamilyFitScore:F2} " +
                    $"ready={row.ReadinessScore:F2} " +
                    $"=> {row.PhaseRecommendation}");
            }
        }
        sb.AppendLine();

        sb.AppendLine("IMPLEMENTATION RULES");
        sb.AppendLine("--------------------");
        sb.AppendLine("1) Keep the new family on 4h only.");
        sb.AppendLine("2) Start with a small phase-1 family set before broad universe expansion.");
        sb.AppendLine("3) Do not expand to 60 pairs first.");
        sb.AppendLine("4) Do not add another timeframe first.");
        sb.AppendLine("5) Use this family to reduce dependence on RNDRUSDT::4h and improve deployable breadth.");
        sb.AppendLine();

        sb.AppendLine("FINAL VERDICT");
        sb.AppendLine("-------------");
        sb.AppendLine(BuildVerdict(implementationRows, liveWinners.Count, result.CashAllocationWeight));
        sb.AppendLine();

        sb.AppendLine("OPERATOR GUIDANCE");
        sb.AppendLine("-----------------");
        sb.AppendLine("1) If the top 3-4 names score strongly here, implement the new family before expanding to 60 pairs.");
        sb.AppendLine("2) After the family is live, expand the universe only around the best family names.");
        sb.AppendLine("3) Delay new timeframe expansion until the family proves it can create a second and third monetized survivor.");
        sb.AppendLine();

        File.WriteAllText(path, sb.ToString());
    }

    private static bool IsStarterMarket(string marketKey)
    {
        if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(marketKey))
            return false;

        string symbol = ExtractSymbol(marketKey);
        string timeframe = ExtractTimeframe(marketKey);

        return timeframe.Equals("4h", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase)
               && Phase1StarterSymbols.Contains(symbol, StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase);
    }

    private static ImplementationRow BuildImplementationRow(
        string marketKey,
        string rejectionReason,
        IReadOnlySet selectedMarkets)
    {
        if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(marketKey))
            return ImplementationRow.Empty;

        if (selectedMarkets.Contains(marketKey))
            return ImplementationRow.Empty;

        string reasonBucket = NormalizeReasonBucket(rejectionReason);

        decimal familyFitScore = 0.50m; // 4h starter universe by design

        if (reasonBucket == "WaveBRejected:DispersionGuard") familyFitScore += 0.35m;
        else if (reasonBucket == "REJECT: regime near-miss lane overflow") familyFitScore += 0.22m;
        else if (reasonBucket == "REJECT: regime not trend/high-vol-up") familyFitScore += 0.15m;
        else if (reasonBucket == "REJECT: outside top leadership set") familyFitScore += 0.12m;
        else if (reasonBucket == "REJECT: low liquidity") familyFitScore += 0.05m;

        decimal readinessScore = familyFitScore;

        bool isRelevant =
            reasonBucket == "WaveBRejected:DispersionGuard" ||
            reasonBucket == "REJECT: regime near-miss lane overflow" ||
            reasonBucket == "REJECT: regime not trend/high-vol-up" ||
            reasonBucket == "REJECT: outside top leadership set" ||
            reasonBucket == "REJECT: low liquidity";

        string phaseRecommendation = BuildPhaseRecommendation(reasonBucket, readinessScore);

        return new ImplementationRow(
            marketKey,
            reasonBucket,
            familyFitScore,
            readinessScore,
            phaseRecommendation,
            isRelevant);
    }

    private static string BuildPhaseRecommendation(string reasonBucket, decimal readinessScore)
    {
        if (reasonBucket == "WaveBRejected:DispersionGuard" && readinessScore >= 0.80m)
            return "Phase 1 implementation";

        if (reasonBucket == "REJECT: regime near-miss lane overflow" && readinessScore >= 0.70m)
            return "Phase 1 secondary implementation";

        if (reasonBucket == "REJECT: regime not trend/high-vol-up" && readinessScore >= 0.60m)
            return "Phase 2 watchlist";

        if (reasonBucket == "REJECT: outside top leadership set" && readinessScore >= 0.60m)
            return "Phase 2 watchlist";

        return "Monitor only";
    }

    private static string NormalizeReasonBucket(string rejectionReason)
    {
        string value = rejectionReason?.Trim() ?? string.Empty;

        if (value.StartsWith("WaveBRejected:DispersionGuard", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase))
            return "WaveBRejected:DispersionGuard";

        if (value.StartsWith("REJECT: regime near-miss lane overflow", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase))
            return "REJECT: regime near-miss lane overflow";

        if (value.StartsWith("REJECT: regime not trend/high-vol-up", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase))
            return "REJECT: regime not trend/high-vol-up";

        if (value.StartsWith("REJECT: outside top", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase))
            return "REJECT: outside top leadership set";

        if (value.StartsWith("REJECT: low liquidity", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase))
            return "REJECT: low liquidity";

        return value;
    }

    private static string ResolveStrategyCode(
        int strategyId,
        IReadOnlyDictionary fitnessSnapshots)
    {
        if (fitnessSnapshots.TryGetValue(strategyId, out var snap) &&
            !string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(snap.StrategyCode))
        {
            return snap.StrategyCode;
        }

        return $"S{strategyId:00}";
    }

    private static string BuildVerdict(
        IReadOnlyList rows,
        int liveWinnerCount,
        decimal cashWeight)
    {
        bool strongReadiness = rows.Take(4).Any(x => x.ReadinessScore >= 0.75m);

        if (liveWinnerCount <= 1 && cashWeight >= 0.90m && strongReadiness)
            return "Implement the new 4h early-trend continuation family first. Do not expand to 60 pairs before validating the family.";

        if (liveWinnerCount <= 2 && cashWeight >= 0.75m && strongReadiness)
            return "The new family is ready for controlled implementation. Keep the universe targeted and delay 60-pair expansion.";

        return "Implementation readiness is not decisive yet.";
    }

    private static string ExtractSymbol(string marketKey)
    {
        if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(marketKey))
            return string.Empty;

        var parts = marketKey.Split(new[] { "::" }, StringSplitOptions.None);
        return parts.Length >= 1 ? parts[0].Trim() : string.Empty;
    }

    private static string ExtractTimeframe(string marketKey)
    {
        if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(marketKey))
            return string.Empty;

        var parts = marketKey.Split(new[] { "::" }, StringSplitOptions.None);
        return parts.Length >= 2 ? parts[1].Trim() : string.Empty;
    }

    private static string TrimTo(string? text, int maxLen)
    {
        string value = text ?? string.Empty;
        if (value.Length <= maxLen)
            return value;

        if (maxLen <= 3)
            return value[..maxLen];

        return value[..(maxLen - 3)] + "...";
    }

    private sealed record ImplementationRow(
        string MarketKey,
        string ReasonBucket,
        decimal FamilyFitScore,
        decimal ReadinessScore,
        string PhaseRecommendation,
        bool IsRelevant)
    {
        public static ImplementationRow Empty =>
            new(string.Empty, string.Empty, 0m, 0m, string.Empty, false);
    }
}
