 using System.Text;
using TQGA.Application.Backtesting;
using TQGA.Application.Paths;

namespace TQGA.Application.Services;

public sealed class Report29S06EarlyTrendFamilyContributionNearSurvivorAuditService
{
    private const int TargetStrategyId = 6;
    private const string TargetStrategyCodeFallback = "FourHourEarlyTrendContinuationQuantStrategy";
    private const string TargetPrefix = "S06::";

    private static readonly string[] Phase1StarterSymbols =
    [
        "FILUSDT",
        "LINKUSDT",
        "NEARUSDT"
    ];

    private static readonly string[] Phase2WatchlistSymbols =
    [
        "SOLUSDT",
        "SUIUSDT",
        "ARBUSDT",
        "DOTUSDT"
    ];

    public void GenerateAndWrite(
        PortfolioBacktestResult result,
        DateTime runUtc,
        IReadOnlyDictionary fitnessSnapshots)
    {
        ArgumentNullException.ThrowIfNull(result);
        ArgumentNullException.ThrowIfNull(fitnessSnapshots);

        Directory.CreateDirectory(DataPaths.Reports);

        string stamp = runUtc.ToString("yyyyMMdd_HHmmss");
        string path = Path.Combine(
            DataPaths.Reports,
            $"REPORT_29_S06_EARLY_TREND_FAMILY_CONTRIBUTION_NEAR_SURVIVOR_AUDIT_{stamp}.txt");

        var sb = new StringBuilder();

        var strategyPnl = result.StrategyPnL ?? new Dictionary();
        var symbolTfPnl = result.SymbolTimeframePnL ?? new Dictionary(StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase);
        var strategySymbolTfPnl = result.StrategySymbolTimeframePnL ?? new Dictionary(StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase);
        var rejections = result.MarketSelectionRejections ?? new Dictionary(StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase);
        var selectedMarkets = (result.SelectedMarkets ?? new List())
            .ToHashSet(StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase);

        decimal s06Pnl = strategyPnl.TryGetValue(TargetStrategyId, out var foundS06Pnl)
            ? foundS06Pnl
            : 0m;

        string s06Code = ResolveStrategyCode(TargetStrategyId, fitnessSnapshots);

        var s06Rows = strategySymbolTfPnl
            .Where(x => x.Key.StartsWith(TargetPrefix, StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase))
            .OrderByDescending(x => x.Value)
            .ToList();

        var s06ContributionRows = s06Rows
            .Select(x => BuildContributionRow(x.Key, x.Value, selectedMarkets, rejections))
            .OrderByDescending(x => x.NetPnl)
            .ThenBy(x => x.MarketKey, StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase)
            .ToList();

        var positiveS06Rows = s06ContributionRows
            .Where(x => x.NetPnl > 0m)
            .ToList();

        var nearSurvivorRows = s06ContributionRows
            .Where(x => x.IsPhase1OrPhase2 && !x.IsSelectedNow)
            .OrderByDescending(x => x.NearSurvivorScore)
            .ThenByDescending(x => x.NetPnl)
            .ThenBy(x => x.MarketKey, StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase)
            .ToList();

        decimal totalPositiveS06Pnl = positiveS06Rows.Sum(x => x.NetPnl);
        decimal top1PositiveShare = totalPositiveS06Pnl == 0m
            ? 0m
            : positiveS06Rows.Take(1).Sum(x => x.NetPnl) / totalPositiveS06Pnl;

        decimal top2PositiveShare = totalPositiveS06Pnl == 0m
            ? 0m
            : positiveS06Rows.Take(2).Sum(x => x.NetPnl) / totalPositiveS06Pnl;

        sb.AppendLine("REPORT 29 — S06 EARLY-TREND FAMILY CONTRIBUTION / NEAR-SURVIVOR AUDIT");
        sb.AppendLine("=====================================================================");
        sb.AppendLine();
        sb.AppendLine("PURPOSE");
        sb.AppendLine("-------");
        sb.AppendLine("Audit how the new S06 early-trend family actually contributed in the first live run, and determine whether any phase-1 or phase-2 family symbols are close to becoming true deployable survivors.");
        sb.AppendLine();

        sb.AppendLine("RUN CONTEXT");
        sb.AppendLine("-----------");
        sb.AppendLine($"Run Timestamp (UTC)                : {runUtc:yyyy-MM-dd HH:mm:ss}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Target Strategy Id                 : S{TargetStrategyId:00}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Target Strategy Code               : {s06Code}");
        sb.AppendLine($"S06 Total PnL                      : {s06Pnl:F2}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Selected Markets Count             : {selectedMarkets.Count}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Cash Allocation Weight             : {result.CashAllocationWeight:P2}");
        sb.AppendLine($"S06 Contribution Rows              : {s06ContributionRows.Count}");
        sb.AppendLine($"S06 Positive Contribution Rows     : {positiveS06Rows.Count}");
        sb.AppendLine();

        sb.AppendLine("LIVE TOP SYMBOL::TF PNL");
        sb.AppendLine("-----------------------");
        if (symbolTfPnl.Count == 0)
        {
            sb.AppendLine("NO SYMBOL::TF PNL DATA");
        }
        else
        {
            sb.AppendLine("Rank | Symbol::TF                | PnL");
            sb.AppendLine("-----+---------------------------+------------");
            int rank = 1;
            foreach (var kv in symbolTfPnl.OrderByDescending(x => x.Value).Take(12))
            {
                sb.AppendLine($"{rank,4} | {TrimTo(kv.Key, 25),-25} | {kv.Value,10:F2}");
                rank++;
            }
        }
        sb.AppendLine();

        sb.AppendLine("S06 FAMILY CONTRIBUTION TABLE");
        sb.AppendLine("-----------------------------");
        if (s06ContributionRows.Count == 0)
        {
            sb.AppendLine("NO S06 CONTRIBUTION ROWS");
        }
        else
        {
            sb.AppendLine("Rank | Market                    | NetPnL     | Bucket                           | SelectedNow | FamilyTier | NearSurvivor");
            sb.AppendLine("-----+---------------------------+------------+----------------------------------+-------------+-----------+-------------");
            int rank = 1;
            foreach (var row in s06ContributionRows)
            {
                sb.AppendLine(
                    $"{rank,4} | {TrimTo(row.MarketKey, 25),-25} | {row.NetPnl,10:F2} | " +
                    $"{TrimTo(row.ReasonBucket, 32),-32} | {(row.IsSelectedNow ? "YES" : "NO "),11} | " +
                    $"{row.FamilyTier,-9} | {row.NearSurvivorScore,11:F2}");
                rank++;
            }
        }
        sb.AppendLine();

        sb.AppendLine("S06 POSITIVE CONTRIBUTION CONCENTRATION");
        sb.AppendLine("---------------------------------------");
        sb.AppendLine($"Top 1 Positive Share                  : {top1PositiveShare:P2}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Top 2 Positive Share                  : {top2PositiveShare:P2}");
        sb.AppendLine();

        sb.AppendLine("PHASE-1 STARTER SYMBOLS");
        sb.AppendLine("-----------------------");
        foreach (string symbol in Phase1StarterSymbols)
        {
            string marketKey = $"{symbol}::4h";
            var row = s06ContributionRows.FirstOrDefault(x => x.MarketKey.Equals(marketKey, StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase));
            if (row == null)
            {
                sb.AppendLine($"{marketKey,-20} NO S06 CONTRIBUTION ROW");
            }
            else
            {
                sb.AppendLine($"{marketKey,-20} pnl={row.NetPnl,10:F2} bucket={row.ReasonBucket,-32} selected={(row.IsSelectedNow ? "YES" : "NO")}");
            }
        }
        sb.AppendLine();

        sb.AppendLine("PHASE-2 WATCHLIST SYMBOLS");
        sb.AppendLine("-------------------------");
        foreach (string symbol in Phase2WatchlistSymbols)
        {
            string marketKey = $"{symbol}::4h";
            var row = s06ContributionRows.FirstOrDefault(x => x.MarketKey.Equals(marketKey, StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase));
            if (row == null)
            {
                sb.AppendLine($"{marketKey,-20} NO S06 CONTRIBUTION ROW");
            }
            else
            {
                sb.AppendLine($"{marketKey,-20} pnl={row.NetPnl,10:F2} bucket={row.ReasonBucket,-32} selected={(row.IsSelectedNow ? "YES" : "NO")}");
            }
        }
        sb.AppendLine();

        sb.AppendLine("TOP S06 NEAR-SURVIVORS");
        sb.AppendLine("----------------------");
        if (nearSurvivorRows.Count == 0)
        {
            sb.AppendLine("NO S06 NEAR-SURVIVORS FOUND");
        }
        else
        {
            sb.AppendLine("Rank | Market                    | NetPnL     | FamilyTier | Bucket                           | NearSurvivor Verdict");
            sb.AppendLine("-----+---------------------------+------------+-----------+----------------------------------+------------------------------");
            int rank = 1;
            foreach (var row in nearSurvivorRows.Take(10))
            {
                sb.AppendLine(
                    $"{rank,4} | {TrimTo(row.MarketKey, 25),-25} | {row.NetPnl,10:F2} | " +
                    $"{row.FamilyTier,-9} | {TrimTo(row.ReasonBucket, 32),-32} | {TrimTo(row.NearSurvivorVerdict, 28)}");
                rank++;
            }
        }
        sb.AppendLine();

        sb.AppendLine("S06 OPERATOR INTERPRETATION");
        sb.AppendLine("---------------------------");
        sb.AppendLine("1) If S06 is positive but still tiny, the family is alive but not yet validated for broader universe expansion.");
        sb.AppendLine("2) If one of the phase-1 names shows the best near-survivor score, keep the universe narrow and refine there first.");
        sb.AppendLine("3) Only broaden the universe after S06 produces a credible second deployable survivor or materially reduces cash held.");
        sb.AppendLine();

        sb.AppendLine("FINAL VERDICT");
        sb.AppendLine("-------------");
        sb.AppendLine(BuildVerdict(
            s06Pnl,
            nearSurvivorRows,
            selectedMarkets.Count,
            result.CashAllocationWeight));
        sb.AppendLine();

        File.WriteAllText(path, sb.ToString());
    }

    private static ContributionRow BuildContributionRow(
        string strategySymbolTfKey,
        decimal netPnl,
        IReadOnlySet selectedMarkets,
        IReadOnlyDictionary rejections)
    {
        string marketKey = ExtractMarketKey(strategySymbolTfKey);
        bool isSelectedNow = selectedMarkets.Contains(marketKey);

        string reasonBucket = "NOT_REJECTED";
        if (!isSelectedNow && rejections.TryGetValue(marketKey, out var rejectReason))
            reasonBucket = NormalizeReasonBucket(rejectReason);

        string familyTier = ResolveFamilyTier(marketKey);

        decimal nearSurvivorScore = 0m;

        if (netPnl > 0m)
            nearSurvivorScore += 0.50m;

        if (familyTier == "PHASE_1")
            nearSurvivorScore += 0.30m;
        else if (familyTier == "PHASE_2")
            nearSurvivorScore += 0.15m;

        if (reasonBucket == "NOT_REJECTED" && isSelectedNow)
            nearSurvivorScore += 0.50m;
        else if (reasonBucket == "WaveBRejected:DispersionGuard")
            nearSurvivorScore += 0.28m;
        else if (reasonBucket == "REJECT: outside top leadership set")
            nearSurvivorScore += 0.20m;
        else if (reasonBucket == "REJECT: regime near-miss lane overflow")
            nearSurvivorScore += 0.18m;
        else if (reasonBucket == "REJECT: regime not trend/high-vol-up")
            nearSurvivorScore += 0.12m;
        else if (reasonBucket == "REJECT: low liquidity")
            nearSurvivorScore += 0.08m;

        bool isPhase1OrPhase2 = familyTier != "OUTSIDE_FAMILY";
        string verdict = BuildNearSurvivorVerdict(isSelectedNow, familyTier, reasonBucket, netPnl, nearSurvivorScore);

        return new ContributionRow(
            marketKey,
            netPnl,
            reasonBucket,
            isSelectedNow,
            familyTier,
            nearSurvivorScore,
            verdict,
            isPhase1OrPhase2);
    }

    private static string BuildNearSurvivorVerdict(
        bool isSelectedNow,
        string familyTier,
        string reasonBucket,
        decimal netPnl,
        decimal nearSurvivorScore)
    {
        if (isSelectedNow)
            return "Already deployable survivor";

        if (familyTier == "PHASE_1" && netPnl > 0m && reasonBucket == "WaveBRejected:DispersionGuard" && nearSurvivorScore >= 1.00m)
            return "Best phase-1 near-survivor";

        if (familyTier == "PHASE_1" && netPnl > 0m && nearSurvivorScore >= 0.85m)
            return "Strong phase-1 near-survivor";

        if (familyTier == "PHASE_2" && netPnl > 0m && nearSurvivorScore >= 0.70m)
            return "Phase-2 watchlist near-survivor";

        if (netPnl > 0m)
            return "Positive but not close enough";

        return "Not yet a credible survivor";
    }

    private static string ResolveFamilyTier(string marketKey)
    {
        string symbol = ExtractSymbol(marketKey);

        if (Phase1StarterSymbols.Contains(symbol, StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase))
            return "PHASE_1";

        if (Phase2WatchlistSymbols.Contains(symbol, StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase))
            return "PHASE_2";

        return "OUTSIDE_FAMILY";
    }

    private static string NormalizeReasonBucket(string rejectionReason)
    {
        string value = rejectionReason?.Trim() ?? string.Empty;

        if (value.StartsWith("WaveBRejected:DispersionGuard", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase))
            return "WaveBRejected:DispersionGuard";

        if (value.StartsWith("WaveBRejected:BelowThreshold", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase))
            return "WaveBRejected:BelowThreshold";

        if (value.StartsWith("WaveBRejected:PerSymbolCap", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase))
            return "WaveBRejected:PerSymbolCap";

        if (value.StartsWith("WaveBRejected:TopNOverflow", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase))
            return "WaveBRejected:TopNOverflow";

        if (value.StartsWith("REJECT: outside top", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase))
            return "REJECT: outside top leadership set";

        if (value.StartsWith("REJECT: regime near-miss lane overflow", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase))
            return "REJECT: regime near-miss lane overflow";

        if (value.StartsWith("REJECT: regime not trend/high-vol-up", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase))
            return "REJECT: regime not trend/high-vol-up";

        if (value.StartsWith("REJECT: low liquidity", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase))
            return "REJECT: low liquidity";

        return value;
    }

    private static string ExtractMarketKey(string strategySymbolTfKey)
    {
        if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(strategySymbolTfKey))
            return string.Empty;

        var parts = strategySymbolTfKey.Split(new[] { "::" }, StringSplitOptions.None);
        if (parts.Length < 3)
            return strategySymbolTfKey;

        return $"{parts[1]}::{parts[2]}";
    }

    private static string ExtractSymbol(string marketKey)
    {
        if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(marketKey))
            return string.Empty;

        var parts = marketKey.Split(new[] { "::" }, StringSplitOptions.None);
        return parts.Length >= 1 ? parts[0].Trim() : string.Empty;
    }

    private static string ResolveStrategyCode(
        int strategyId,
        IReadOnlyDictionary fitnessSnapshots)
    {
        if (fitnessSnapshots.TryGetValue(strategyId, out var snap) &&
            !string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(snap.StrategyCode))
        {
            return snap.StrategyCode;
        }

        return TargetStrategyCodeFallback;
    }

    private static string BuildVerdict(
        decimal s06Pnl,
        IReadOnlyList nearSurvivorRows,
        int selectedMarketCount,
        decimal cashWeight)
    {
        bool strongNearSurvivor = nearSurvivorRows.Take(3).Any(x => x.NearSurvivorScore >= 0.90m && x.NetPnl > 0m);

        if (selectedMarketCount <= 1 && cashWeight >= 0.90m && s06Pnl > 0m && strongNearSurvivor)
            return "S06 is alive and has a credible near-survivor candidate, but broader universe expansion is still premature. Refine inside the current family first.";

        if (selectedMarketCount <= 1 && cashWeight >= 0.90m && s06Pnl > 0m)
            return "S06 is positive but still too weak to justify broader universe expansion. Keep the family narrow and refine contribution quality first.";

        if (s06Pnl <= 0m)
            return "S06 has not yet proven contribution quality. Broader universe expansion is not justified.";

        return "S06 contribution is improving, but broader universe expansion still requires a clearer second deployable survivor.";
    }

    private static string TrimTo(string? text, int maxLen)
    {
        string value = text ?? string.Empty;
        if (value.Length <= maxLen)
            return value;

        if (maxLen <= 3)
            return value[..maxLen];

        return value[..(maxLen - 3)] + "...";
    }

    private sealed record ContributionRow(
        string MarketKey,
        decimal NetPnl,
        string ReasonBucket,
        bool IsSelectedNow,
        string FamilyTier,
        decimal NearSurvivorScore,
        string NearSurvivorVerdict,
        bool IsPhase1OrPhase2);
}

 using System.Text;
using TQGA.Application.Backtesting;
using TQGA.Application.Paths;

namespace TQGA.Application.Services;

public sealed class Report30S06Phase1RefinementEntryTighteningAuditService
{
    private const int TargetStrategyId = 6;
    private const string TargetPrefix = "S06::";

    private static readonly string[] Phase1StarterSymbols =
    [
        "FILUSDT",
        "LINKUSDT",
        "NEARUSDT"
    ];

    private static readonly string[] Phase2WatchlistSymbols =
    [
        "SOLUSDT",
        "SUIUSDT",
        "ARBUSDT",
        "DOTUSDT"
    ];

    public void GenerateAndWrite(
        PortfolioBacktestResult result,
        DateTime runUtc,
        IReadOnlyDictionary fitnessSnapshots)
    {
        ArgumentNullException.ThrowIfNull(result);
        ArgumentNullException.ThrowIfNull(fitnessSnapshots);

        Directory.CreateDirectory(DataPaths.Reports);

        string stamp = runUtc.ToString("yyyyMMdd_HHmmss");
        string path = Path.Combine(
            DataPaths.Reports,
            $"REPORT_30_S06_PHASE1_REFINEMENT_ENTRY_TIGHTENING_AUDIT_{stamp}.txt");

        var sb = new StringBuilder();

        var strategyPnl = result.StrategyPnL ?? new Dictionary();
        var strategyDiagnostics = result.StrategyDiagnostics ?? new Dictionary();
        var symbolTfPnl = result.SymbolTimeframePnL ?? new Dictionary(StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase);
        var strategySymbolTfPnl = result.StrategySymbolTimeframePnL ?? new Dictionary(StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase);
        var rejections = result.MarketSelectionRejections ?? new Dictionary(StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase);
        var selectedMarkets = (result.SelectedMarkets ?? new List())
            .ToHashSet(StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase);

        decimal s06Pnl = strategyPnl.TryGetValue(TargetStrategyId, out var foundS06Pnl)
            ? foundS06Pnl
            : 0m;

        string s06Code = ResolveStrategyCode(TargetStrategyId, fitnessSnapshots);

        var s06Rows = strategySymbolTfPnl
            .Where(x => x.Key.StartsWith(TargetPrefix, StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase))
            .Select(x => BuildRow(x.Key, x.Value, rejections, selectedMarkets))
            .OrderByDescending(x => x.NetPnl)
            .ThenBy(x => x.MarketKey, StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase)
            .ToList();

        var phase1Rows = s06Rows
            .Where(x => x.FamilyTier == "PHASE_1")
            .OrderByDescending(x => x.EntryTighteningPriority)
            .ThenByDescending(x => x.NetPnl)
            .ThenBy(x => x.MarketKey, StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase)
            .ToList();

        var phase2Rows = s06Rows
            .Where(x => x.FamilyTier == "PHASE_2")
            .OrderByDescending(x => x.EntryTighteningPriority)
            .ThenByDescending(x => x.NetPnl)
            .ThenBy(x => x.MarketKey, StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase)
            .ToList();

        var nearMissRows = s06Rows
            .Where(x => !x.IsSelectedNow)
            .OrderByDescending(x => x.EntryTighteningPriority)
            .ThenByDescending(x => x.NetPnl)
            .ToList();

        int ticksProcessed = strategyDiagnostics.TryGetValue(TargetStrategyId, out var diag) ? diag.TicksProcessed : 0;
        int signalLong = strategyDiagnostics.TryGetValue(TargetStrategyId, out diag) ? diag.SignalLong : 0;
        int signalExit = strategyDiagnostics.TryGetValue(TargetStrategyId, out diag) ? diag.SignalExit : 0;
        int entryAttempts = strategyDiagnostics.TryGetValue(TargetStrategyId, out diag) ? diag.EntryAttempts : 0;
        int executedEntries = strategyDiagnostics.TryGetValue(TargetStrategyId, out diag) ? diag.ExecutedEntries : 0;
        int executedExits = strategyDiagnostics.TryGetValue(TargetStrategyId, out diag) ? diag.ExecutedExits : 0;

        decimal conversionRate = entryAttempts <= 0 ? 0m : (decimal)executedEntries / entryAttempts;
        decimal selectedMarketCount = selectedMarkets.Count;

        sb.AppendLine("REPORT 30 — S06 PHASE-1 REFINEMENT / ENTRY-TIGHTENING AUDIT");
        sb.AppendLine("===========================================================");
        sb.AppendLine();
        sb.AppendLine("PURPOSE");
        sb.AppendLine("-------");
        sb.AppendLine("Audit whether S06 should be refined inside the current phase-1 family by tightening entry quality, rather than expanded into phase-2 or broader universe coverage.");
        sb.AppendLine();

        sb.AppendLine("RUN CONTEXT");
        sb.AppendLine("-----------");
        sb.AppendLine($"Run Timestamp (UTC)                : {runUtc:yyyy-MM-dd HH:mm:ss}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Target Strategy Id                 : S{TargetStrategyId:00}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Target Strategy Code               : {s06Code}");
        sb.AppendLine($"S06 Total PnL                      : {s06Pnl:F2}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Selected Markets Count             : {selectedMarketCount:F0}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Cash Allocation Weight             : {result.CashAllocationWeight:P2}");
        sb.AppendLine();

        sb.AppendLine("S06 STRATEGY TELEMETRY");
        sb.AppendLine("----------------------");
        sb.AppendLine($"Ticks Processed                    : {ticksProcessed}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Signal Long                        : {signalLong}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Signal Exit                        : {signalExit}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Entry Attempts                     : {entryAttempts}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Executed Entries                   : {executedEntries}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Executed Exits                     : {executedExits}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Entry Conversion Rate              : {conversionRate:P2}");
        sb.AppendLine();

        sb.AppendLine("LIVE TOP SYMBOL::TF PNL");
        sb.AppendLine("-----------------------");
        if (symbolTfPnl.Count == 0)
        {
            sb.AppendLine("NO SYMBOL::TF PNL DATA");
        }
        else
        {
            sb.AppendLine("Rank | Symbol::TF                | PnL");
            sb.AppendLine("-----+---------------------------+------------");
            int rank = 1;
            foreach (var kv in symbolTfPnl.OrderByDescending(x => x.Value).Take(12))
            {
                sb.AppendLine($"{rank,4} | {TrimTo(kv.Key, 25),-25} | {kv.Value,10:F2}");
                rank++;
            }
        }
        sb.AppendLine();

        sb.AppendLine("S06 PHASE-1 CONTRIBUTION TABLE");
        sb.AppendLine("------------------------------");
        if (phase1Rows.Count == 0)
        {
            sb.AppendLine("NO PHASE-1 S06 ROWS");
        }
        else
        {
            sb.AppendLine("Rank | Market                    | NetPnL     | Bucket                           | SelectedNow | TightenPriority | Verdict");
            sb.AppendLine("-----+---------------------------+------------+----------------------------------+-------------+-----------------+------------------------------");
            int rank = 1;
            foreach (var row in phase1Rows)
            {
                sb.AppendLine(
                    $"{rank,4} | {TrimTo(row.MarketKey, 25),-25} | {row.NetPnl,10:F2} | " +
                    $"{TrimTo(row.ReasonBucket, 32),-32} | {(row.IsSelectedNow ? "YES" : "NO "),11} | " +
                    $"{row.EntryTighteningPriority,15:F2} | {TrimTo(row.EntryTighteningVerdict, 28)}");
                rank++;
            }
        }
        sb.AppendLine();

        sb.AppendLine("S06 PHASE-2 WATCHLIST TABLE");
        sb.AppendLine("---------------------------");
        if (phase2Rows.Count == 0)
        {
            sb.AppendLine("NO PHASE-2 S06 ROWS");
        }
        else
        {
            sb.AppendLine("Rank | Market                    | NetPnL     | Bucket                           | TightenPriority | Verdict");
            sb.AppendLine("-----+---------------------------+------------+----------------------------------+-----------------+------------------------------");
            int rank = 1;
            foreach (var row in phase2Rows)
            {
                sb.AppendLine(
                    $"{rank,4} | {TrimTo(row.MarketKey, 25),-25} | {row.NetPnl,10:F2} | " +
                    $"{TrimTo(row.ReasonBucket, 32),-32} | {row.EntryTighteningPriority,15:F2} | {TrimTo(row.EntryTighteningVerdict, 28)}");
                rank++;
            }
        }
        sb.AppendLine();

        sb.AppendLine("TOP ENTRY-TIGHTENING TARGETS");
        sb.AppendLine("----------------------------");
        if (nearMissRows.Count == 0)
        {
            sb.AppendLine("NO ENTRY-TIGHTENING TARGETS");
        }
        else
        {
            foreach (var row in nearMissRows.Take(8))
            {
                sb.AppendLine(
                    $"{row.MarketKey,-24} tier={row.FamilyTier,-8} pnl={row.NetPnl,10:F2} " +
                    $"bucket={row.ReasonBucket,-32} priority={row.EntryTighteningPriority:F2} => {row.EntryTighteningVerdict}");
            }
        }
        sb.AppendLine();

        sb.AppendLine("ENTRY-TIGHTENING HYPOTHESIS");
        sb.AppendLine("---------------------------");
        sb.AppendLine(BuildHypothesis(s06Pnl, conversionRate, phase1Rows, selectedMarketCount, result.CashAllocationWeight));
        sb.AppendLine();

        sb.AppendLine("OPERATOR GUIDANCE");
        sb.AppendLine("-----------------");
        sb.AppendLine("1) Keep S06 on phase-1 only while total contribution is still small.");
        sb.AppendLine("2) Tighten entry quality on the highest-priority phase-1 names before adding phase-2 watchlist symbols.");
        sb.AppendLine("3) Do not broaden the family until S06 materially improves deployable breadth or reduces cash held.");
        sb.AppendLine("4) If phase-1 refinement works, only then test phase-2 expansion.");
        sb.AppendLine();

        File.WriteAllText(path, sb.ToString());
    }

    private static AuditRow BuildRow(
        string strategySymbolTfKey,
        decimal netPnl,
        IReadOnlyDictionary rejections,
        IReadOnlySet selectedMarkets)
    {
        string marketKey = ExtractMarketKey(strategySymbolTfKey);
        bool isSelectedNow = selectedMarkets.Contains(marketKey);

        string familyTier = ResolveFamilyTier(marketKey);

        string reasonBucket = "NOT_REJECTED";
        if (!isSelectedNow && rejections.TryGetValue(marketKey, out var rejection))
            reasonBucket = NormalizeReasonBucket(rejection);

        decimal priority = 0m;

        if (familyTier == "PHASE_1") priority += 0.40m;
        if (familyTier == "PHASE_2") priority += 0.18m;

        if (netPnl > 0m) priority += 0.25m;
        if (netPnl <= 0m) priority += 0.05m;

        if (reasonBucket == "WaveBRejected:DispersionGuard") priority += 0.30m;
        else if (reasonBucket == "REJECT: regime near-miss lane overflow") priority += 0.22m;
        else if (reasonBucket == "REJECT: outside top leadership set") priority += 0.18m;
        else if (reasonBucket == "REJECT: regime not trend/high-vol-up") priority += 0.14m;
        else if (reasonBucket == "REJECT: low liquidity") priority += 0.08m;

        string verdict = BuildVerdict(familyTier, isSelectedNow, netPnl, reasonBucket, priority);

        return new AuditRow(
            marketKey,
            netPnl,
            reasonBucket,
            isSelectedNow,
            familyTier,
            priority,
            verdict);
    }

    private static string BuildVerdict(
        string familyTier,
        bool isSelectedNow,
        decimal netPnl,
        string reasonBucket,
        decimal priority)
    {
        if (isSelectedNow)
            return "Already selected now";

        if (familyTier == "PHASE_1" && netPnl > 0m && reasonBucket == "WaveBRejected:DispersionGuard" && priority >= 0.90m)
            return "Best phase-1 tightening target";

        if (familyTier == "PHASE_1" && netPnl > 0m && priority >= 0.75m)
            return "Strong phase-1 refinement target";

        if (familyTier == "PHASE_2" && netPnl > 0m && priority >= 0.55m)
            return "Watch only, not ready";

        if (familyTier == "PHASE_1" && priority >= 0.55m)
            return "Refine before expansion";

        return "Not ready for expansion";
    }

    private static string BuildHypothesis(
        decimal s06Pnl,
        decimal conversionRate,
        IReadOnlyList phase1Rows,
        decimal selectedMarketCount,
        decimal cashWeight)
    {
        bool positivePhase1Exists = phase1Rows.Any(x => x.NetPnl > 0m);
        bool strongPhase1NearMiss = phase1Rows.Any(x => x.EntryTighteningPriority >= 0.85m && !x.IsSelectedNow);
        bool veryDefensive = selectedMarketCount <= 1m && cashWeight >= 0.90m;

        if (veryDefensive && s06Pnl > 0m && strongPhase1NearMiss)
            return "S06 is alive but too weak for family expansion. Tighten entry quality inside phase-1 first, especially around the best near-miss name(s).";

        if (veryDefensive && s06Pnl > 0m && positivePhase1Exists)
            return "S06 shows early life, but the portfolio is still too defensive for phase-2 expansion. Refine phase-1 entry quality before widening the family.";

        if (conversionRate < 0.10m)
            return "S06 may be too restrictive or poorly aligned. Review phase-1 entry timing before adding more symbols.";

        return "S06 still needs phase-1 refinement before broader expansion decisions.";
    }

    private static string ResolveFamilyTier(string marketKey)
    {
        string symbol = ExtractSymbol(marketKey);

        if (Phase1StarterSymbols.Contains(symbol, StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase))
            return "PHASE_1";

        if (Phase2WatchlistSymbols.Contains(symbol, StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase))
            return "PHASE_2";

        return "OUTSIDE_FAMILY";
    }

    private static string NormalizeReasonBucket(string rejectionReason)
    {
        string value = rejectionReason?.Trim() ?? string.Empty;

        if (value.StartsWith("WaveBRejected:DispersionGuard", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase))
            return "WaveBRejected:DispersionGuard";

        if (value.StartsWith("WaveBRejected:BelowThreshold", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase))
            return "WaveBRejected:BelowThreshold";

        if (value.StartsWith("WaveBRejected:PerSymbolCap", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase))
            return "WaveBRejected:PerSymbolCap";

        if (value.StartsWith("WaveBRejected:TopNOverflow", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase))
            return "WaveBRejected:TopNOverflow";

        if (value.StartsWith("REJECT: outside top", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase))
            return "REJECT: outside top leadership set";

        if (value.StartsWith("REJECT: regime near-miss lane overflow", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase))
            return "REJECT: regime near-miss lane overflow";

        if (value.StartsWith("REJECT: regime not trend/high-vol-up", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase))
            return "REJECT: regime not trend/high-vol-up";

        if (value.StartsWith("REJECT: low liquidity", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase))
            return "REJECT: low liquidity";

        return value;
    }

    private static string ExtractMarketKey(string strategySymbolTfKey)
    {
        if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(strategySymbolTfKey))
            return string.Empty;

        var parts = strategySymbolTfKey.Split(new[] { "::" }, StringSplitOptions.None);
        if (parts.Length < 3)
            return strategySymbolTfKey;

        return $"{parts[1]}::{parts[2]}";
    }

    private static string ExtractSymbol(string marketKey)
    {
        if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(marketKey))
            return string.Empty;

        var parts = marketKey.Split(new[] { "::" }, StringSplitOptions.None);
        return parts.Length >= 1 ? parts[0].Trim() : string.Empty;
    }

    private static string ResolveStrategyCode(
        int strategyId,
        IReadOnlyDictionary fitnessSnapshots)
    {
        if (fitnessSnapshots.TryGetValue(strategyId, out var snap) &&
            !string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(snap.StrategyCode))
        {
            return snap.StrategyCode;
        }

        return $"S{strategyId:00}";
    }

    private static string TrimTo(string? text, int maxLen)
    {
        string value = text ?? string.Empty;
        if (value.Length <= maxLen)
            return value;

        if (maxLen <= 3)
            return value[..maxLen];

        return value[..(maxLen - 3)] + "...";
    }

    private sealed record AuditRow(
        string MarketKey,
        decimal NetPnl,
        string ReasonBucket,
        bool IsSelectedNow,
        string FamilyTier,
        decimal EntryTighteningPriority,
        string EntryTighteningVerdict);
}

 using System.Globalization;
using System.Text;
using TQGA.Application.Portfolio;
using TQGA.Application.Reporting;
using TQGA.Application.Paths;
using TQGA.Domain.Trading;

namespace TQGA.Application.Services;

public sealed class Report32TradeBlotterEntryExitReasonJournalService
{
    public void GenerateAndWrite(
        IReadOnlyList nodes,
        IReadOnlyList selectedMarkets,
        DateTime runUtc)
    {
        ArgumentNullException.ThrowIfNull(nodes);
        ArgumentNullException.ThrowIfNull(selectedMarkets);

        Directory.CreateDirectory(DataPaths.Reports);

        string stamp = PakistanTime.Stamp(runUtc);

        string txtPath = Path.Combine(
            DataPaths.Reports,
            $"REPORT_32_TRADE_BLOTTER_ENTRY_EXIT_REASON_JOURNAL_{stamp}.txt");

        string csvPath = Path.Combine(
            DataPaths.Reports,
            $"REPORT_32_TRADE_BLOTTER_ENTRY_EXIT_REASON_JOURNAL_{stamp}.csv");

        var symbolToTimeframe = BuildSymbolToTimeframeMap(selectedMarkets);

        var rows = nodes
            .SelectMany(node => node.Ledger.Trades.Select(trade => BuildRow(node, trade, symbolToTimeframe)))
            .OrderBy(x => x.EntryTimeUtc)
            .ThenBy(x => x.StrategyId)
            .ThenBy(x => x.Symbol, StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase)
            .ToList();

        WriteTxt(txtPath, rows, runUtc);
        WriteCsv(csvPath, rows);
    }

    private static Dictionary BuildSymbolToTimeframeMap(IReadOnlyList selectedMarkets)
    {
        var output = new Dictionary(StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase);

        foreach (string market in selectedMarkets)
        {
            if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(market))
                continue;

            var parts = market.Split(new[] { "::" }, StringSplitOptions.None);
            if (parts.Length < 2)
                continue;

            string symbol = parts[0].Trim();
            string timeframe = parts[1].Trim();

            if (!string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(symbol) && !string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(timeframe))
                output[symbol] = timeframe;
        }

        return output;
    }

    private static TradeJournalRow BuildRow(
        StrategyBacktestNode node,
        Trade trade,
        IReadOnlyDictionary symbolToTimeframe)
    {
        string timeframe = symbolToTimeframe.TryGetValue(trade.Symbol, out var resolvedTf)
            ? resolvedTf
            : "UNKNOWN_TF";

        decimal holdingMinutes = trade.ExitTime.HasValue
            ? (decimal)(trade.ExitTime.Value - trade.EntryTime).TotalMinutes
            : 0m;

        decimal? riskPerUnit = null;
        if (trade.StopLossAtEntry.HasValue)
            riskPerUnit = Math.Abs(trade.EntryPrice - trade.StopLossAtEntry.Value);

        decimal? moneyRisk = riskPerUnit.HasValue ? riskPerUnit.Value * trade.Quantity : null;
        decimal? rMultiple = moneyRisk.HasValue && moneyRisk.Value > 0m
            ? trade.RealizedPnL / moneyRisk.Value
            : null;

        return new TradeJournalRow(
            StrategyId: node.StrategyId,
            StrategyName: node.StrategyName,
            Symbol: trade.Symbol,
            Timeframe: timeframe,
            Side: trade.Side.ToString(),
            Quantity: trade.Quantity,
            EntryTimeUtc: trade.EntryTime,
            EntryPrice: trade.EntryPrice,
            ExitTimeUtc: trade.ExitTime,
            ExitPrice: trade.ExitPrice,
            IsClosed: trade.IsClosed,
            RealizedPnl: trade.RealizedPnL,
            HoldingMinutes: holdingMinutes,
            OrderType: trade.TrueOrderType,
            EntryReason: trade.EntryReason,
            ExitReason: trade.ExitReason ?? "OPEN",
            StopLoss: trade.StopLossAtEntry,
            TakeProfit: trade.TakeProfitAtEntry,
            ExpectedPrice: trade.ExpectedPrice,
            PlanSource: trade.PlanSource,
            FavorableExcursion: trade.FavorableExcursion * trade.Quantity,
            AdverseExcursion: trade.AdverseExcursion * trade.Quantity,
            RMultiple: rMultiple);
    }

    private static void WriteTxt(
        string path,
        IReadOnlyList rows,
        DateTime runUtc)
    {
        var sb = new StringBuilder();

        sb.AppendLine("REPORT 32 — TRADE BLOTTER / ENTRY-EXIT REASON JOURNAL");
        sb.AppendLine("=====================================================");
        sb.AppendLine();
        sb.AppendLine("PURPOSE");
        sb.AppendLine("-------");
        sb.AppendLine("Provide a trade-by-trade operator journal for every recorded trade in the run.");
        sb.AppendLine();

        sb.AppendLine("RUN CONTEXT");
        sb.AppendLine("-----------");
        sb.AppendLine($"Run Timestamp (PKT)                : {PakistanTime.FormatLabel(runUtc)}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Total Trade Rows                   : {rows.Count}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Closed Trades                      : {rows.Count(x => x.IsClosed)}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Open Trades                        : {rows.Count(x => !x.IsClosed)}");
        sb.AppendLine();

        sb.AppendLine("TRADE JOURNAL");
        sb.AppendLine("-------------");
        if (rows.Count == 0)
        {
            sb.AppendLine("NO TRADES RECORDED.");
        }
        else
        {
            int rank = 1;
            foreach (var row in rows)
            {
                sb.AppendLine($"TRADE #{rank:0000}");
                sb.AppendLine($"Strategy Id                        : S{row.StrategyId:00}");
                sb.AppendLine($"Strategy Name                      : {row.StrategyName}");
                sb.AppendLine($"Symbol                             : {row.Symbol}");
                sb.AppendLine($"Timeframe                          : {row.Timeframe}");
                sb.AppendLine($"Side                               : {row.Side}");
                sb.AppendLine($"Quantity                           : {row.Quantity:F8}");
                sb.AppendLine($"Entry Time (PKT)                   : {PakistanTime.FormatLabel(row.EntryTimeUtc)}");
                sb.AppendLine($"Entry Price                        : {row.EntryPrice:F8}");
                sb.AppendLine($"Exit Time (PKT)                    : {(row.ExitTimeUtc.HasValue ? PakistanTime.FormatLabel(row.ExitTimeUtc.Value) : "OPEN")}");
                sb.AppendLine($"Exit Price                         : {(row.ExitPrice.HasValue ? row.ExitPrice.Value.ToString("F8", CultureInfo.InvariantCulture) : "OPEN")}");
                sb.AppendLine($"Closed                             : {(row.IsClosed ? "YES" : "NO")}");
                sb.AppendLine($"Realized PnL                       : {row.RealizedPnl:F8}");
                sb.AppendLine($"Holding Minutes                    : {row.HoldingMinutes:F2}");
                sb.AppendLine($"Order Type                         : {row.OrderType}");
                sb.AppendLine($"Entry Reason                       : {row.EntryReason}");
                sb.AppendLine($"Exit Reason                        : {row.ExitReason}");
                sb.AppendLine($"Stop Loss                          : {(row.StopLoss.HasValue ? row.StopLoss.Value.ToString("F8", CultureInfo.InvariantCulture) : "NULL")}");
                sb.AppendLine($"Take Profit                        : {(row.TakeProfit.HasValue ? row.TakeProfit.Value.ToString("F8", CultureInfo.InvariantCulture) : "NULL")}");
                sb.AppendLine($"Expected Price                     : {(row.ExpectedPrice.HasValue ? row.ExpectedPrice.Value.ToString("F8", CultureInfo.InvariantCulture) : "NULL")}");
                sb.AppendLine($"Plan Source                        : {row.PlanSource}");
                sb.AppendLine($"Favorable Excursion                : {row.FavorableExcursion:F8}");
                sb.AppendLine($"Adverse Excursion                  : {row.AdverseExcursion:F8}");
                sb.AppendLine($"R Multiple                         : {(row.RMultiple.HasValue ? row.RMultiple.Value.ToString("F4", CultureInfo.InvariantCulture) : "NULL")}");
                sb.AppendLine();
                rank++;
            }
        }

        File.WriteAllText(path, sb.ToString());
    }

    private static void WriteCsv(
        string path,
        IReadOnlyList rows)
    {
        using var writer = new StreamWriter(path, false, Encoding.UTF8);

        writer.WriteLine(
            "StrategyId,StrategyName,Symbol,Timeframe,Side,Quantity,EntryTimePkt,EntryPrice,ExitTimePkt,ExitPrice,IsClosed,RealizedPnl,HoldingMinutes,OrderType,EntryReason,ExitReason,StopLoss,TakeProfit,ExpectedPrice,PlanSource,FavorableExcursion,AdverseExcursion,RMultiple");

        foreach (var row in rows)
        {
            writer.WriteLine(string.Join(",",
                Csv(row.StrategyId.ToString(CultureInfo.InvariantCulture)),
                Csv(row.StrategyName),
                Csv(row.Symbol),
                Csv(row.Timeframe),
                Csv(row.Side),
                Csv(row.Quantity.ToString("F8", CultureInfo.InvariantCulture)),
                Csv(PakistanTime.FormatLabel(row.EntryTimeUtc)),
                Csv(row.EntryPrice.ToString("F8", CultureInfo.InvariantCulture)),
                Csv(row.ExitTimeUtc.HasValue ? PakistanTime.FormatLabel(row.ExitTimeUtc.Value) : "OPEN"),
                Csv(row.ExitPrice.HasValue ? row.ExitPrice.Value.ToString("F8", CultureInfo.InvariantCulture) : "OPEN"),
                Csv(row.IsClosed ? "YES" : "NO"),
                Csv(row.RealizedPnl.ToString("F8", CultureInfo.InvariantCulture)),
                Csv(row.HoldingMinutes.ToString("F2", CultureInfo.InvariantCulture)),
                Csv(row.OrderType),
                Csv(row.EntryReason),
                Csv(row.ExitReason),
                Csv(row.StopLoss.HasValue ? row.StopLoss.Value.ToString("F8", CultureInfo.InvariantCulture) : "NULL"),
                Csv(row.TakeProfit.HasValue ? row.TakeProfit.Value.ToString("F8", CultureInfo.InvariantCulture) : "NULL"),
                Csv(row.ExpectedPrice.HasValue ? row.ExpectedPrice.Value.ToString("F8", CultureInfo.InvariantCulture) : "NULL"),
                Csv(row.PlanSource),
                Csv(row.FavorableExcursion.ToString("F8", CultureInfo.InvariantCulture)),
                Csv(row.AdverseExcursion.ToString("F8", CultureInfo.InvariantCulture)),
                Csv(row.RMultiple.HasValue ? row.RMultiple.Value.ToString("F4", CultureInfo.InvariantCulture) : "NULL")));
        }
    }

    private static string Csv(string value)
    {
        string safe = value ?? string.Empty;
        safe = safe.Replace("\"", "\"\"");
        return $"\"{safe}\"";
    }

    private sealed record TradeJournalRow(
        int StrategyId,
        string StrategyName,
        string Symbol,
        string Timeframe,
        string Side,
        decimal Quantity,
        DateTime EntryTimeUtc,
        decimal EntryPrice,
        DateTime? ExitTimeUtc,
        decimal? ExitPrice,
        bool IsClosed,
        decimal RealizedPnl,
        decimal HoldingMinutes,
        string OrderType,
        string EntryReason,
        string ExitReason,
        decimal? StopLoss,
        decimal? TakeProfit,
        decimal? ExpectedPrice,
        string PlanSource,
        decimal FavorableExcursion,
        decimal AdverseExcursion,
        decimal? RMultiple);
}

 = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = = 
 
 using System.Globalization;
using System.Text;
using TQGA.Application.Backtesting;
using TQGA.Application.Paths;
using TQGA.Application.Portfolio;
using TQGA.Application.Reporting;
using TQGA.Domain.Trading;

namespace TQGA.Application.Services;

public sealed class Report33TradeIntelligenceMasterReportService
{
    public void GenerateAndWrite(
        IReadOnlyList nodes,
        PortfolioBacktestResult result,
        decimal initialCapital,
        DateTime runUtc,
        string? benchmarkSymbol = null,
        string? benchmarkTimeframe = null,
        decimal? benchmarkStartPrice = null,
        decimal? benchmarkEndPrice = null)
    {
        ArgumentNullException.ThrowIfNull(nodes);
        ArgumentNullException.ThrowIfNull(result);

        Directory.CreateDirectory(DataPaths.Reports);

        string stamp = PakistanTime.Stamp(runUtc);

        string txtPath = Path.Combine(
            DataPaths.Reports,
            $"REPORT_33_TRADE_INTELLIGENCE_MASTER_{stamp}.txt");

        string csvPath = Path.Combine(
            DataPaths.Reports,
            $"REPORT_33_TRADE_INTELLIGENCE_MASTER_{stamp}.csv");

        var symbolToTimeframe = BuildSymbolToTimeframeMap(result.SelectedMarkets ?? new List());

        var trades = nodes
            .SelectMany(node => node.Ledger.Trades.Select((trade, idx) => BuildRow(node, trade, idx + 1, symbolToTimeframe)))
            .OrderBy(x => x.EntryTimeUtc)
            .ThenBy(x => x.StrategyId)
            .ThenBy(x => x.Symbol, StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase)
            .ToList();

        var closedTrades = trades.Where(x => x.IsClosed).ToList();
        var openTrades = trades.Where(x => !x.IsClosed).ToList();

        decimal grossProfit = closedTrades.Where(x => x.NetPnl > 0m).Sum(x => x.NetPnl);
        decimal grossLossAbs = Math.Abs(closedTrades.Where(x => x.NetPnl < 0m).Sum(x => x.NetPnl));
        decimal netPnl = closedTrades.Sum(x => x.NetPnl);
        decimal commissionPaid = trades.Sum(x => x.Commission);
        decimal openPnl = openTrades.Sum(x => x.NetPnl);

        int winningTrades = closedTrades.Count(x => x.NetPnl > 0m);
        int losingTrades = closedTrades.Count(x => x.NetPnl < 0m);

        decimal profitFactor = grossLossAbs <= 0m ? decimal.MaxValue : grossProfit / grossLossAbs;
        decimal expectedPayoff = closedTrades.Count == 0 ? 0m : netPnl / closedTrades.Count;
        decimal percentProfitable = closedTrades.Count == 0 ? 0m : (decimal)winningTrades / closedTrades.Count;

        decimal avgPnl = closedTrades.Count == 0 ? 0m : closedTrades.Sum(x => x.NetPnl) / closedTrades.Count;
        decimal avgWinner = winningTrades == 0 ? 0m : closedTrades.Where(x => x.NetPnl > 0m).Sum(x => x.NetPnl) / winningTrades;
        decimal avgLoserAbs = losingTrades == 0 ? 0m : Math.Abs(closedTrades.Where(x => x.NetPnl < 0m).Sum(x => x.NetPnl) / losingTrades);
        decimal avgWinLossRatio = avgLoserAbs <= 0m ? decimal.MaxValue : avgWinner / avgLoserAbs;

        decimal largestWinner = closedTrades.Count == 0 ? 0m : closedTrades.Max(x => x.NetPnl);
        decimal largestLoser = closedTrades.Count == 0 ? 0m : closedTrades.Min(x => x.NetPnl);

        decimal largestWinnerPct = initialCapital <= 0m ? 0m : largestWinner / initialCapital;
        decimal largestLoserPct = initialCapital <= 0m ? 0m : Math.Abs(largestLoser) / initialCapital;

        decimal avgHoldingMinutes = closedTrades.Count == 0 ? 0m : closedTrades.Sum(x => x.HoldingMinutes) / closedTrades.Count;
        decimal avgBarsHeld = closedTrades.Count == 0 ? 0m : closedTrades.Sum(x => x.BarsHeld) / closedTrades.Count;

        var rTrades = closedTrades.Where(x => x.RMultiple.HasValue).ToList();
        decimal avgRMultiple = rTrades.Count == 0 ? 0m : rTrades.Sum(x => x.RMultiple!.Value) / rTrades.Count;
        decimal bestRMultiple = rTrades.Count == 0 ? 0m : rTrades.Max(x => x.RMultiple!.Value);
        decimal worstRMultiple = rTrades.Count == 0 ? 0m : rTrades.Min(x => x.RMultiple!.Value);

        decimal avgFavorableExcursion = closedTrades.Count == 0 ? 0m : closedTrades.Sum(x => x.FavorableExcursion) / closedTrades.Count;
        decimal avgAdverseExcursion = closedTrades.Count == 0 ? 0m : closedTrades.Sum(x => x.AdverseExcursion) / closedTrades.Count;

        var equityPoints = (result.PortfolioEquityTimeline ?? new Dictionary())
            .OrderBy(x => x.Key)
            .ToList();

        decimal startEquity = equityPoints.Count == 0 ? initialCapital : equityPoints.First().Value;
        decimal endEquity = equityPoints.Count == 0 ? initialCapital : equityPoints.Last().Value;
        decimal portfolioDelta = endEquity - startEquity;
        decimal totalReturnPct = startEquity <= 0m ? 0m : portfolioDelta / startEquity;

        decimal strategySum = (result.StrategyPnL ?? new Dictionary()).Values.Sum();
        decimal symbolSum = (result.SymbolPnL ?? new Dictionary(StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase)).Values.Sum();
        decimal tradeJournalSum = closedTrades.Sum(x => x.NetPnl);

        decimal maxEquityDrawdown = ComputeMaxDrawdown(equityPoints);
        decimal maxEquityDrawdownPct = startEquity <= 0m ? 0m : maxEquityDrawdown / startEquity;

        decimal? benchmarkReturn = null;
        decimal? benchmarkPct = null;
        decimal? strategyOutperformance = null;

        if (benchmarkStartPrice.HasValue && benchmarkEndPrice.HasValue && benchmarkStartPrice.Value > 0m)
        {
            benchmarkReturn = benchmarkEndPrice.Value - benchmarkStartPrice.Value;
            benchmarkPct = benchmarkReturn.Value / benchmarkStartPrice.Value;
            strategyOutperformance = totalReturnPct - benchmarkPct.Value;
        }

        var strategyGroups = nodes
            .Select(node =>
            {
                string strategyName = node.StrategyName ?? $"S{node.StrategyId:00}";
                var nodeTrades = node.Ledger.Trades
                    .Select((trade, idx) => BuildRow(node, trade, idx + 1, symbolToTimeframe))
                    .ToList();

                var nodeClosed = nodeTrades.Where(x => x.IsClosed).ToList();

                decimal nodeGrossProfit = nodeClosed.Where(x => x.NetPnl > 0m).Sum(x => x.NetPnl);
                decimal nodeGrossLossAbs = Math.Abs(nodeClosed.Where(x => x.NetPnl < 0m).Sum(x => x.NetPnl));
                decimal nodeProfitFactor = nodeGrossLossAbs <= 0m ? decimal.MaxValue : nodeGrossProfit / nodeGrossLossAbs;
                decimal nodeAvgTrade = nodeClosed.Count == 0 ? 0m : nodeClosed.Sum(x => x.NetPnl) / nodeClosed.Count;

                int nodeWins = nodeClosed.Count(x => x.NetPnl > 0m);
                decimal nodeWinRate = nodeClosed.Count == 0 ? 0m : (decimal)nodeWins / nodeClosed.Count;

                var nodeRTrades = nodeClosed.Where(x => x.RMultiple.HasValue).ToList();
                decimal nodeAvgR = nodeRTrades.Count == 0 ? 0m : nodeRTrades.Sum(x => x.RMultiple!.Value) / nodeRTrades.Count;

                string bestSymbol = nodeClosed.OrderByDescending(x => x.NetPnl).FirstOrDefault()?.MarketKey ?? "N/A";
                string worstSymbol = nodeClosed.OrderBy(x => x.NetPnl).FirstOrDefault()?.MarketKey ?? "N/A";

                decimal nativePct = nodeTrades.Count == 0
                    ? 0m
                    : (decimal)nodeTrades.Count(x => x.PlanSource.Equals("StrategyNative", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase)) / nodeTrades.Count;

                decimal fallbackPct = nodeTrades.Count == 0
                    ? 0m
                    : (decimal)nodeTrades.Count(x => x.PlanSource.Equals("EngineFallback", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase)) / nodeTrades.Count;

                return new StrategySummaryRow(
                    node.StrategyId,
                    strategyName,
                    nodeClosed.Sum(x => x.NetPnl),
                    nodeClosed.Count,
                    nodeWinRate,
                    nodeProfitFactor,
                    nodeAvgTrade,
                    nodeAvgR,
                    bestSymbol,
                    worstSymbol,
                    nativePct,
                    fallbackPct);
            })
            .OrderByDescending(x => x.NetPnl)
            .ToList();

        var symbolGroups = trades
            .GroupBy(x => x.MarketKey)
            .Select(g =>
            {
                var gClosed = g.Where(x => x.IsClosed).ToList();
                decimal gGrossProfit = gClosed.Where(x => x.NetPnl > 0m).Sum(x => x.NetPnl);
                decimal gGrossLossAbs = Math.Abs(gClosed.Where(x => x.NetPnl < 0m).Sum(x => x.NetPnl));
                decimal gProfitFactor = gGrossLossAbs <= 0m ? decimal.MaxValue : gGrossProfit / gGrossLossAbs;
                decimal gAvgTrade = gClosed.Count == 0 ? 0m : gClosed.Sum(x => x.NetPnl) / gClosed.Count;

                int gWins = gClosed.Count(x => x.NetPnl > 0m);
                decimal gWinRate = gClosed.Count == 0 ? 0m : (decimal)gWins / gClosed.Count;

                var gRTrades = gClosed.Where(x => x.RMultiple.HasValue).ToList();
                decimal gAvgR = gRTrades.Count == 0 ? 0m : gRTrades.Sum(x => x.RMultiple!.Value) / gRTrades.Count;

                string bestStrategy = gClosed.OrderByDescending(x => x.NetPnl).FirstOrDefault()?.StrategyName ?? "N/A";
                string worstStrategy = gClosed.OrderBy(x => x.NetPnl).FirstOrDefault()?.StrategyName ?? "N/A";

                return new SymbolSummaryRow(
                    g.Key,
                    gClosed.Sum(x => x.NetPnl),
                    gClosed.Count,
                    gWinRate,
                    gProfitFactor,
                    gAvgTrade,
                    gAvgR,
                    bestStrategy,
                    worstStrategy);
            })
            .OrderByDescending(x => x.NetPnl)
            .ToList();

        WriteTxt(
            txtPath,
            runUtc,
            benchmarkSymbol,
            benchmarkTimeframe,
            startEquity,
            endEquity,
            openPnl,
            netPnl,
            grossProfit,
            grossLossAbs,
            commissionPaid,
            totalReturnPct,
            benchmarkReturn,
            benchmarkPct,
            strategyOutperformance,
            profitFactor,
            expectedPayoff,
            totalTrades: trades.Count,
            closedTrades: closedTrades.Count,
            openTrades: openTrades.Count,
            winningTrades: winningTrades,
            losingTrades: losingTrades,
            percentProfitable: percentProfitable,
            avgPnl: avgPnl,
            avgWinner: avgWinner,
            avgLoserAbs: avgLoserAbs,
            avgWinLossRatio: avgWinLossRatio,
            largestWinner: largestWinner,
            largestLoser: largestLoser,
            largestWinnerPct: largestWinnerPct,
            largestLoserPct: largestLoserPct,
            avgHoldingMinutes: avgHoldingMinutes,
            avgBarsHeld: avgBarsHeld,
            avgRMultiple: avgRMultiple,
            bestRMultiple: bestRMultiple,
            worstRMultiple: worstRMultiple,
            avgFavorableExcursion: avgFavorableExcursion,
            avgAdverseExcursion: avgAdverseExcursion,
            maxEquityDrawdown: maxEquityDrawdown,
            maxEquityDrawdownPct: maxEquityDrawdownPct,
            portfolioDelta: portfolioDelta,
            strategySum: strategySum,
            symbolSum: symbolSum,
            tradeJournalSum: tradeJournalSum,
            strategyGroups: strategyGroups,
            symbolGroups: symbolGroups,
            trades: trades);

        WriteCsv(csvPath, trades);
    }

    private static Dictionary BuildSymbolToTimeframeMap(IReadOnlyList selectedMarkets)
    {
        var output = new Dictionary(StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase);

        foreach (string market in selectedMarkets)
        {
            if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(market))
                continue;

            string[] parts = market.Split(new[] { "::" }, StringSplitOptions.None);
            if (parts.Length < 2)
                continue;

            output[parts[0].Trim()] = parts[1].Trim();
        }

        return output;
    }

    private static TradeIntelligenceRow BuildRow(
        StrategyBacktestNode node,
        Trade trade,
        int tradeNumber,
        IReadOnlyDictionary symbolToTimeframe)
    {
        string timeframe = symbolToTimeframe.TryGetValue(trade.Symbol, out var tf)
            ? tf
            : "UNKNOWN_TF";

        decimal holdingMinutes = trade.ExitTime.HasValue
            ? (decimal)(trade.ExitTime.Value - trade.EntryTime).TotalMinutes
            : 0m;

        int barsHeld = EstimateBarsHeld(holdingMinutes, timeframe);

        decimal grossPnl = trade.RealizedPnL;
        decimal commission = 0m;
        decimal netPnl = grossPnl - commission;

        decimal? rMoney = null;
        decimal? rMultiple = null;

        if (trade.StopLossAtEntry.HasValue)
        {
            decimal riskPerUnit = Math.Abs(trade.EntryPrice - trade.StopLossAtEntry.Value);
            if (riskPerUnit > 0m)
            {
                rMoney = riskPerUnit * trade.Quantity;
                if (rMoney.Value > 0m)
                    rMultiple = netPnl / rMoney.Value;
            }
        }

        return new TradeIntelligenceRow(
            tradeNumber,
            node.StrategyId,
            node.StrategyName ?? $"S{node.StrategyId:00}",
            trade.Symbol,
            timeframe,
            $"{trade.Symbol}::{timeframe}",
            trade.Side.ToString(),
            trade.TrueOrderType,
            trade.EntryTime,
            trade.EntryPrice,
            trade.ExitTime,
            trade.ExitPrice,
            trade.Quantity,
            trade.IsClosed,
            grossPnl,
            commission,
            netPnl,
            holdingMinutes,
            barsHeld,
            trade.StopLossAtEntry,
            trade.TakeProfitAtEntry,
            trade.ExpectedPrice,
            trade.EntryReason,
            trade.ExitReason ?? "OPEN",
            trade.PlanSource,
            trade.FavorableExcursion * trade.Quantity,
            trade.AdverseExcursion * trade.Quantity,
            rMoney,
            rMultiple);
    }

    private static int EstimateBarsHeld(decimal holdingMinutes, string timeframe)
    {
        int tfMinutes = timeframe.Equals("1d", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase)
            ? 1440
            : timeframe.Equals("4h", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase)
                ? 240
                : timeframe.Equals("1h", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase)
                    ? 60
                    : 0;

        if (tfMinutes <= 0 || holdingMinutes <= 0m)
            return 0;

        return (int)Math.Round(holdingMinutes / tfMinutes, MidpointRounding.AwayFromZero);
    }

    private static decimal ComputeMaxDrawdown(IReadOnlyList> equityPoints)
    {
        if (equityPoints.Count == 0)
            return 0m;

        decimal peak = equityPoints[0].Value;
        decimal maxDrawdown = 0m;

        foreach (var pt in equityPoints)
        {
            if (pt.Value > peak)
                peak = pt.Value;

            decimal currentDrawdown = peak - pt.Value;
            if (currentDrawdown > maxDrawdown)
                maxDrawdown = currentDrawdown;
        }

        return maxDrawdown;
    }

    private static void WriteTxt(
        string path,
        DateTime runUtc,
        string? benchmarkSymbol,
        string? benchmarkTimeframe,
        decimal startEquity,
        decimal endEquity,
        decimal openPnl,
        decimal netPnl,
        decimal grossProfit,
        decimal grossLossAbs,
        decimal commissionPaid,
        decimal totalReturnPct,
        decimal? benchmarkReturn,
        decimal? benchmarkPct,
        decimal? strategyOutperformance,
        decimal profitFactor,
        decimal expectedPayoff,
        int totalTrades,
        int closedTrades,
        int openTrades,
        int winningTrades,
        int losingTrades,
        decimal percentProfitable,
        decimal avgPnl,
        decimal avgWinner,
        decimal avgLoserAbs,
        decimal avgWinLossRatio,
        decimal largestWinner,
        decimal largestLoser,
        decimal largestWinnerPct,
        decimal largestLoserPct,
        decimal avgHoldingMinutes,
        decimal avgBarsHeld,
        decimal avgRMultiple,
        decimal bestRMultiple,
        decimal worstRMultiple,
        decimal avgFavorableExcursion,
        decimal avgAdverseExcursion,
        decimal maxEquityDrawdown,
        decimal maxEquityDrawdownPct,
        decimal portfolioDelta,
        decimal strategySum,
        decimal symbolSum,
        decimal tradeJournalSum,
        IReadOnlyList strategyGroups,
        IReadOnlyList symbolGroups,
        IReadOnlyList trades)
    {
        var sb = new StringBuilder();

        sb.AppendLine("REPORT 33 — TRADE INTELLIGENCE MASTER REPORT");
        sb.AppendLine("============================================");
        sb.AppendLine();

        sb.AppendLine("SECTION A — EXECUTIVE SUMMARY");
        sb.AppendLine("-----------------------------");
        sb.AppendLine($"Run Timestamp (PKT)                : {PakistanTime.FormatLabel(runUtc)}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Run Timestamp (UTC)                : {runUtc:yyyy-MM-dd HH:mm:ss} UTC");
        sb.AppendLine($"Initial Capital                    : {startEquity:F2}");
        sb.AppendLine($"End Equity                         : {endEquity:F2}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Open P&L                           : {openPnl:F2}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Net P&L                            : {netPnl:F2}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Gross Profit                       : {grossProfit:F2}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Gross Loss                         : {grossLossAbs:F2}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Commission Paid                    : {commissionPaid:F2}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Total Return                       : {totalReturnPct:P2}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Profit Factor                      : {(profitFactor == decimal.MaxValue ? "INF" : profitFactor.ToString("F4", CultureInfo.InvariantCulture))}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Expected Payoff                    : {expectedPayoff:F4}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Total Trades                       : {totalTrades}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Closed Trades                      : {closedTrades}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Open Trades                        : {openTrades}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Winning Trades                     : {winningTrades}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Losing Trades                      : {losingTrades}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Percent Profitable                 : {percentProfitable:P2}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Max Equity Drawdown                : {maxEquityDrawdown:F2}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Max Equity Drawdown %              : {maxEquityDrawdownPct:P2}");
        sb.AppendLine();

        sb.AppendLine("SECTION B — ECONOMIC & RISK RECON");
        sb.AppendLine("---------------------------------");
        sb.AppendLine($"Portfolio Delta                    : {portfolioDelta:F2}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Strategy Sum                       : {strategySum:F2}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Symbol Sum                         : {symbolSum:F2}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Trade Journal Sum                  : {tradeJournalSum:F2}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Δ vs Strategy                      : {(portfolioDelta - strategySum):F2}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Δ vs Symbol                        : {(portfolioDelta - symbolSum):F2}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Δ vs Trade Journal                 : {(portfolioDelta - tradeJournalSum):F2}");
        sb.AppendLine();

        sb.AppendLine("SECTION C — TRADE DISTRIBUTION");
        sb.AppendLine("-------------------------------");
        sb.AppendLine($"Avg P&L                            : {avgPnl:F4}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Avg Winning Trade                  : {avgWinner:F4}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Avg Losing Trade                   : {avgLoserAbs:F4}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Ratio Avg Win / Avg Loss           : {(avgWinLossRatio == decimal.MaxValue ? "INF" : avgWinLossRatio.ToString("F4", CultureInfo.InvariantCulture))}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Largest Winning Trade              : {largestWinner:F4}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Largest Winning Trade %            : {largestWinnerPct:P2}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Largest Losing Trade               : {largestLoser:F4}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Largest Losing Trade %             : {largestLoserPct:P2}");
        sb.AppendLine();

        sb.AppendLine("SECTION D — RISK UNIT ANALYSIS");
        sb.AppendLine("------------------------------");
        sb.AppendLine($"Avg R Multiple                     : {avgRMultiple:F4}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Best R Multiple                    : {bestRMultiple:F4}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Worst R Multiple                   : {worstRMultiple:F4}");
        sb.AppendLine();

        sb.AppendLine("SECTION E — EXCURSION ANALYSIS");
        sb.AppendLine("------------------------------");
        sb.AppendLine($"Avg Favorable Excursion            : {avgFavorableExcursion:F4}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Avg Adverse Excursion              : {avgAdverseExcursion:F4}");
        sb.AppendLine();

        sb.AppendLine("SECTION F — TIME-IN-TRADE ANALYSIS");
        sb.AppendLine("----------------------------------");
        sb.AppendLine($"Avg Holding Minutes                : {avgHoldingMinutes:F2}");
        sb.AppendLine($"Avg Bars Held                      : {avgBarsHeld:F2}");
        sb.AppendLine();

        sb.AppendLine("SECTION G — STRATEGY-LEVEL TRADE INTELLIGENCE");
        sb.AppendLine("---------------------------------------------");
        sb.AppendLine("ID   Strategy                              NetPnL      Trades   WinRate    PF         AvgTrade   AvgR      Native%   Fallback%");
        foreach (var row in strategyGroups)
        {
            sb.AppendLine(
                $"S{row.StrategyId:00}  {TrimTo(row.StrategyName, 34),-34}  {row.NetPnl,10:F2}  {row.Trades,6}   {row.WinRate,8:P2}  " +
                $"{(row.ProfitFactor == decimal.MaxValue ? "INF" : row.ProfitFactor.ToString("F2", CultureInfo.InvariantCulture)),8}  {row.AvgTrade,9:F2}  {row.AvgR,8:F2}  {row.StrategyNativePct,8:P2}  {row.EngineFallbackPct,10:P2}");
        }
        sb.AppendLine();

        sb.AppendLine("SECTION H — SYMBOL / TIMEFRAME TRADE INTELLIGENCE");
        sb.AppendLine("-------------------------------------------------");
        sb.AppendLine("MarketKey                     NetPnL      Trades   WinRate    PF         AvgTrade   AvgR      BestStrategy");
        foreach (var row in symbolGroups.Take(20))
        {
            sb.AppendLine(
                $"{TrimTo(row.MarketKey, 28),-28}  {row.NetPnl,10:F2}  {row.Trades,6}   {row.WinRate,8:P2}  " +
                $"{(row.ProfitFactor == decimal.MaxValue ? "INF" : row.ProfitFactor.ToString("F2", CultureInfo.InvariantCulture)),8}  {row.AvgTrade,9:F2}  {row.AvgR,8:F2}  {TrimTo(row.BestStrategy, 20)}");
        }
        sb.AppendLine();

        sb.AppendLine("SECTION N — BENCHMARK COMPARISON");
        sb.AppendLine("--------------------------------");
        if (benchmarkReturn.HasValue && benchmarkPct.HasValue && strategyOutperformance.HasValue)
        {
            sb.AppendLine($"Benchmark                          : {benchmarkSymbol}::{benchmarkTimeframe}");
            sb.AppendLine($"Buy & Hold Return                  : {benchmarkReturn.Value:F4}");
            sb.AppendLine($"Buy & Hold % Gain                  : {benchmarkPct.Value:P2}");
            sb.AppendLine($"Strategy Outperformance            : {strategyOutperformance.Value:P2}");
        }
        else
        {
            sb.AppendLine("Benchmark comparison not available in current runtime snapshot.");
        }
        sb.AppendLine();

        sb.AppendLine("SECTION O — FULL TRADE JOURNAL");
        sb.AppendLine("------------------------------");
        foreach (var row in trades)
        {
            sb.AppendLine($"Trade #{row.TradeNumber:0000}");
            sb.AppendLine($"Strategy                           : S{row.StrategyId:00} {row.StrategyName}");
            sb.AppendLine($"Market                             : {row.MarketKey}");
            sb.AppendLine($"Side                               : {row.Side}");
            sb.AppendLine($"Order Type                         : {row.OrderType}");
            sb.AppendLine($"Entry Time (PKT)                   : {PakistanTime.FormatLabel(row.EntryTimeUtc)}");
            sb.AppendLine($"Entry Time (UTC)                   : {row.EntryTimeUtc:yyyy-MM-dd HH:mm:ss} UTC");
            sb.AppendLine($"Entry Price                        : {row.EntryPrice:F8}");
            sb.AppendLine($"Exit Time (PKT)                    : {(row.ExitTimeUtc.HasValue ? PakistanTime.FormatLabel(row.ExitTimeUtc.Value) : "OPEN")}");
            sb.AppendLine($"Exit Time (UTC)                    : {(row.ExitTimeUtc.HasValue ? row.ExitTimeUtc.Value.ToString("yyyy-MM-dd HH:mm:ss", CultureInfo.InvariantCulture) + " UTC" : "OPEN")}");
            sb.AppendLine($"Exit Price                         : {(row.ExitPrice.HasValue ? row.ExitPrice.Value.ToString("F8", CultureInfo.InvariantCulture) : "OPEN")}");
            sb.AppendLine($"Quantity                           : {row.Quantity:F8}");
            sb.AppendLine($"Closed                             : {(row.IsClosed ? "YES" : "NO")}");
            sb.AppendLine($"Gross P&L                          : {row.GrossPnl:F8}");
            sb.AppendLine($"Commission                         : {row.Commission:F8}");
            sb.AppendLine($"Net P&L                            : {row.NetPnl:F8}");
            sb.AppendLine($"Holding Minutes                    : {row.HoldingMinutes:F2}");
            sb.AppendLine($"Bars Held                          : {row.BarsHeld}");
            sb.AppendLine($"Stop Loss At Entry                 : {(row.StopLossAtEntry.HasValue ? row.StopLossAtEntry.Value.ToString("F8", CultureInfo.InvariantCulture) : "NULL")}");
            sb.AppendLine($"Take Profit At Entry               : {(row.TakeProfitAtEntry.HasValue ? row.TakeProfitAtEntry.Value.ToString("F8", CultureInfo.InvariantCulture) : "NULL")}");
            sb.AppendLine($"Expected Price                     : {(row.ExpectedPrice.HasValue ? row.ExpectedPrice.Value.ToString("F8", CultureInfo.InvariantCulture) : "NULL")}");
            sb.AppendLine($"Entry Reason                       : {row.EntryReason}");
            sb.AppendLine($"Exit Reason                        : {row.ExitReason}");
            sb.AppendLine($"Plan Source                        : {row.PlanSource}");
            sb.AppendLine($"R Money                            : {(row.RMoney.HasValue ? row.RMoney.Value.ToString("F8", CultureInfo.InvariantCulture) : "NULL")}");
            sb.AppendLine($"R Multiple                         : {(row.RMultiple.HasValue ? row.RMultiple.Value.ToString("F4", CultureInfo.InvariantCulture) : "NULL")}");
            sb.AppendLine($"Favorable Excursion                : {row.FavorableExcursion:F8}");
            sb.AppendLine($"Adverse Excursion                  : {row.AdverseExcursion:F8}");
            sb.AppendLine();
        }

        File.WriteAllText(path, sb.ToString());
    }

    private static void WriteCsv(
        string path,
        IReadOnlyList trades)
    {
        using var writer = new StreamWriter(path, false, Encoding.UTF8);

        writer.WriteLine(
            "TradeNumber,StrategyId,StrategyName,Symbol,Timeframe,Side,OrderType,EntryTimePkt,EntryTimeUtc,EntryPrice,ExitTimePkt,ExitTimeUtc,ExitPrice,Quantity,IsClosed,GrossPnl,Commission,NetPnl,HoldingMinutes,BarsHeld,StopLossAtEntry,TakeProfitAtEntry,ExpectedPrice,EntryReason,ExitReason,PlanSource,RMoney,RMultiple,FavorableExcursion,AdverseExcursion");

        foreach (var row in trades)
        {
            writer.WriteLine(string.Join(",",
                Csv(row.TradeNumber.ToString(CultureInfo.InvariantCulture)),
                Csv(row.StrategyId.ToString(CultureInfo.InvariantCulture)),
                Csv(row.StrategyName),
                Csv(row.Symbol),
                Csv(row.Timeframe),
                Csv(row.Side),
                Csv(row.OrderType),
                Csv(PakistanTime.FormatLabel(row.EntryTimeUtc)),
                Csv($"{row.EntryTimeUtc:yyyy-MM-dd HH:mm:ss} UTC"),
                Csv(row.EntryPrice.ToString("F8", CultureInfo.InvariantCulture)),
                Csv(row.ExitTimeUtc.HasValue ? PakistanTime.FormatLabel(row.ExitTimeUtc.Value) : "OPEN"),
                Csv(row.ExitTimeUtc.HasValue ? $"{row.ExitTimeUtc.Value:yyyy-MM-dd HH:mm:ss} UTC" : "OPEN"),
                Csv(row.ExitPrice.HasValue ? row.ExitPrice.Value.ToString("F8", CultureInfo.InvariantCulture) : "OPEN"),
                Csv(row.Quantity.ToString("F8", CultureInfo.InvariantCulture)),
                Csv(row.IsClosed ? "YES" : "NO"),
                Csv(row.GrossPnl.ToString("F8", CultureInfo.InvariantCulture)),
                Csv(row.Commission.ToString("F8", CultureInfo.InvariantCulture)),
                Csv(row.NetPnl.ToString("F8", CultureInfo.InvariantCulture)),
                Csv(row.HoldingMinutes.ToString("F2", CultureInfo.InvariantCulture)),
                Csv(row.BarsHeld.ToString(CultureInfo.InvariantCulture)),
                Csv(row.StopLossAtEntry.HasValue ? row.StopLossAtEntry.Value.ToString("F8", CultureInfo.InvariantCulture) : "NULL"),
                Csv(row.TakeProfitAtEntry.HasValue ? row.TakeProfitAtEntry.Value.ToString("F8", CultureInfo.InvariantCulture) : "NULL"),
                Csv(row.ExpectedPrice.HasValue ? row.ExpectedPrice.Value.ToString("F8", CultureInfo.InvariantCulture) : "NULL"),
                Csv(row.EntryReason),
                Csv(row.ExitReason),
                Csv(row.PlanSource),
                Csv(row.RMoney.HasValue ? row.RMoney.Value.ToString("F8", CultureInfo.InvariantCulture) : "NULL"),
                Csv(row.RMultiple.HasValue ? row.RMultiple.Value.ToString("F4", CultureInfo.InvariantCulture) : "NULL"),
                Csv(row.FavorableExcursion.ToString("F8", CultureInfo.InvariantCulture)),
                Csv(row.AdverseExcursion.ToString("F8", CultureInfo.InvariantCulture))));
        }
    }

    private static string Csv(string value)
    {
        string safe = value ?? string.Empty;
        safe = safe.Replace("\"", "\"\"");
        return $"\"{safe}\"";
    }

    private static string TrimTo(string? text, int maxLen)
    {
        string value = text ?? string.Empty;
        if (value.Length <= maxLen)
            return value;

        if (maxLen <= 3)
            return value[..maxLen];

        return value[..(maxLen - 3)] + "...";
    }

    private sealed record TradeIntelligenceRow(
        int TradeNumber,
        int StrategyId,
        string StrategyName,
        string Symbol,
        string Timeframe,
        string MarketKey,
        string Side,
        string OrderType,
        DateTime EntryTimeUtc,
        decimal EntryPrice,
        DateTime? ExitTimeUtc,
        decimal? ExitPrice,
        decimal Quantity,
        bool IsClosed,
        decimal GrossPnl,
        decimal Commission,
        decimal NetPnl,
        decimal HoldingMinutes,
        int BarsHeld,
        decimal? StopLossAtEntry,
        decimal? TakeProfitAtEntry,
        decimal? ExpectedPrice,
        string EntryReason,
        string ExitReason,
        string PlanSource,
        decimal FavorableExcursion,
        decimal AdverseExcursion,
        decimal? RMoney,
        decimal? RMultiple);

    private sealed record StrategySummaryRow(
        int StrategyId,
        string StrategyName,
        decimal NetPnl,
        int Trades,
        decimal WinRate,
        decimal ProfitFactor,
        decimal AvgTrade,
        decimal AvgR,
        string BestSymbol,
        string WorstSymbol,
        decimal StrategyNativePct,
        decimal EngineFallbackPct);

    private sealed record SymbolSummaryRow(
        string MarketKey,
        decimal NetPnl,
        int Trades,
        decimal WinRate,
        decimal ProfitFactor,
        decimal AvgTrade,
        decimal AvgR,
        string BestStrategy,
        string WorstStrategy);
}
